# Preface

Presented herewith is the first-ever English version of the full text of the translation of Maharshi Parasara's Hora-sastra. But for the blessings of Ganesa, this would have been an uphill task as the god of astrology, Sri Maha Vishnu, is Parasara.

The work is in the form of a carritch between Parasara and his disciple Maitreya who belonged to Vasishta's lineage. Parasara was the preceptor of the earliest sages in the field of astrology. Saunaka was one of the disciples.

This date can be understood to roughly be the era of Dharma Raja, born in the present Yuga. The sage states that Salivahana, with the combination of... He further states the reader could find statements relating to Prajapati, Swayambhu Manu, etc., which could possibly be made by no ordinary mortal.

Statements could be attributed to Mihira in Brihat Samhita, Kalyana Varma in Saravali, and many such other illustrious authors. The astrological statements of Parasara's Hora find their translation in Malayalam, Bengali, and partly in Hindi. I have rendered the following translations with me.

For a majority of slokas, one can find common Sanskrit versions.



After scrutinizing critically the manuscripts, for reasons of more credibility, I have chosen the Sanskrit version rendered by Sitaram Jha. The Chaukambha version of Khelari Lal's is almost the same as the other versions that I have come across:

1. Tamil translation by C. G. Rajan - for only 36 chapters, without Sanskrit verses.
2. English translation by N. N..K. Rao - for only 25 chapters, without Sanskrit slokas.

Thus, I have felt a need to make the original version in English available to the fullest extent. Our version has 97 chapters containing English translation and annotations and examples. To handle the publication easily, we have divided the work in two volumes. The first volume contains 45 chapters while the remaining 52 chapters have been put in the second volume.

Chapter 1 and chapter 2 give some preliminary extra-astrological information. From chapter 3, the astrological information begins. In this chapter, the astrological benefics and malefics, planetary descriptions, primordial deities, complexions, compounds, seasons, relationships, dignities, etc. are given. Methods of calculating the upagrahas like Muburta and velas like Gulika are given. These are totally ten Grabas and have their own say on a nativity, as the other nine Lain alter in suitable proportions and Muhurta velas can affect the effects due to Nava graha.



# In the matter of calculation of Gullka

A different concept comes to light from this oldest work. The later authors have given altogether variable advice in knowing Gulika's position whereas Perasara advised that it should be cast for the beginning of Saturn's Muhurta. Whereas some suggest that it should be for the ending of Saturn.

# Rasi

In chapter 4, Slokas 25-30 are the climax of this chapter. An unerring method to find out the Nisheka Lagna (or the moment causing conception) is outlined. Though the process of calculation is as simple as a school student's mathematical quiz, it has truth in it which modern science could not discover. To prove the truth of the statement in sago's instruction, a practical example has been given by me.

An assumed problem cannot better solve the case where the time of coitus is astrologically chosen. The time of birth has also been accurately noted. From the time of birth, the time (or coitus) is traced which is not in variation, even the slightest extent, with the originally noted Nisheka time.

Again, the birth time is traced in a forward manner from the time of Nisheka, in traditional rules of astrology. This proves using only three important points:

1. The point of M.C. is to be found out in the metal houses accordingly. This is popularly intersected and originally advocated by Parasara.
2. Gulika's position should be found for the beginning of Saturn's Muhurta only.
3. Lahiri's Ayanamsa is the best. The reader will find that we have used Moon's exact longitude in the above process. Simple angular distance by any Ayanamsa will not alter the solution, but a slight change in position will take us far away from the truth. With Lahiri's Ayanamsa, we can safely work out even Nadiamsas, which change.


# Chapter 5

The method given by astrologers can help to foretell the exact moment of birth from the time of coition. The query has to be very well timed to reveal that time.

Reseaches of Nisheka touch on various special Lagna, Hora Lagna, and Bhava. The importance of these cannot be underestimated. A final Bhava chart can only emerge after merging different charts. This final Bhava chart can be considered exclusively on the natal ascendant.

Whereas sometimes the bhava chart can mislead, this is what the sage emphasises in sloka 9.

The zodiac is divided into sixteen Vargas. How to use these Vargas is fully explained. These Vargas are from Rasi down to Shashtiamsa. In the classification, 10 Vargas are made in four groups, i.e., 6 Vargas, and 16 Vargas and special technical names have been given for easy identification.

For example, if a planet is in 15 good Vargas, it indicates that out of 16 Vargas, it is in kamsa, gradation of Raja Yogas.

Each Varga finds a specific position. For example, without tangible results due to the native's parents' positions, these planets are of supreme importance.

In this very chapter, the sage enunciates what is called Vimsopaka points of strength. He assigns a maximum of 20 points differently taking again four classifications, viz. Shadvarga, Sapta Varga, Dasa Varga, and Shodasa Varga.

The consideration is whether a planet is in its own sign, friendly sign, or enemy's sign and the like in concern. Then an evaluation is done to reveal the extent of auspicious effects that enables us to decide the strength of a planet in a dasa.



# Chapter 8

What is called Jaimini deals with aspects Rasi basis. Maharshi Jaimini was the sage who expanded Parasari principles very extensively on these aspects for easy memorization and successful applicability. The original concept is however from Parasara.

# Childhood

Evils discussed are in chapter 9 while chapter 10 prescribes possible planetary combinations to combat such evils.

Basic information about the 12 houses could be found in chapter 11 while specific attention may be given to slokas 14-16. These 3 slokas serve an important role in knowing how a Bhava is going to give effects under various circumstances.

# Chapters 12-23

Give a variety of information and instructions in analysing the 12 houses of a horoscope in a systematic manner. A close study of these rules will tame one's mind to approach the horoscope scientifically for fruitful results.

# Chapter 24

The chapter is again one of the most important chapters. Here, various effects of a lord being in a specific Bhava are fully covered. How to sort out a situation in case of contrary indications is given out in slokas 145-148.

The bhava effects of Dhooma, Vyatipata, Gulika, etc., are fully narrated in chapter 25. Pranapada reveals special effects as could be seen in this chapter.

# Ishta Phalas

Shadbala and Kashta related calculations, and other mathematical aspects are elaborately laid down in the 3 chapters, 26, 27 and 28.

It is not in order if planets are studied with reference to natal chart. Padas for various houses will further alter the planetary effects. This is what is taught in chapter 29.

# Raja Yogas

Are best analysed through Arudha chart or Pada chart. The sage suggests Graha Padas as well, but unfortunately he leaves it at that without much adding information.

For still deeper research, Upapada will be more effective. This will give more clues about marriage, finance, and diseases.

# Chapter 31

Entitled 'Argaladhyaya', though worthy brief information on planetary interventions, has effects and obstructions thereof.






# Chapter 32

Significance is the Rasi occupied by Atma Karakamsa forming a certain relationship with Karaka. Planets and their effects are narrated in chapter 33. This is one of the most instructive. Planets again assume a certain tendency by virtue of owning certain roles for various ascendants.

# Chapter 34

The sage elaborately touches on such principles. He decides for each of the 12 ascendants. Marakas and Karakas give us understanding whether planets will yield beneficial results or adverse effects. This will enable us to guess the period of one's death, allow for the Yogas which lists Nabhasa.

Many new Raja Yogas could be found in chapter 36, like Khadga, Mridanga, etc. Kahala yogas with Lunar and Solar are dealt in chapters 37 and 38. Raja yogas in chapter 39 are popularly known. Yogas for financial combinations are in chapter 40, and royal association special mention, containing a variety of authoritative information on finances, say the planets have a bearing on death.

These are tersely dealt with in the 42nd chapter. The chapter on longevity, Amsayu, and Naisargayu, is among the most important ones. Pindayu pairs on ascendant/planetary signs contain common computations based on linking with movable, fixed, and taken aspects.

I have worked out a full-fledged example touching all aspects for deductions by placement in bhavas 12. I have considered contributions to the various bhava positions for longevity. I have simply not given one common formula covering the six planetary positions but degree-wise deductions.

This can be usefully extended to any loss of years as far as the reader can work out the exact loss.

# DIET BRIHAT PARASARA, HORA SASTRA

Postrate the lotus-feet of Lord Vighneswara, before the offspring of Uma, the cause of destruction, the great ganas (the elements of the universe) who is served by Bhuta and consumes the fruits of the essence of Kapiththa and Jambu.

# Chapter I

# The Creation

Offering folded hands, I said, "O Venerable Maitreya, Astrology has three divisions, the supreme limb of the Yedas, to all-knowing sage Prasara."






# Brihat porasara Hora Sastra

Ganita and Samhita. Among the said genethliac three divisions, Hora or part of astrology is still more excellent. I desire to know of its glorious aspects from this Universe. Be pleased to tell me, "How is created? How does the relationship of the animals born on it end? What is the relationship of the heavenly bodies with this earth? Please speak."

Notes: Maitreya was elaborately Parasara's ardent disciple. Parasara was the illustrious father of Bhagawan Veda Vyasa. Parasara Smriti, Pergssn Sambita present parasert Horl are some of the immortal contributions made by our sage. Parasara's preceptor was Saunaka, the reputed sage of Rigveda Pratisakhya and other Vedic compositions, from whom he took instructions in astrology. Saunaka was taught by Narada, son of Lord Brahma Pitamaha in the matter of astrology and others. Narada got direct instructions from the present Pitamaha.

These details are stated by sage Parasara in the concluding chapter of the present work. The sage, in the course of his treatise, states that Salivahana will be born in the yogas caused by the relationship between lord a trinat lor as both an uigular and are in Simhasgntmstrvide ch. 41 sloka 32. While the technicalities of the astrological part of this statement will be understood by the reader as he progresses with the study of this work, it will be evident that much before Salivahana. The Parasara in it D 72. Since the era of Salivahana commenced, Veda Vyasa is reverentially referred to as Parasaratmdja, the offspring of Parasara, who lived during the Bhanta era.

Sage Maitreya's name appears in Veda Vyasa's Srimad Bhagavata Purana. Maitreya was Kusaru's offspring. Sage Maitreya achieved a great deal of knowledge in spiritual and other topics. Vidura abandoned his kith and kin and met sage Maitreya to achieve religious merits.

As can be seen, our sage text is in the form of a dialogue between Parasara and Maitreya, the Master and the Disciple respectively. Astrology has three divisions, viz. Hora, Ganita and Samhita. Hora deals with the genethliac part while mathematical aspects like planetary movements, strengths etc. are taught by the Ganita branch. Samhita means a collection or compendium.

Brihat Parasara Hora Sastra

9-12. Sri Vishnu who is the lord (of all matters), undefiled who has spirit, is endowed with the three Gunas. He transcends the grip of (i.e. Gunatita), who is the Author of this Universe, who is glorious, who is the Cause, who is endowed with valour has no beginning. He authored the Universe and administers it with a quarter of his power. The other three quarters of Him, filled with nectar, are known only to the philosophers as the perceptible (of maturity). The principal Evolysl who is both imperceptible and perceptible is Vasu Dwa. The Imperceptible part of the Lord is endowed with powers while the Perceptible has dual powers with triple.

13-15. The three powers are: Sri (Mother Sattwa Guna, Mother Sakti Lakshmi) with Bhoo Sakti (Earth) with Rajoguna Neela, Sdtcri with Tamoguna. Apart from the three, the kind of Vishnu, influenced by Sri Sakti and Bhoa Sakti, assumes the form of Sankarshana with Rajogwa and of Anirudha with Satwa Guna, of Guna.

16-17. Mahattatwa, Ahamkera and Ahamkara Murthi, Brahma, are born from Samkarshana, Pradyumna respectively. All these three forms and Anirudha are endowed with all the gunas, predominance of the Guna due to their origin.






# Chapter

Ahamkara is of three classes, i.e. with Satwik, Rajasik and Tanasik dispositions. Divine class, and the five primordial compounds (ar, sensory respectively from the said three Ahamkaros.

Lord Vishnu coupled with Sri Sakti rules over the worlds. Coupled with Bhu sakti, He is Brahma, causing the Universe. Coupled with Neela sakti, He is Shiva, destroying the Universe.

The Lord is in all beings and the entire Universe contains Him. All beings have predominance of the former while some have the latter in predominance. Some have predominance in the Grah^r viz. Sun etc. and powers or consorts Brahma, Shiva and others. Their too have predominance paramatmonso. Others have more of Jeevatmamsa.






# Chapter 1: Incarnations

# The Lord

1. Maitreya: "The incarnations of Sri Krishna, Sri Rama, etc. are endowed with Jeevamsa."

2. Parasara: "O Brahmin, the four incarnations, viz. Rama, Krishna, Narasimha and Varaha are wholly with Jeevamsa. The other incarnations (ten) have too."

The lord has many incarnations. He is Unborn.

3-4. The living beings on the planets (Grahas) are due to their Karmas. He bestows the results to Janardana. He assumed the form to destroy the demons and sustain the auspicious divine forces.





Chapter 2
# 5-7 From the Sun

God the incarnation of Rama, Moon that of Krishna. from Mars that of Narasimha, from Mercury that of Budhdha, from Jupiter that of Vamana, Venus that of Parasu Rama, from Saturn that of Koorma (Tortoise), from Rahu that of Varaha (pig) of Meena (Fish) occurred. All other incarnations also are through the Grahas.

The beings with more are called divine beings.

Jeevatmamsa (mortal) beings. The high degree of paramatmamsa are from the Sun, etc., did incarnate as Rama, Krishna, etc. After completing the mission, the Parantatmamsas (in the "respective") merge in the Grahas. The Jeevatma portions from the Grahas take births as human beings according to their Karmas and again live their lives. And at the time of Great Destruction, they merge in the Grahas.

One who knows of all these, will become versed in the knowledge of past, present and future. Without a knowledge of astrology, these cannot be known. Hence every.





Srihat Parasara Sastra

One should have a knowledge of Astrology particularly the Brahmin. One who, devoid of astrological knowledge, blames this science will be reborn to the hell called 'Raurava' and will be blind.

# Chapter 3

# Planetary Characters

Maitreya: Sage, have you affectionately explained the dispositions. Now kindly detail about their characters.

Perasara: "O Brahmin, listen to the account of the heavenly bodies. Out of the many luminous bodies in the skies, some are stars; some are planets (or Grahas). Those that have no movements are the Nakshatras. Notes: Placed in the firmaments are many stars which we have, for astrological purposes, among 27 stars and planets. Rahu and Ketu though recognised as planets are shadowy. These two are nodes of the Moons."

# Chapter 21

given be taken planets a time positions for

8-9. The durations of the planets per Drikganiia. And with the help of Rasi places, at birth should be known. Now I tell you about the castes' descriptions of the dispositions of Planets.

10. NAMES OF PLANETS. The names of the nine planets are: the Sun, Moon, Mars, Mercury, Jupiter, Venus, Saturn, Rahu, and Ketu.

Notes: In the Sanskrit literature of astrology, see ch. 2 of my English translation for additional information in this regard.

11. BENEFICS AND MALEFICS. Among these, the Sun, Moon, Mars, Rahu and Ketu (the ascending and descending nodes of the Moon) are malefics and decreasing Mercury, however, is a malefic while the rest are benefics.

Notes: That decreasing Moon is conveyed as a malefic and a benefic respectively. Some commentators hold the following view: the Moon is a malefic of the Sun but within 120°, she is very auspicious, she has medium strength. Between 120° to 240° she is bereft of strength. This is Yavanas' view, vide P. 70 of my English translation or otherwise, while waning Moon (Krishna Paksha or dark half Moon) is a malefic and waxing Moon (Sukla Paksha or bright half Moon) is a benefic.

Should the Moon be conjunct a benefic, she turns benefic, even if in a waning state.






# 28

# Parasara Brihat Hora Sastra

As regards Mercury, we have clear instructions that he becomes a malefic if he joins a malefic. If the Moon and Mercury join, refer to the benefics:


 the sun is happiness. Venus governs grief.

Notes: The degree of benefic effects mentioned of the indications above will be commensurate with the planet concerned. If the Sun is strong, one will have a matured soul and will make abundant spiritual knowledge and happiness will be perpetually acquired. Grief will not be there, if Saturn is under the strength.

# PLANETARY CABINET

Sun and the Moon while apparent are the royal status. Mars is the army chief. Mercury is the ministerial planet. Jupiter and Venus are servants. Rahu and Ketu form the army.

# Chapter 3

# 1617. PLANETARY COMPLEXIONS

The Sun is blood-red. The Moon is tawny. Mars is blood-ied who is not tall. Mercury's hue is akin to that of green grass. Tawny, variegated and dark are Jupiter, Venus and Saturn in their order.

# 18. PLANETARY DEITIES

Fire (Agni), Water (Varuna), Maha Siva's son following Ganesa, Vishnu, Indra, Sachi (the consort of Lord Indra) and Devi are the presiding deities of the 7 planets in their order.

Notes: The deities or Adhidovatas of the planets given above may be invoked to get the respective planets' afflictions cured. For example, evils indicated by Mercury can be brought under control by offering prayers to Sri Vishnu Bhagawan.

The names of the planetary deities loyed by Varaha Mihira in selecting a name for the child are additionally emp- consonants and vowels under. The names are attributed to the seven planets as follows:



The name of the child can be selected with an initial letter stronger based on the natal ascendant and Navamsa lord. For example, if the ascendant lord is Mars, the name can be Kumara (gqn) or Guha (gq). Deductions can be suitably made in other cases.

# Chapter 3

Alternatively, Lord Ganesa representing Ketu may also be pleased suitably.

19. SEX OF THE PLANETS .

Mercury and Saturn are neuters. The Moon and Venus are females while the Sun, Mars and Jupiter are males.

20. PRIMORDIAL COMPOUNDS ..

The Pancha Bhootas, viz. fire, earth, water and air are respectively governed by Mars, Mercury, Jupiter, Venus and Saturn.

21. PLANETARY CASTES .

Jupiter and Venus are Brahmins. The Sun is a royal planet while the Moon and Mercury belong to commercial community. Saturn rules the Sudras (4th caste).

22. The planets are classified as follows: Satwik planets are the luminaries, Rajasik planets include Mercury, while Mars, Jupiter, Venus and Saturn are Tamasik planets.

Notes: The Satwa, Rajas and Tamasik natures of planets will have a say on the disposition of the native. For further information, see my notes, lrde P. 51 of Seravali.

23. DESCRIPTION OF THE SUN ..

The Sun's eyes are honey-coloured. He has a square body. He is of clean habits, intelligent and has limited hair on his head.






# Brihaf parasara Hora Sastra

# Notes

Much additional details could be gathered from my notes in ch. 4 of saravari and ch. 2 of Horasrra. The native will be influenced in appearance, disposition etc. by the strongest planet or the ascendant lord or the Navamsa lord.

# 24. DESCRIPTION OF THE MOON

The Moon is windy and phlegmatic. She is learned and has a round body. She looks sweet and has fickle-minded, lustful speech.

# 25. DESCRIPTION OF MARS

Mars has blood-red eyes, is fickle-minded, liberal, given to anger and has a thin physique. He has a thin waist.

# 26. DESCRIPTION OF MERCURY

Mercury is endowed with an attractive physique and capacity with many meanings. He is fond of jokes. He has a mix of all the three humours.

# 27. DESCRIPTION OF JUPITER

Jupiter has a big tawny body, tawny hair and eyes, is phlegmatic, intelligent and learned in all sastras.

# 28. DESCRIPTION OF VENUS

Venus is charming, has a splendorous physique, is excellent or great in disposition, has charming eyes, is a poet, is phlegmatic and windy and has curly hair.






# Chapter 3

Notes: The word in the text has purports happy, virtuous, charming etc. Since Venus is a charming planet, the meaning has been used. However, I do not imply that Venus is not a virtuous planet etc.

# 29. DESCRIPTION OF SATURN

Saturn has a long physique, an emaciated appearance, and has tawny eyes, big teeth, is windy in temperament, is indolent and lame and has coarse hair.

# 30. DESCRIPTION OF RAHU AND KETU

Rahu has a smoky appearance with a blue-mix physique. He is horrible. He resides in forests and is windy in temperament. Ketu is intelligent and akin to Rahu.

# 31. PRIMARY INGREDIENTS (SAPTA DHATUS):

Blood, marrow, skin, fat, semen, bones, and muscles are respectively denoted by the planets from the Sun etc.

Notes: The Sun and others up to Saturn rule the Sapta Dhatus ingredients of the body, as indicated above. Their strength or weakness indicates safety or otherwise to the Dhatu concerned. For example, if the Sun is afflicted at birth, the native is liable to suffer disorders of bones, breakage of bones, and the like. The native will incur disorders of blood if the Moon is ill-disposed. Similarly, aspects of the Dhatus may be considered.

# 32. PLANETARY ABODES

Temple, watery place, fire, filthy ground, sport-ground, bed-room, treasure-house, and these seven are respectively the abodes for the planets from the Sun onward.





Brihat Parasara Hora Sastra

Notes: The abodes particularly denoted have varied in astrology. If, for example, Mercury is related to the recovery of a lost article, it will be near it in the bed-room, a sport-ground. If it is Venus, and so on and so forth.

# 33. PLANETARY PERIODS

Ayana, Muhurtha, a day (consisting of day and night), Ritu, month, and fortnight. These periods are the durations allotted to the planets from the Sun to Saturn.

Notes: The cited can be related to the maturity of an event, particularly in horary astrology and in Dasa judgements. Should the Sun, for example, be related to the fruition of an event, it will be in about six months. Ayana is the time taken by the Sun to complete one course—northern or southern in the zodiac. This is about six months. The Moon indicates 48 minutes. Ritu is Muhurtha, which is equal to approximately two months or the time required for the Sun's transit of two Rasis.

The period indicated by Rahu is 8 months and Ketu 3 months (vide sloka 46 of this ch.). Also see sloka 18, ch. 4 of Saravali which states further use of these indications.

# 34. A PLANETARY

Every bitter, pungent, saline, mixed, sweet, acidulous and astringent respectively are tastes lorded by the Sun.

Notes: The strongest planet will give the native a penchant for the particular taste ruled by it. Alternatively, one may denote a taste related to the 2nd lord. The strongest one prevails.






# PLANETARY STRENGTHS

are Mercury and Jupiter. The sun and Mars are strong in the east while Saturn is the only planet that derives strength in the south. The Moon and Venus are endowed with vigour when north. Again, strong during night are the Moon, Mars and Mercury while Jupiter, the Sun and Venus are strong during day (i.e. night). The rest are strong only in day time. Malefics acquire strength in the bright half of the month. Malefics and benefics are respectively strong in Dakshinayana and Uttarayana. The month, day and Hora (planetary hour) are stronger than the other in ascending order. Again stronger than the other in the ascending order are: Saturn, Mars, Mercury, Jupiter, the Moon and the Sun.

Notes: Indicated in the first instance strengths are directional or digbala. The following are the directions related to a horoscope.

| East  | ascendant  |
| ----- | ---------- |
| North | 4th house  |
| West  | 7th house  |
| South | 10th house |

These are to be reckoned only from the ascendant and not from the Moon. Jupiter and Mercury have Digbala in the ascendant. The Sun and Mars acquire this strength in the 10th house; Saturn does so in the 7th. The 4th gives directional strength to the Moon and Venus. The planet gets no Digbala if it is in the opposite sign with reference to its Digbala house. For example, Saturn has no Digbala if he rises.

The use of Digbala is: all

Related trees: The Sun rules strong trees (i.e. stout with trunks). Saturn useless trees, (like yielding rubber plants), the Moon (like bitter plants), Venus fruitless ones, Jupiter fruitful ones and Mercury floral ones.

# DHATU, MOOLA AND JEEVA DIVISIONS

while the Sun, the Moon and planets like Mars, Rahu, Jupiter, Saturn and Ketu rule Jeevas. Moola planets are Mercury, Dhatu (metals), and Moola (roots, vegetables, etc.) have great use in astrology, particularly horary astrology.

Query: If Rahu is in the ascendant for example, relates to a metal. For a fuller appreciation, see Prabhu Deeprka Bhuvlna.

# SATURN

Out of all the planets, Saturn is the eldest and bestows the highest number of years in Naisargika Dasa.

# EXALTATION AND DEBILITATION

For the seven planets from the sun, the signs of exaltation are respectively: Aries, Taurus, Cancer, Virgo, Libra, Capricorn, and Pisces.





# Chapter 3

The deepest exaltation degrees are respectively 10, 3, 28, 15, 27, 20 in those signs. And in the seventh sign from the exaltation sign, each planet has its own debilitation. The same degrees of deep exaltation apply to deep fall.

Notes: Each planet assumes significance in a certain sign. In the opposite sign therefrom, it is debilitated. Even in the sign of the debilitation sign, it is very highly or highly detrimental as the case may be, in a certain degree.

For example, the Sun is exalted in Aries and is the most powerful on the 10th degree therein. In Libra, he gets debilitated and if he is in the 10th degree of Libra, he is worst affected. Suitable deductions can be made for other planets.

As for the exaltations and debilitation of the nodes, there are different views. Please see page 20 of my English translation of Horasara for necessary information.

# ADDITIONAL DIGNITIES

In Leo, the first 20 degrees are the Sun's Moolatrikona while the rest is his own. The first 12 degrees in Aries are Moolatrikona with the rest simply becoming his own house. For Mercury, the first 15 degrees in Virgo are the exaltation zone, the next 5 degrees are Moolatrikona and the last 10 degrees are his own house. The first 30 degrees of Sagittarius is the Moolatrikona of Jupiter while the remaining part thereof is his own house. Venus divides Libra into two halves keeping the first as Moolatrikona and the second as his own house. Saturn's arrangements are the same in Aquarius as the Sun has in Leo.



Brihat Parasara Sastra
# Hora

NATURAL RELATIONSHIPS. Note the signs and Moolatrikona are 4th, 2nd, 12th, 5th, 9th from the planets. The 8th from the sign is its enemy.

The ruling planet of a kona is a planet. The lord of its exaltation is a friend to such other than its sign. Lords are these friends.

lf a planet becomes equal, it is neutral. Given this sloka is a simple formula to compute planetary relationships. From Moolatrikona, the lords are its friends.

The 2nd, 4th, 5th, 8th, 9th lords are friendly. The rest 3rd, 6th, 7th, 10th and 11th from Moolatrikona sign's lord is its enemies. The exaltation lord is always the 10th from Moolatrikona.

If friendship prevails, however, enmity or neutrality occur simultaneously but equality is none for example in the case of Mars. The Moolatrikona from there is Aries. The 11th lord is Saturn hence a friend, he is as well as is lord of Mars. Since we get enmity on one count and equal on the other, Saturn becomes equal to Mars.

Take the friendship of Venus. He owns the 2nd from Mars, thus becoming a friend and enemy to Mars. Hence respectively.

# See the table below for an easy grasp of relationship:

| Planet  | Friends       | Enemies | Equals  |
| ------- | ------------- | ------- | ------- |
| Sun     | Moon, Jupiter | Saturn  | Mercury |
| Moon    | Sun           | Jupiter | Saturn  |
| Mars    | Sun           | Moon    | Jupiter |
| Mercury | Venus         | Saturn  | Mercury |
| Jupiter | Moon, Mars    | Saturn  | Venus   |
| Venus   | Mercury       | Sun     | Mars    |
| Saturn  | Moon, Mars    | Jupiter | Venus   |





# Chapter 3

The Moon does not consider anyone as her enemy. The following statement from Parasara (Benares edition by Chaukamba) further has an identical meaning: "The Sun and Mercury are Moon's friends while others are her neutrals." Saravali view.

As for Rahu and Ketu, the following may be of additional rest.

| Rahu | The Sun, Moon and Mars are his enemies | Jupiter, Venus and Saturn are his friends | Mercury is his neutral  |
| ---- | -------------------------------------- | ----------------------------------------- | ----------------------- |
| Ketu | The luminaries                         | Mercury and Jupiter are his friends       | Saturn are his neutrals |

# RELATIONSHIPS

# TEMPORARY (HOROSCOPIC)

6. The planet posited in the 4th, 11th, 3rd, 2nd or the 12th, otherwise, enmity is mutual. There is a given friend. (This applies to a horoscope).

Notes: The hints in sloka 55 are to understand the constant relationship among planets. In the sloka we are advised based on a certain relationship of planets having given positions, i.e. if two are mutually cordial in 4th and 12th, they become friends, and in 11th or in 2nd and 10th, or in 3rd they may be otherwise, they should be temporary enmity. This rule is very simple and needs no explanation.

# COMPOUND RELATIONSHIP

Should two planets be naturally friendly and temporarily friendly, they become extremely friendly. Friendship on one count and neutrality on another count make them friendly.




Brihat pitrasara Hora Sastra

# 42

Combined with affinity on the other turns into equality. Enmity and neutralship cause only enmity. Should there be extreme enmity in both manners, an astrologer should consider these and declare horoscopic effects accordingly.

Notes: The final relationship, as a result of natural dispositions, is called S-fold relationship, or cSqT. The same is shown below in a Speculum of Compound Relationships:

| One relationship | Another relationship | Net relationship   |
| ---------------- | -------------------- | ------------------ |
| Friendship       | Friendship           | Extreme Friendship |
| Neutrality       | Friendship           | Friendship         |
| Enmity           | Enmity               | Extreme Enmity     |
| Neutrality       | Enmity               | Enmity             |
| Enmity           | Friendship           | Neutral            |

It is understood that if there is friendship, then neutrality will also prevail with enmity.

RATIO OF EFFECTS: Planet A in exaltation fully good gives effects while in Mooratrikona it is bereft of its auspicious effects by one fourth. It is half benefic in its own house. Its beneficence is in one-fourth in a friendly sign. In an equal sign, one eighth of auspicious effects is useful. The good effects are nil in debilitation. Inauspicious effects are quite the reverse with reference to what is stated.

# 65. EFFECTS OF SUB-PLANETS

If one of these affects the Sun, the native's longevity will be short while the ascendant and the Moon respectively will affect wisdom.

Notes: If the Sun is afflicted by one of these Upagrahas, the native's dynasty will not continue, there will be loss of all sons or lack of sons. If the ascendant is afflicted, life will come to pass short.

The conjunction of an Upagraha is treated as 'affliction' for the Sun. We better treat it except can join any of the five Vyatipata from the example.

# Brihat Parasara Hora Sastra

# 46

| Indrachapa   | Sagittarius | Gemini      | Cancer  |
| ------------ | ----------- | ----------- | ------- |
| Upaketu      | Aquarius    | Leo         | Cancer  |
| Gulika       |             | Aquarius    |         |
| Yamaghantaka |             |             | -       |
| Ardhapiahara |             | Sagittarius |         |
| Kala         |             |             | u       |
| Mrityu       |             | C           | Scorpio |

From the Sun to Saturn, no one is exalted in the mentioned exaltation signs, nor debilitated in the above mentioned debilitation signs.

Out of the 5 Kalavelas, viz. Gulika etc. four except Kala (related to the Sun) have own sign system in the respective ruled signs by their fathers. Gulika, son of Saturn, has Aquarius house. Jupiter's son, Yamaghantaka, has it in Sagittarius. Ardhaprahara, Mrityu, son of Mercury's son, is in own sign if in Gemini. Mars has Scorpio as own house. It is why Kala, a son of the Sun shifted to Capricorn, a sign (Saturn) of his brother leaving his father's Leo. Obviously, Saturn has given his Moolatrikona to his son Gulika while he gave a secondary sign to his brother Kala.

# 70. GULIKA'S POSITION

The degree ascending time (as at the above) will be given the longitude of Gulika at a place. Based on this longitude effects particular only, Gulika's for a nativity be estimated.

Notes: The day duration or night duration as may be the case for calculation the five Kalavelas, viz. Gulika etc. be considered for the latitude of birth. Some authorities suggest to use the period end of the for ascertaining longitudes of these. Sage Parasara's view is correct in this respect, as exemplified in the notes for slokas 25-30, ch. 4 infra. and interchanged in our own text mean one and the same.

# Chapter 4

# Zodiacal signs Described

IMPORTANCE OF HORA.. The word Hora derived from Ahoratra after dropping the last syllables. Thus Hora (ascendants) remains (i.e. in between day and night) and after knowing Hora, the good and bad effects of a native be known. sri Vishnu, personified. Inviiible, Time His limbs are the 12 Rasis from Aries.

# NAMES OF THE ZODIAC

The 12 signs of the zodiac in order: Aries, Taurus, Gemini, Cancer, Leo, Virgo, Libra, Scorpio, Sagittarius, Capricorn, Aquarius, and Pisces.

# LIMBS OF KALAPURUSHA

The personified time has limbs as under with reference to the 12 signs: Head, face, arms, heart, stomach, hip, space below privities, navel, thighs, knees, ankles and feet. The limbs of Kalapurusha are divided treating Aries as ascendant. For an individual, the ascending sign will denote head, 2nd sign face and so on and forth. See the diagram given below in the case of a native, Scorpio for an easy grasp.

The limbs related to malefics will suffer defects and the ones related to benefics will be beautiful while the ones related to adversities are immune to danger. These are stloola (broad) and sookshma (minute) of limbs, the 36 deca-scheme are resorted to.

5-51. CLASSIFICATION OF 'S/GIL'S Movable, Fixed

These signs are given the 12 dual. The names to known malefic and benefic, successively. Similarly, Aries, Leo and Sagittarius are male and female. Taurus, Virgo and Capricorn are bilious. Gemini, Libra and Aquarius are windy. The rest are phlegmatic while mixed are dual. Movable are Aries, Cancer, Leo, Scorpio and Capricorn. The signs are dual or common: Gemini, Virgo, Sagittarius and Pisces.

# 9-9I. GEMINI DESCRIBED

The Gemini represents a male and female holding hands. It is airy and is a biped. Its head is in the west and lives in villages. It is windy in nights and has strong temperament. It has a green body with Mercury.

# 10-11. CANCER DESCRIBED

Cancer represents a strong sign related to forests and resorts. It is a centipede and has many feet. It is bulky in disposition and ruled by the Moon. It rises back in watery nights.

# 12. LEO DESCRIBED

Leo is a quadruped and a royal sign. It resorts to forests and is strong in the day. It has a large white body with its head and rises in the east.

# |3. |4. VIRGO DESCRIBED

This sign is a hill resort and is strong in the day-time. It rises with its head and has a medium build. It resides in the south and is a biped. It relates to business and has grains in its hands. It belongs to fire and is variegated. It relates to hurricanes.

Similarly, 30 degrees make 1,0E,000 seconds duration at birth in our example of arc. The night is 12h 50m 48s as of 17.21984 the sunrise is at 6h 59m 58s and Sunset New Delhi. Now see the process as under:

| 108000              | (30 seconds deg.)    | 46248 seconds (or 12h 50m 48s) - |
| ------------------- | -------------------- | -------------------------------- |
| 37237" 10' 20' 37"' | loror\*3223?)/108000 | : 15945.711 seconds              |

So say, 4h 26m have from the Sunset, i.e. 18h 9m 10s. This denotes from 22h 34m 55s which should be birth time. And we have the birth time recorded as 22h 35m. This cannot be a coincidence or manipulation for a serious student of astrology like me, but a meaningful process and scientific.

When the Adhana Moon's Dwadammsa is known correctly, the natal Moon can be checked. She, at birth, should be in the Dwadasamsa as she was at Adhana. Please note this agreeability - Adhana Moon as well as natal Moon in Capricorn being similarity. Hence our natal Moon is just another verification factor, which however need not exist if the Moon's Dwadasama distance is whatever coincides, the angular prevail between the Adhana Moon and Adhana Lagna will be between the natal Moon and ascendant.

In our example, the difference between the Adhana Moon and Adhana is 48° 44' whereas a natal Moon and ascendant 49° 6' apart.






# Chapter O

The curious reader may note one thing. There are many rules to the birth month, natal Moon, natal ascendant with the help of (or prasna). And the correct ones bringing various possibilities to a coincidental manner should be correctly judged without rushing to conclusions theoretically. Thus the reader will be convinced time noted is correct as we got to the back birth details Adhana and vice versa accurately without any ambiguity whatsoever.

From the said processes based on accurately maintained records for purposes of scientific research, I, rather we, firmly conclude the following without a shadow of doubt:

1. Gulika's longitude will correspond to the beginning of Saturn's Muhurta only, as suggested by other authority stating that it should be for the end of Muhurta ruled by Saturn. In fact, I have not come across any work stating contrarily to what Parasara stated in this regard. Suppose we calculated Gulika for the given birth chart for the end of Saturn's muhurta, the longitude of Gulika would still be 24 degrees advanced. That would put Gulika 24 days behind the noted date. Please note that we have reached exactly the Adhana date as the record maintained without any variation. This proves that Gulika should be at the beginning of Saturn's Muhurta.
2. Ayanamsa is only that of Lahiri and that accurate is as we have made use of the Moon's longitude. This contention is proved by the fact that we used the process of getting back to Adhana simply. Other longitudes in the angular distances are used by us. But the Moon's Ayanamsa longitude will vary plus or minus according to the variation. Whereas the position of the Moon, we did not experience any anomaly with Lahiri's computation. Similarly in progressing from the Adhana date towards the birth date, the Moon's longitude played a significant role. If for example, the Moon goes with another Ayanamsa position, the natal position in the Adhana will be inconsistent with Adhana. Hence Lahiri Ayanamsa has all the perfection required for calculation of even the Nadiamsas.






# Chapter 5

# Ascendants

Special ascendants of the Brahmins, excellent viz. Bhava I explain below again special ascendants, Lagna, Hora and Ghatika.

From the time of birth to the time of birth in ghatis (or 120 minutes) constitute one Bhava lagna. Every 5 minutes (in ghatis, etc.)

Divide the quotient by 5 and add the Sun's longitude at Sunrise. This is called Lagna.

Notes: To work out the various ascendants, assume that the birth is at 12gh 30vi and the Sun's longitude at the time of birth is 4s 12'. Find out the Bhava in the instance, as under:

| When birth time is divided by 5 | Sun's longitude as | which is | to get   | 27' as Lagna. |
| ------------------------------- | ------------------ | -------- | -------- | ------------- |
| 132"                            | 207"               | Bhava    | or Libra |               |

# 5

HORA LAGNA.. Again from Sun-rise of birth, Hora Lagna repeats itself every ghatis (24 minutes). Divide the time past upto birth from the Sunrise and add the quotient etc. in signs, degrees and so on to the longitude of the Sun at the Sunrise. This will yield Hora Lagna in Rasi, degrees etc.

Notes: Let us find out the Hora Lagna for the same example. Birth time is to be divided by 2.5. When done so, we get 5 signs or 150 degrees. Add this to the Sun's longitude as (i.e. at sunrise plus 132 + 150 = 282). We get thus Hora Lagna Capricorn as 12°.

# 6-8. GHATT LAGNA (GHATIKA LAGNA)..

Now listen to the method of working out Ghatika Lagna. This Lagna changes the birth time in Ghati and vighatis. Consider the number of ghatis past as number of Rasis or Ghatika Lagnas. The Vighatis be divided by 2 to arrive at degrees in the said Ghatika lagna. The product so arrived in Rasis, and minutes be added to the Sun's longitude as Sunrise to get the exact location of Ghatika Lagna.

Notes: Let us find out the Ghatika lagna in the above example case, Birth time is 12 ghatis which gives 12 Rasis. Vighatis are left 30 which are to be divided by 2 and treated as degrees. Divided by 2 yields 15, i.e. 15°. Thus, we note 12 signs.

# 9. USE OF SPECIAL

Keeping the various planets at birth as done for the natal ascendant to analyse special ascendant. This is a very important clue given by the sage.

Notes longitudes viz ascendants, We get the of the three special Apart from the Lagna, Hora Lagna Ghatika Bhava the planets will remain in different bhavas being considered. # Chapter 65

VARNADA DASA: I now derail just by knowing which, one can deal with the longevity of native. If the natal ascendant is an odd sign count directly from Aries to natal ascendant. If the natal ascendant is an even sign, count from Pisces to the natal ascendant, in the reverse order. Similarly, if the Hora Lagna is an odd one, count from Aries to Hora Lagna in direct order. If the Hora Lagna is an even one, count from Pisces to Hora Lagna in the reverse order. If both products are odd or even signs, then add both figures. If one is odd and the other is even, then know the difference between the two products. If the latest in this process is an odd one, count so many signs from Aries in direct order; if an even one, count so many signs from Pisces in reverse order. The sign known will be the Varnada for the ascendant.

Take the case of a native who has a natal ascendant as Libra (odd sign) and Hora Lagna as Scorpio (even sign). When we count from Aries to Libra (odd sign - hence direct), we get ?. Again from Pisces (Hora Lagna - reverse), we have to Scorpio lagna, and we have 5 signs. We have to add these two figures, which are of the same class, i.e. odd. We get a product of even one. Hence, we have to count 12 signs in a reverse manner to get Varnada for the Rasi of natal ascendant. Thus we get Aries. This is a suggestion that the counting when done from Aries, be taken into consideration. In that case, counting is done from zero degree. And from Pisces, it is from the last degree of Pisces, i.e. the 30th point.






# 66 Brihat Parasara Sastra

Now listen to the natal and Hora effects of the above. Out of the two, viz. Lagna, there is a clock. If the natal ascendant is stronger, from whichever Varnada starts, the counting of Dasas is an old sign, equal to years dasa will be anti-clockwise. Otherwise, the number of signs intervening between the natal ascendant and Varnada, similarly for other houses.

# 15. EFFECTS

Should by a trine from the ascendant's occupied Varnada be treated. The Varnada is capable of causing evils, the above mentioned planets as the Rudra planet in Rasi. Just the dasa of the said planets is considered.

# 16-20.

The native will live only up to the longevity of elder brothers, the 11th from Varnada will denote the longevity of younger brothers and sisters, the 3rd longevity of mother, the 4th longevity of the 5th, the longevity of sons, sisters, and the 9th longevity of the future. The dasa of the soola Rasi will inflict greater evils. The Rudra planet is the one which has more strength.

Notes: The lords of 2nd and 8th are considered when.

# Parasara Erihat Hora Sastra

O sage, I have known you from about the descriptions of the planets, and their divisions. I desire to know the details of various signs, which please narrate.

# 2-4. NAMES OF THE 16 VARGAS

Lord Brahma has described 16 kinds of Vargas (Divisions) for each sign. Listen to those. The same are: Rasi, Hora, Drekkana, Dvadasamsa, Navamsa, Shodasamsa, Sapthamamsa, Chaturvimsamsa, Trimsamsa, Vinsamsa, Sapthavimsamsa, Akshavedamsa, Khavcdamsa.

# 5.6. RASI AND HORA

The Rasi is called by sign (one half of an old ris sign). The first half is the Hora ruled by the Sun while the second is called the Hora of the Moon. This is true in the case of Rasi counted from 24. These are totally (at the rate of 12) the whole of the zodiac.

# Notes

The names of the planets lording over the 12 signs have been given earlier. The following table throws light on the Horas (15° of each) of the 12 signs.

# SAPTHAMAMSA

The Sapthamamsa from the same sign commences counting of a Rasi.

It is from the seventh division of the seven signs that the names are considered.

The names of an odd sign are Dadhi, Ghritha, Ikshu^Rasa, Ksheera, etc. These designations are reversed for even signs.

Each sign is made in 7 equal parts. As far as the Saptamamsas are concerned, the counting is in the successive manner.

Example for Aries: the sign is made for Taurus, while Gemini, etc., see the table given below.




# 12. NI,YAMSA : The Navamsa

The Navamsa calculation for a movable sign are from there itself, for a fixed sign from the 9th thereof for a dual sign from the 5th thereof. They by designations (divine), Manushya (human) and Rakshasa in a successive and repetitive order for a movable sign. Rakshasa and Deva are the order for a fixed sign while Rakshasa, Manushya and Deva are a dual sign's order.

Note: Navamsa is 1/9th part of a sign or J. 20,. The Navamsas in order commence from the same sign for a movable from the 9th for fixed sign. For example the Navamsas themselves; from Capricorn for of Aries are counted from Aries, Taurus and from Libra for Gemini. These are fully shown in the table below:

# SIDDHAMSA

The Siddhamsa distribution commences for an odd sign respectively from Leo and Cancer. In the case of an even sign, the ruling deities repeat twice in the order of Skanda, Parsudhara, Anala, Viswakarma, Bhaga, Maya, Vrisha-dhwaja, Govinda, Madana and Mitra, Antaka, Bhima. Reverse these to know the deities for the Siddhamsa in an even sign.

# Brihat Parasura Hora Sastra

TRIMSAMSA: The Trimsamsa lords for an odd sign are Mars, Mercury and Venus. Each of them rules over 5, 5, 8, 7 degrees, respectively. The deities in the Trimsamsas are Indra, Kubera, Agni, Vayu, and Varuna. In the case of an even sign, the planetary lordship and deities get reversed.

Notes: For Trimsamsa see Speculum of Trimsamsas.

| Signs    |             | Signs    |           |
| -------- | ----------- | -------- | --------- |
| First 5° | Aries       | First 5° | Taurus    |
| Next 5°  | Aquarius    | Next 5°  | Virgo     |
| Next 8°  | Sagittarius | Next 8°  | Pisces    |
| Next 7°  | Gemini      | Next 5°  | Capricorn |
| Next 5°  | Libra       | Next 5°  | Scorpio   |

CHATI/ARIMSAMSA: For odd signs count from Aries and for an even sign (each part of a sign) from Libra in respect of 45' of arc. The deities are Vishnu, Marichi, Chandra, Tvashta, Dhata, Siva, Ravi, Yama, Yaksha, Harva, Kala and Varuna, repeating successively presiding in the same order for all signs.

Notes: Chatvarimsamsa is a fortieth part of a sign or 45' of arc. These are successively distributed from Aries in case of any odd sign, and from Libra in case of any even sign. See the table noted below.

SHASHTIAMSA (ll60th part a of sign or half-a-degree

To calculate Shashtiamsa the position of a planet and take the degrees etc. it traversed in that sign. Multiply that figure by 2 and divide the degrees by 12. Add to the remainder which will indicate the sign in which the Shashtiamsa lord falls. The names of Shashtiamsas are:

1. Ghora
2. Rakshasa
3. Deva
4. Kubera
5. Yaksha
6. Kinnara
7. Bhrashta
8. Kulaghna
9. Garala
10. Vahni
11. Maya
12. Purishaka
13. Apampathi
14. Kala
15. Sarpa
16. Amrita
17. Indu
18. Marutwan
19. Mridu
20. Kornala
21. Heramba
22. Brahma
23. Vishnu
24. wara
25. Deva
26. Ardrc
27. Kalinasa
28. Mahes
29. Kamalakara
30. Gulika
31. Mrithyu
32. Kshiteesa
33. Davagni
34. Kaala
35. Ghora
36. Yama
37. Kantaka
38. Amrita
39. Sudha
40. Poornachandra
41. Vishadagdha
42. Vamsakshaya
43. Utpata
44. Kaala
45. Kulanasa
46. Komala
47. Seetala
48. Karala
49. Saumya
50. Damshtra
51. mukhi
52. Praveena
53. Kalapavaka
54. Chandra
55. Saumya
56. Dandayudha
57. Nirmala
58. Kroora
59. Atiseetala
60. Amrita (Indurekha)
61. Payodhi
62. Bhramana
63. order
64. Chandrarekha

The method of calculating the Shashtiamsa (or 1/60th of a sign or 30' of arc) is advised in sloka 33 above. Assume that Venus is placed in Capricorn 13" 25'. To find out the Shashtiamsa lord, ignore the position and multiply the degrees and minutes by 2. Hence the degrees (ignoring 25' i.e. 26 13" x2:26" minutes) be divided by 12. The remainder is 2 which should be increased:

1. Thus we count 3 signs from Capricorn. The resulting Shashtiamsa is Pisces whose lord is Jupiter.

'These positions can also be marked in a zodiacal diagram for an easy grasp of the order of Shashtiamsas along with the meanings of

# 42-53. yARGA CLASSIFICATION

Maitreya, now are explained the sum effects of classifications of different (or Varps so far narrated). These are four kinds, divisions (6 viz. Shad Varga divisions (7 considered), Saptha Yarga divisions (10 yarga Dasa Varga divisions considered) (all the l6 divisions and Shodasa considered).

In the Shadvarga classification, the Varga designations are Kimsuka, Vyanjana, Chatra and Kundala according to a planet Chaamara, being combinations good in 2 to 6 Vargas. Next is the Sapt avarga which these classifications continue in the same manner combinations good upto six the 7th additional getting classified Varga as Mukutir- In Dasa the Varga scheme, the commence designations from Parijata etc. such as gooti 2 Vargas-parijatha.

In these the divisions falling in the planet's exaltation Moolatrikona sign, own sign, and the signs owned of an angle by the loid from the Arudha ascendant (as are all to be considered good Vargas). The divisions of a combust planet, pllyrt, planet defeated weak and a planet in bad Avasthas like Sayana all ignored to be auspicious, for these destroy the good.

Notes: Four kinds of summary of the Vargas are suggested or diyisions thus:





# Chapter 6

(a) Shadvarga (considering Vargas) six vi;. Rasi, Navarnsa Hora, Decanate, Dvadasamsa and Trimsamsa.

(b) Snpta (soven Varga Vargas) addir;i: Saptamamsa Shad to the Varga.

(c) Dasa (ten Varga Vargas) adding Shodasamsa, Shashtiamsa Dasama and divisions to the Sapta Varga.

(d) Shodasa (all the 16 Vargas so far narrated by the s.rge). The groups as per above are as slokas 17.20.

The Vargas to be considered are:

1. Exaltation
2. Moolatrikona divisions.
3. Own divisions.
4. The divisions of the owners of the four angles from the Arudha Pada counted or Pada Lagna.

The first three are clear. The fourth one needs clarification. The word (Sx'anullnrh) has been used which means from the Arudha Pada. Hence the last of sloka 52 hints at the divisions of the lord.s of angles the Arudha (Similarly from Pada) means the Navamsa occupied by Atma Karaka i.e. Kara ascendant, ch. kamsa 33, infra.

The sage suggests that the signs owned by the lords of Arudha and its angles are considered good for Varga Division. This will bring many signs--sometimes as many in the purview of this rule. It has been felt necessary this approach to bring liberal contained in the sloka to the attention of the reader. In my opinion, the truer strength of a planet lies in its Moolatrikona, exaltation and own positions.

For the sake of brevity, the good Vargas of Shadvarga in number in the context through Shodasa Varga given detailed are special designations below:

If Shadvarga scheme is considered two or more good Vargas are known thus:

1. Kimsuka
2. Vyanjana
3. Chamara
4. Chatra
5. Kundala.

If Sapta Varga scheme is used the same names apply upto six good Vargas while seven good Vargas go under the name Mukuta.




# Brihat Parasara Hora Sastra

If Dasa Varga scheme is resorted to, the Vargas are called thus:

1. Parijata
2. Uttama
3. Gopura
4. Simhasana
5. Devaloka
6. Brahmaloka
7. Sakravahana
8.
9.
10.

The author of Sarvartabha Chintamani designates respectively 8, 9 and 10 as Amara, Iravata and Vaiseshikamsas. These three are popularly known with these names rather than with the ones given by Maharshi.

When Shodasa Varga scheme is wholly considered, the number of divisions are known as:

1. Bhedaka
2. Kusuma
3. Nagapushpa
4. Kanduka
5. Kerala
6. Kalpavriksha
7. Chandanavana
8. Ichchaisrava
9. Poornachandra
10.
11. Dharmvantari
12. Suryakanta
13.
14. Sakrasirnhasana
15. Vidruma
16.
17. Goloka
18. Sri Vallabha

It may be noted that most of even the hoary authors have not gone beyond Dasa Varga scheme. The sage has fully explained all 16 Vargas involved so that an actual disposition is properly known.

As far as Hora or half of a sign is concerned, Vargas should be flexibly used as except the Sun and Moon, none has rulership of Hora. Jupiter in Moon's Hora is exaltation if in Sun's Hora, and for Jupiter in Sun's Hora, and four in Hora, for other any how do we classify the Varga?

In my opinion, we have to follow the hint given in sloka 13 of the next chapter that Jupiter, Sun and Mars give effects as if in Sun's Hora as concerned and the rest except Mercury in Moon's Hora. Mercury is in both the Horas. So to these good Horas are for the planets that Jupiter and Mercury are good in any Hora for Varga classification.

There are further hints about Hora, vide sloka 13 onwards.

Nextly, a brief clarification is required that Sun and Moon not having their own Trimsamsas. Sun can occupy in Trimsamsas the Moon can be in Aries and can be in Taurus. They cannot be in Leo or Cancer Trimsamsa. Exaltation will apply to them in Trimsamsa.

Now, coming to the Varga, we will take some for clarifications. The word "Suryakantamsa" denotes

Notes: The method of calculating Vimsopakastrengthis instructs present strength. The sage given in slokas 17-21 of the chapter will be suggestive. Other sources related to assess strength are suggested to a planet's proper disposition.

Brihat Parasara

towards debilitation, transitting degree its and by degree, the planet becomes fully void in the strength when from fall to sign. Again it climbs exaltation, gains potential in exaltation. It is stated also that planets get full strength in their own signs. Planets in male signs are noted. Here a distinction is made. Male planets get full strength. Mars and others in female signs have a male planet in each sign. Mars, for example, is better placed in Scorpio, while Venus is better in Libra. Such inference may be elaborately discussed in the details of Shadbala calculation etc. The chapters of the matter are wisely made.

HORA, DECANATE AND TRIMSAMSA EFFECTS.

Mars gives effects and do so in the hora of the Sun. The Moon, Venus, and Saturn when in Moon's hora will be powerful even in an odd sign. The Sun's hora will be Full, while the effects in the beginning and nil will be the medium applications made at the end of a hora. Similar effects will be for middle etc. As for Turyamsa, Navamsa, and Trimsamsa decanate, the Moon is akin to Venus. The Sun is akin to Mars and applicable to Rasi to Trimsamsa. The three planets male in Sun's Hora will be revealing while Venus and Saturn are good in Moon's Hora.





# Chapter 7

Here Sun's Hora of odd signs and Moon's Hora in even signs given are powerful that Sun, Mars, Jupiter highly in the first half of an odd sign and Venus Saturn are very revealing. Mercury is powerful in the second sign whether an odd or otherwise. The due Hora will be derived fully if the planet is in the first one-third of the Hora. The effects will be nil according to the placements being in the second medium or third part of the Hora.

# VIMSOPAKA (six divisions)

STRENGTH. The Shadvargas consist of Rasi, decanate, Hora, Navamsa, and Dvadasa msa. The full strength, respectively for each of the divisions are 6, 2, 4, 5, 2, 1. This is the Vimsopaka strength relating to Shadvarga msa. Adding the Sapthama to the Shad Vargas, we get Sapta strength which is: 5, 2, 3, 2t, 4, 12, and 2, 1. These gross strengths are while subtle ones should be understood by exact positions.

# Notes:

Vimsopaka strength is the 20 strength obtained by a planet continuously occupying its own Vargas in the various schemes like Shad Varga to Shodasa Varga. For fuller appreciation, see the notes under slokas 26-27 of the current chapter.

20. Add Dasamsa, Shodasamsa and Shastiamsa to the Saptha Varga Divisions, to get to the said scheme of Dasa Varga.

# Division

The figure against each individual is called "Swaviswa". For example, in Rasi Division under Shodasa you find 3.5 which is the Swaviswa.

Varga, shown as in the total strength is the Viswa.

Yarga placement in own house, extreme the various dignities like in friend's horse etc.

If a planet is continuously in own Vargas of Shad Vutp scheme or any other, it gets all the 20 points of strength. This is not possible. By virtue of a placement in Sambandha Panchadha, the points diminish. In this context, from slokas learnt by us, the relationship is to be considered.

In the above table, SV: Swavisva; vV: Varga Viswa VS: Vimsopaka strength. The rest of the points will be clear to the reader from the calculations. And the Vimsopaka strengths accordingly be estimated.

Maharshi Parasara fixes broad guidelines to know the use of this strength as under:

- 5 points - Inauspicious (or neutralisation of good results)
- 5-10 points - good effects
- 10-15 points - Some effects
- 15-20 points - Mediocre effects
- 20 points - Wholly favourable effects

In our example, Venus gets 16.8 points and hence he should confer wholly favourable effects when considered. I would, however, prefer the use of all the 16 Vargao for a truer picture.

# Chapter 7

# 30.32. DASA EFFECTS VITH STRENGTH

Maitreya, after assessing the vimsopaka strength through the various divisions, the rising and setting planets considered. The Vimsopaka strength is classified as Poorna, Atipoorna, Madhya, Atimadhya, Swalpa, Atibeena, and Atiswarpa. Thus should be classified the vimsopaka strength and the period Dasa results declared accordingly.

Notes: The sage uses 8 distinct terms to classify the effects of vimsopaka strength. I have used the same original terms for the sake of identity while the table below with percentages will enlighten the students to what these terms imply.

| Grade     | Vimsopaka points | Beneficial effects |
| --------- | ---------------- | ------------------ |
| Atipoorna | 17.5 to 20.0     | w\.s-rw%           |
| Poorna    | 15.0 to 17.5     | 75.0-87.5%         |
| Atimadhya | 12.5 to 15.0     | 62.5-75.0%         |
| Madhya    | 10.0 to 12.5     | 50.0-62.5%         |
| Swalpa    | 7.5 to 10.0      | 37.5-50.0%         |
| Atiswalpa | 5.0 to 7.5       | 25.0-37.5%         |
| Heena     | 2.5 to 5.0       | 12.5-25.0%         |
| Atiheena  | 0 to 2.5         | 0-12.5%            |

The percentages given by me are numerical assignments for a comparative study so that an idea is gained originally or the gradations suggested.

# Chapter Of The Signs

Aspects

Every movable sign aspects to the fixed adjacent sign. The 3 fixed signs leaving the movable sign lends the aspect. A common sign aspects the same. The planet in a sign (in which the planet is) does not lend aspects to the other three common signs. The aspect of planets, Maharshi Notes: Apart from usual aspects, these are also aspects with Rasi.

Parasara by Jaimini (a disciple of Vedavyasa and author of Poorva Mimamsa) is known as the original propounder of this system. The Jaimini system though.






# 106

Brihst Parasara liora Sostta

Jaimini Maharshi also astrology. He is an equally worshipped authority on.

Mainly uses Rasi aspects, Rasi Dasas apart from other Dasas, Arudha Pada, Atrna Karaka etc. by longitudes, Karakamsa etc.

The current 3 slokas throw light on the sign aspects.

Each of the 3 fixed signs, leaving the nearest movable sign. For example, Leo, Aries-movable sign-does not aspect Taurus but Scorpio and Aquarius, Taurus-a fixed sign aspects movable signs, 3 movable viz. Cancer, Libra and Capricorn Aries, but does not aspect the nearest movable sign. Gemini's planet aspects are similar signs and Pisces. The in 4th sign aspects as above and also in these aspects, the occupant thereof. Hence, are ignorable. Longitudes of the aspector and the aspected.

# 6-9. ASPECT{AL DIAGRAM

As depicted by Lord Brahma, now narrate the aspectual diagram so that aspects are easily understood by a mere sight of the diagram. Draw a square or a circle marking the 8 directions (4 corners and 4 quarters thereof). Mark the zodiacal signs as under: Aries in the east, Gemini in the north-east, Cancer in the north, Virgo in the north-west, and Leo in the west, Libra and Scorpio in the south-west, Capricorn in the south, and Aquarius in the south-east. (as the earlier slokas)

The aspects per can be shown in a square diagram (as or circular diagram per convenience).






# Chapter 9

# Evils At Birth

O Brahmin, first of all, estimate the evils factors thereof through the ascendant and checking effects and then declare the evils of the 12 bhavas.

Notes: The ascendant is the most important in the matter of causing evils or counteracting evils. The sage refers to the ascendant Balarishta or infant mortality specifically in the context that up to the age of 24, no definite assurances can be made about longevity.

The Moon becomes important in the matter of checking evils and factors for longevity from the age of 32. And the sun is the centre up to the year of 32. This does not mean that the evils from the Moon do not exist till the 32nd year of age, and so on and so forth.

Evils causing premature end exist up to the 24th year of one's age. As such, no definite calculation of life can be made till such year of age.

Notes: While the sage declares that up to the 24th year, it will not be possible to declare definitively, other works like Horasrra, Jyotisharnava (version), Sarvartha Chinramani, Navaneethamu, Shluel, Jathaka, and Ptalr Deepiks etc. say that longevity calculations will be possible till the 12th year of age.






# Brlhat Parasara

# Hora Sastra

3-6. SHORT-LIFE COMBINATIONS (upto sloka 23):

Should the Moon be in the 6th, 8th, or the 12th from the ascendant and be in aspect to a malefic, the child will die soon. If in the 6th, 8th or the 12th there be benefic's aspect, it may live upto 8.

If a benefic is retrograde in the 6th, 8th or the 12th being in aspect to a malefic, this is true only when the ascendant is unoccupied by benefic. Should the ascendant be occupied by Saturn, jointly, (early) 5th by Mars and the Sun, death of mother and brother will come to pass.

Mars placed in the ascendant or in the 8th and be conjunct Saturn or be in aspect to a malefic, the Sun or malefic being bereft of benefic aspect will prove a source of immediate death.

Here a pertinent query may emerge as to why the combinations mentions premature death while longevity cannot be decidedly declared upto the 24th year of age as per sage statement. These yogas will guide us to detect his own defects for longevity and resort to remedial measures, immediate prayers, donations, medicine etc. like fire sacrifice, to save the from Akala Mrityu, an evil house vide ch. 5 of Horasara.

The Moon in aspect at birth to a malefic will cause early death. Even a benefic's aspect on the Moon, in the said Yoga, will not cause the end at the age of 8, suggests the sage. If she is increasing, this need be feared.






# Chapter 11

As the ascendant will live only for a fortnight. Immediate death will occur if Saturn is in the 10th, Mars in the 7th. One will immediately go to the abode of Yama (the god of death) if the Moon is in the ascendant while Saturn is in the 8th and the 3rd. Moon and Jupiter are in their order of life who has Sun in the 11th. All planets in the 12th will be a source of short life, specifically Venus and Rahu. But the aspect of the luminaries, four planets (on the 12th) will counteract such evils.

Notes: One of the 4 planets among the Moon, Rahu, and Venus will contribute to premature death if in the 12th. The evils of one of these is aspect (This proves that aspects are checked.)

However, the 12th for Libra ascendant will confer a life span of early end if she is causing unrelated malefic with a benefic.

12. The Moon will come to pass if there is a birth in the morning or evening or in a hora ruled by the Moon.

13. Early death will come to junctions.

In each of the three yogas, prerequisite is that the ascendant be captured by Moon malefics.

The last Navamsas of Cancer, and of Scorpio of Pisces are called Gandanta. According to a host of authors, the Moon will cause premature death,

14. DEFINITION OF SANDHYA: 3 Ghatikas before the sight of the Sun's disc (half of the semi) as morning twilight following the Sun set are called evening twilight, respectively.

Notes: Morning twilight (or Pretah Sandhyr) lasts for 22 minutes in the morning before the sight of the Sun's disc and for a similar duration in the evening twilight.

This is deciding the sage for evils of longevity. Sandhya is defined differently in context with a purpose, vide ch.46 of Yol' II.

EARLY DEATH: Should malefics in the occidental half, early death are in the oriental half while benefics will follow. In this case, there is no need of any rethinking.

Notes: The area of one born in Scorpio horoscope via the 7th house (or the 10th cusp) is known as occidental (or eastern) half while the rest is oriental (or western) half.






Chapter 9

One born in Scorpio ascendant and with malefics in the occidental half will face immediate death. This yoga is called as Vajra as quoted by Kalyana Varma.

The Moon should be in the Occidental half if it is a benefic or be in the oriental half if it is a malefic. If Mercury remains by a malefic, this yoga will not come to pass.

# Chapter 10

# Antidotes For Evils




# Chapter 19

Those are the evils due to native. I now narrate the antidotes for such evils to assess the extent of inauspiciousness.

Notes: The antidotes mentioned in the context may carry with them the concept of short life. While some yogas are fortunate, every principle does not.

1. Should an angle from the ascendant eliminate all evils, Jupiter as the Sun, Mercury, and Venus will be in darkness.

2. Just a single reverential obeisance to Lord Siva frees one from all sins, but strong Jupiter in the ascendant will ward off all the evils.

In the case of Capricorn ascendant, Jupiter should be exceedingly strong by other virtues, as otherwise, it can lead to short life. For, sage Bhrigu specifically hints at the medium of life with Jupiter in the ascendant, debilitation, or inimical sign with malefic sign.

3. The lord is singly capable of counteracting all evils if he is strongly placed in an angle as Lord Siva, the holder of Bow, destroyed by Maya for the three cities of demons.

4. All evils are destroyed if a benefic aspects the ascendant born during night in the bright half. Similarly, on the aspect of the ascendant of one born during the day in the dark half.

# Chapter II

# Judgement of Houses



# Chapter II

1. O sage, have you come to know of the evils and antidotes thereof? Please tell me, what is to be deduced from each house.

# 2. INDICATIONS OF THE FIRST HOUSE

(The sage replies): Physique, appearance, intellect (the organ of intelligence, i.e. brain), complexion of the body, vigour, grief and happiness, innate nature are all to be guessed through the ascending sign.

Notes: We are tersely told here of the prime indications to be deduced from each house. There are many matters related to each house which have been listed rather exhaustively in my English translation of Horasaro. See pp. 183-187 ibid.

# 3. SECOND HOUSE

Wealth, (food, precious metals, stones, etc.), family, enemies, etc. are to be understood through the 2nd house.

# 4. THIRD HOUSE

From the 3rd house, (attendants, brothers, sisters, etc.), know of the following: labour, servants, journey, and parent's death.

# 5. FOURTH HOUSE

Conveyances, happiness, relatives, mother, treasure, lands and houses are to be consulted through the 4th house.




# 5. FIFTH HOUSE

The learned should deduce from the 5th house amulets, sacred spells, learning, royalty (or authority), fall of position etc.

# 6. SIXTH HOUSE

Maternal step mother etc. are to be estimated from the 6th house. Doubts about death, ulcers, enemies.

# 7. SEVENTH HOUSE

Wife, travel, trade, loss of sight, death etc. are known from the 7th house.

# 8. EIGHTH HOUSE

The 8th house indicates battle, wealth of the enemies, longevity, death and things that have happened to the future births.

# 9. NINTH HOUSE

Fortunes, brother, religion, shrines, visits to brother's wife, known from the 9th house.

# 10. TENTH HOUSE

(Authority), Royalty, place, living (livelihood), honour, father, in foreign lands and debts are to be understood from the 10th house.

Notes: "Father" is to be studied through the above sloka. The sage obviously refers to the 10th house in this context as the 7th is the 4th. Western astrology too follows this view.






# Chapter

Here we need some elaboration. The status of the father, family consisting of the native's mother etc., will be known through the 10th house. The father as an individual and his well-being etc. also discusses the father with reference to the 9th house in one of the ensuing chapters. Thus it follows that both the 9th and 10th are primary houses related to the father.

All articles, prosperity, income, quadrupeds etc. are to be understood from the 11th house.

# TWELFTH HOUSE

From the 12th house, one can know about expenses, history of enemies, one's own death etc.

# PROSPERITY OR ANNIHILATION OF A HOUSE

Predict prosperity of the house which is aspected or is conjunct by a benefic. Also when its lord is in Prabuddhavastha or in Kaumaravastha or in the 10th house, the bhava's wellbeing is indicated. The bhava which is aspected by its lord or whose lord is with a malefic or with one of evil and such other (i.e. 8th, 12th) or is defeated in a planetary war or is in one of the...






# Erthat parasara Hora Sastrtt

# threc Avasthas, viz, Vriddhavastha, Mritavastha and Suptavastha

Notes: The prosperity or well-being of a house under the following conditions is assured:

- The house that contains a benefic.
- The house that is aspected by a benefic.
- The house whose lord is in Yuvavastha or in Kumara Avastha.

These two Avasthas are among the 5 viz. Kumara, Yutbna, Vriddha and Mrita by Avasthas, being respectively in 6. portion. This is for an odd sign placement. It is reverse in the case of an even sign. However, also see ch. 45 infra.

To say, if the lord of a house is in 6. to 1 of an odd sign, he will be one of the two Avasthas required. Alternatively, it should be between 12' and 24' of an odd sign. (If a planet is debilitated or is combust, the goods cited are void).

(d) Praluddhavastha is a state, another name for Jagradavastha, meaning of awakeness. This applies to a planet in own or in exaltation sign. The bhava owned by an exalted or placed planet in own sign flourishes. Except the luminaries, the five other own each two houses. It is that a planet placed in own house, it predominantly acts on behalf of that house occupied by it. Simultaneously, the house also gets strengthened by virtue of such a placement.

For example, Saturn owns the 3rd and 4th for Scorpio. If he is in the 4th, he will give mainly good effects of the 4th (the Moola'trikona house). This does not mean that the 3rd is left uncared.

(c) The house owned by a planet placed in the ascendant will produce good results. Closely related to the 10th (or effective cusp meridian) it is the most potent point of the natus. For details, see 2 of my work, "Doctrinor notes for rule 1, ch. 2".

Next we are told of Suke Xsil-Retnld., of the conditions under which a house suffers annihilations which are:

- The bhava unaspected by its lord does not flourish.

Each bhava cannot be under the aspect of its lord. Then this does not mean that the bhava suffers annihilation. It may be construed that in the absence of such an aspect, the bhava can...





# Chapter II

look upto sources mentioned alternative eartier. If a malefic is there for bhava, its lord's aspect is an antidote.

(b) The lord of a bhava is a disadvantage for the bhava. If the said malefic is joining a friendly planet to the bhava then the evil is minimized. Even an exalted malefic, if it is in favorable houses, may also be expected.

(c) The lord of a house in conjunction with the lord of 6th/8th/12th cannot be productive. If he himself is an evil lord, then some relief can be expected. This is mainly from a point and not in all respects.

(d) If a planet is defeated in planetary war, its bhava's potence is void. Normally, we are taught that the two are on the same degree with lesser longitude there occurs a war and the winner is declared.

In this connection, please refer to (Vol. II of our present work). Rajan has a detailed and elaborate account of planetary war. According to him if two planets have identical longitudes to the minute of arc there is a war, (This does not involve luminaries). He adds that they should be on the same latitude, i.e. both northern or both southern. The one with higher latitude involving Saturn is declared winner. He gives an example for 0347 hrs on 15th December 1925:

|        | Longitude |          | Latitude |
| ------ | --------- | -------- | -------- |
|        | Mars      | 209° 24' | 0N21     |
| Saturn | 209° 24'  | 2N25     |          |

He declares Saturn as the winner. We need not rush to the conclusion that Mr. Rajan's version is contrary to Parasara's. We should appreciate the pains taken by Mr. Rajan in throwing more light on the subject. He gives more advanced and sound arguments reproduced here for the sake of achieving brevity.




# Brihat Parasara Hoi.s Sastra

# practical

For purposes, we are guided by the collaboration of Mr. Rajan.

(e) The house (i.e. whose lord is in Vriddhavastha) is said to be ineffective from the viewpoint of good results.

(f) If a planet is in Mgi!rygllA (in an Avastha, will be destroyed) its bhava is in an even sign or in the last 6" of an odd sign.

(g) Lastly, a planet in the neutralises due to a debilitated planet or the one in an inimical camp.

The reader will thus see the significance present in the slokas, of the principle prakasr" enumerated by Hemaprabhe Suri, a Jain astrologer of eminence, in his work 'Trailokya' (edited by Sarup Sharma, Lahore) that the bhava occupied by the Moon undergoes good or bad effects. That is, if the Moon is increasing, good effects will increase; otherwise effects will diminish.

# 8. COILED BIRTH

There is a birth in either one of Aries, Taurus or Leo containing Saturn or Mars, and the child is born with a coil around the limb. The corresponding Rasi or Navamsa will be in accordance with the rising.

Notes: This rule applies to only three ascendants, viz. Mars or Saturn should be in Aries, Taurus and Leo. The limbs are shown in sloka 4 of ch. 4 sup. These apply to the Navamsas well. The present slokas of the chapter have limbs denoted in 12-15 and should not be mixed for the purpose of coiled birth, which will be simply obvious to the reader.
