# 9. BIRTH OF TWINS

The native, who has a quadruped sign while in dual signs with strength, is born as one of the twins.

Notes: The signs are: Aries, Leo, Taurus, Capricorn and Sagittarius. If the Sun is in a quadruped sign while all others are in dual signs-Gemini, the native will be one of the twins. The other six planets be endowed with strength.






# Chapter 12

# 1A. TO BE NURTURED By 3 MOTHERS

If the Sun and Moon join in one bhava and fall in the same Navamsa, the native will be nurtured by 3 different mothers for 3 months from its birth and later will be brought up by its father and brother.

Notes: In my opinion, the position of the luminaries in conjunction seems to be excepted. They should be in the same quarter of a constellation and will naturally be in one Navamsa. This combination obviously implies loss of mother within the first three months, apart from meaning general. A brother calls for interpretation in relative.

# 11. IMPORTANCE

The learned in astrology should base the effects on the Moon also as applicable to the ascendant. Now explained are clues on one's identity marks etc.

Notes: This well-known rule is a speciality in Hindu Astrology and has the sage's sanction. The Moon is given a significant status equal to the ascendant for she rules one's mind and the mind in turn functions according to one's Karma.

# 12-14. EYES, EARS, DECANATES AND BODILY LIMBS

Head, nose, temple, chin and face is the order of limbs denoted by the various houses when the first decanate of a sign.






Brihat Parasara Ilora Sastra

In the case of the second decanate ascending, the order is neck, shoulder, arm, side, heart, stomach and navel. The order for the third decanate ascending is pelvis, testicles, calf, thigh, knee, and foot. The portion that has already risen indicates the left side of the body (where the one yet to rise is invisible). Half denotes the right side of the body.

Notes: The portion that has already risen is known as half of the horoscope. From the cusp of the ascendant to the cusp of the descendant, the 10th cusp is visible half. The rest is invisible half, which represents the left side of the body while invisible right side of the body.

The limbs suggested by the 2 shlokas in three different orders are shown in the three diagrams for an easy grasp. The assumption is that the first decanate, second decanate, and third decanate of Aries rise in the respective cases:

| ear            | Aries ascendant |
| first decanate | side            |
| nostril        | temple          |

Brihat parasora Hora Sastra

The above three diagrams are made for the three decanates of Aries ascendant. The reader can change positions according to the sign and its decanate prevailing at birth. The two halves in the ascendant and Zth please noted may be attentively.

The corresponding part for female is ovary as against male's testicle. Similarly, female's privity prevails in exchange of male organ. Pelvis is made into two parts, viz. true pelvis and false pelvis. The true pelvis is denoted by the portion of the zodiac to rise while false by the half of zodiac rose.

15. LIMBS AFFECTED: The limb related by occupation to a malefic will have ulcers or scars while the one by benefic will have a mark (like moles etc). So say the learned in astrology.

Notes: Also see sloka 6, ch. 4 of Saravati, which states that a malefic or a benefic if be in own Rasi or Navamsa, will be effects right from birth. In other cases, it will be in the course of one's life that these effects will come to possess.

# Chapter 13

# Effects of Second House

COMBINATIONS FOR WEALTH: O excellent Brahmanas, listen to me speaking on the effects of the 2nd.






# Chapter 13

If the lord of the 2nd house is in the 2nd or is in an angle or in a trine, he will promote one's wealth (or monetary state). If he should be in the 6th/8th/12th, financial conditions will decline. A benefic in the 2nd will give wealth while a malefic instead will destroy the same.

Notes: Venus or Jupiter in the 2nd will be wholly favorable for us. Jupiter in the 2nd, however, is ruling aspects will be smooth. That is why the sage specifically mentions this fact in the sloka. It does not mean that Jupiter, in the 2nd, will be wholly harmful. This denotes a problematic situation in money matters. Various authors have given different views in their works; for a summary of which the reader may switch over to page 491 of my English translation of Saravali.

One will be wealthy if Jupiter is in the 2nd or is with Mars. The lord of the 2nd are two independent conditions: There are notes in the 2nd, in this verse Jupiter, should denote wealth. If the native be the ruler of the 2nd, in that case, Jupiter should be abundant or not. Whether the 2nd, if be by conjunction will be acquired by the native; wealth in the 2nd house occupied by them.

Notes: If the lord of the 2nd is in the 11th, wealth will be acquired by the native. Alternatively, these two lords may join in an angle or in a trine. The 11th lord has a say in financial matters apart from the 2nd. One's gains are indicated by the 11th lord. If he is in exchange with the lord, the native will be wealthy. These two planets in the ascendant, 4th, 7th, 10th, 5th, 9th will also lead to financial gains.






# Erthat Parasara

# Hora Sastra

5. If the lord of the 2nd is in an angle while is in a trine the lrth lord thereof or is aspected by or conjunct by Jupiter Venus, and the subject will be wealthy.

Notes: The lord of the 2nd should be in the 1st or 4th/7th/10th house. The 11th lord should be counted in the 5th/8th from the house occupied by the 2nd lord. Alternatively, the 2nd lord should be related (and) in conjunction or by aspect to Jupiter or Venus. Both the combinations gaining wealth.

6-7. YOGAS FOR POVERTY: One will be penniless if the lord of the 2nd is in an evil house while the 11th lord is so placed and also the 2nd is occupied by a malefic. There will be penury right from birth and the native will have to beg even for his food if the lords of the 2nd and the 11th are both combust with malefics.

Notes: The lords of the 2nd and 11th should be jointly carried in the 6th/8th/12th or individually disposed in any two of the three said houses. Simultaneously the 2nd house needs a malefic in it. Thus there are afflictions from three directions which will make the native extremely poor. Even food is denied to one having combust 2nd lord and combust 11th lord. Alternatively, the 2nd lord may be with a severe malefic while similarly the 11th lord is also placed. The conjunction of the 2nd lord with a Yogakarka, although a malefic, will not be adverse matter in the case of finance. On the contrary, for example, Mercury, the 2nd lord, joining Saturn of a Taurus native, will make financial profit superior.






# Chapter 13

# 8. OF WEALTH THROUGH THE KING

The lords of the 2nd and 11th (jointly or separately) should be relegated to the 6th/8th while Mars is in the 11th and Rahu is in the 2nd, the native will lose his wealth on account of punishments.

Notes: This combination will cause financial losses through penalties, fines imposed by the government, etc. Modern context. Monetary deficiencies will persist throughout.

# 9. EXPENSES ON GOOD ACCOUNTS

In the 11th, Jupiter in the 2nd, and Venus a benefic lord conjunct in the 12th while the 2nd is a benefic there will be expenses on religious or charitable grounds.

# 10. FAME ETC.

If the 2nd lord is in own sign or is exalted, the native will look after his people, and others will help and become famous.

Notes: Our text requires the 2nd lord to be in exaltation or own sign so that the native will look after his family members. It has been practically seen that the 2nd lord's dignity is essential for one to be helpful to others and be dutiful towards family members.

Chaukhamba has a different condition in this edition: It states that the 2nd lord should be deep in exaltation or in own sign and be in aspect to Jupiter. The result therein is 'fame liked by all'. The condition of 'deep' exaltation seems to me to be somewhat excessive while a simple alternative, as such, I feel mere exaltation of the 2nd lord is enough for obtaining the results.






# 136

# Porasara

# Erlhat Hora Sastra

# 11. EFFORTLESS ACQUISITION

If the 2nd lord is a benefic, good division like Paravatamsa, and be in a good division, he will be endowed with wealth effortlessly.

There are all kinds of Vargas in family, six good Vargas out of the Dasavarga scheme (vide supra). The text denotes "Paravatamsa" and "Paravatamsadau".

The higher Vargas denote such or other good divisions. To be in Devalokamsa, the 2nd lord should be in Paravatamsa or Brahmalokamsa, in the Dasavarga scheme. The corresponding superior Amsas are used above.

In the Dasavarga scheme, the fixes denote why the sage said the good divisions are obvious. This varga denotes the good divisions, i.e., above 50% of good dignity.

The 2nd lord being endowed with a Varga brings in effortless wealth and wealth of all kinds. It follows that the 2nd disposition (Jupiter) will decide the financial status of a native.

# 12. EYES

If the 2nd lord is endowed with beautiful eyes, the native will possess beautiful eyes. Should there be deformity or disease, the 6th, 8th, or 12th lord signifies the disease.

Notes: "Netresa" does not mean that the 2nd lord and 12th lord have nothing to do with eyes. Precisely, this is from the right eye and left eye lord over respectively.

The beauty of the eyes is known, it is from the 2nd house only. Jupiter is said to give beautiful eyes when placed well in the 2nd, or the 2nd lord in exaltation.

While Venus will not deprive one of beautiful sight, defects will result from the said position. Mercury in the 2nd will have a say on the speech rather than on the sight.

Hence, Jupiter's position in the 2nd is a safe bet for strong sight and beauty of the eyes, if the planet is not with evils of fall and the like.






# Chapter 14

# 13. UNTRUTHFUL PERSON

If the 2nd house and its lord are conjunct malefics, the native will be a tale-bearer, speak untruth and will be afflicted by windy diseases.

Notes: The 2nd house and its lord are referred to in the matter of windy diseases. Gastric troubles, rheumatism and other disorders are classified under windy disorders. If the 2nd house or its lord is associated with Saturn, it will cause affliction. If Jupiter is in affliction, rheumatism and gastric troubles will come to pass.

# Effects Of The Third House

The 3rd house should be conjunct or aspected by a benefic, the native will be endowed with co-born brothers and courageous.

Notes: 'Bhratru' in Sanskrit simply means brother. Proper adjectives are to be added, Jyeshto for elder and Kanishta for younger. The 3rd house specifically deals with the after-born while the 1st house deals with the pre-born. This can lead us to consider Mars for the 3rd bhava and Jupiter for the 11th house. The younger sister is denoted by the 3rd house while the elder sister is denoted by the 11th house.







# 138

# Brihat Parasara Hora Sastra

If the 3rd lord along with Mars aspects the native the 3rd house will enjoy good results due to the 3rd house. Alternately these two planets may be in the 3rd itself. Notes: Mars alone in the 3rd, except in Capricorn, Scorpio or in Aries, is not conductive to brothers.

The form of sloka jointly is different in that the 3rd house be aspected or occupied by Mars and the 3rd lord for the prosperity of coborn.

# 3.

Destruction at once of coborn will come to pass if the said planets are together with a malefic or in a sign owned by a malefic. Notes: "The coborn will not live long" is the phrase given by the "Sadyo nihantarau". Mars joining a malefic's sign or a malefic is said to be adverse for the longevity of coborn. Similarly Jupiter and such the 11th lord in a state is adverse for elder brothers and elder sisters; and placed Venus the 7th lord so for spouse, the Jupiter and the 5th lord placed progeny; so for Sun placed father, and the 9th lord so for the Moon and placed the 4th lord so for mother, and on and so forth. So to the significator and the concerned lord of the house together in a malefic's sign (or in an evil house) will bring harm to the said relative.

# 4-4t. FEMALE AND MALE COBORN

If the 3rd lord is a female planet or if the house be occupied by female planets, one will have sisters born after him. Similarly male signs denote younger brothers. Should coborn be of mixed nature, it will be obtained of both sexes. These effects will be declared after assessing the strength and weakness of the concerned.





# Chapter 14

# Notes: Saturn and Mercury

Saturn and Mercury are termed planets. Rahu and Ketu are shadowy ones. In the matter of coborn progeny, the deciding sex of Saturn and Rahu be treated as males while Mercury and Ketu are females. (Trailokyapraknsika vide sloka 12 treats Ketu as a female and Rahu as a eunuch. Daivagnabharana considers the reverse of this at one place and quotes a different school of thought. Thus: Rahu is a male and Ketu a eunuch.)

All signs are male signs and all even signs are female signs. Male signs exclusively occupied by male planets will cause the birth of brothers. Converse is the case with female signs occupied by female planets. This should be known from the 3rd house. If the 3rd house is occupied by a male planet as well as a female planet, there will be brothers and sisters as well. The contribution will come if the contributor is strong. For example, Jupiter in a male sign if strong will cause the birth of a brother. If he is weak, the acquisition of a brother through Jupiter will not be fruitful.

Then to look up to alternative sources whether the native will have a brother or not.

Should the 3rd lord and Mars be together in the destruction of coborn will result. Happiness will come to pass if Mars or the 3rd lord is in an angle, trine, exaltation/friendly or in a division.

The suggestions given in the notes for sloka 3 about spouse, brother, elder mother etc. may be suitably respected in this with the help of the present verse. For example, if Venus and the 7th lord are together in the native's married life will be short in bad taste. Similarly, their conjunction in an angle or in a trine will confer long-lasting benefic effects.

Further hint that can be taken from the verse is: If a significator and house lord join together in a sign that is identical with debilitation/inimical sign for one of them.

# Chapter 14

There will be 7 coborn if the 12th (some texts read as the 11th lord) joins Mars and Jupiter while the 3rd is occupied by the Moon. If the Moon is lonely placed in aspect in the 3rd to male planets, there will be younger brothers; the aspect of Venus denotes younger sisters.

# 14. ADVERSE PLANETS

The Sun in the 3rd will destroy the preborn. The afterborn will be destroyed if Saturn is found in the 3rd. In the same situation, Mars will destroy both the preborn and later born.

Notes: Sage Bhrigu also opines that the Sun in the 3rd house will not allow the native to retain his elder brothers. This position will affect relationship with sisters. Regarding Mars, one's placement in the 3rd, Garga Maharshi states that the native will obtain two brothers and two sisters, of whom all the 4 will pass away early. The placement of Mars in the 3rd has also adverse say on the native's character. For further details, see my detailed notes in Bhavas, in the chapter of Saravali.

After estimating the strength and weakness of such yogas, the effects related to brothers and sisters be announced.






# Chapter 15

# Effects Of The Fourth House

1. O excellent Brahmins, thus have been briefly told the effects about the 3rd house. Now listen to the results related to the 4th house.

2. HOUSING COMFORTS: One will have residential comforts in full degree if the 4th is occupied by its lord or by the ascendant lord and be aspected by a benefic.

3. MISCELLANEOUS: Should the 5th lord be in his own house, or in own Navamsa or in exaltation, the native will be endowed with comforts related to lands, conveyances, musical houses and instruments.

4. HOUSING COMFORTS: If the 4th lord joins the 10th lord in an angle or in a trine, the native will acquire full mansions.

5. RELATIVES: Should Mercury be in the ascendant while the 4th lord being a benefic is aspected by another benefic, the native will be honoured by his relatives.





# Chapter 15

# 6. LONG-LIVING MOTHER

If the 4th house is occupied by a benefic while its lord is in his exaltation sign, the indicator of mother is endowed with strength, have a long-living mother.

Notes: The stronger among the Moon and Mars is denoted as the significator of mother, vide srokas infra. There are still many more views about the karakatwas of parents given by various authors.

# 7. HAPPINESS TO MOTHER

The native's mother will be happy if the 4th lord is in an angle while Venus is also in an angle as Mercury is exalted.

# 8. SATURN

The Sun in the 4th, Moon in the 9th and Mars in the 11th - this yoga will confer cows and buffaloes on the native.

# 9. DUMBNESS

Should the 4th house be a movable one while its lord and Mars are together in the 6th or the 8th house, the native will be dumb.




# Brihat Parasara Sastra

CONVEYANCES

If the ascendant lord is benefic while the lord is in the 11th (Venus) the 4th in fall and the significator is in the 12th, then the native will obtain conveyances in the year.

Should the 4th lord be exalted with Venus, then one will acquire conveyances in his year. It will be in the 32nd year if the 4th lord joins the 10th lord in the 4th house, as the 4th lord will confer conveyances.

A benefic related to the 4th house will produce only malefic effects in respect of conveyances. This is known why the 4th lord should not be in fall for obtainment of conveyances.

This condition seems to result as the next line adds that the 4th lord may be in the 11th. To me, it occurs that the correct version should read as: If the ascendant lord is benefic while the 4th is tenanted by Venus and the 11th lord is in the 4th, early obtainment of conveyance will come to pass.

Another similar effect is an exchange between the 4th and the 11th. Should the 4th be in conjunction with or aspect the lord of the 4th house, then the native will be free from accidents and will be happy.

A malefic replacing the said will cause severe losses concerning vehicles.

# Chapter 16

# Of The Fifth House Effects

O Brahmin, now I tell the effects of the 5th house. If the lord of the 5th house is in an angle or in a trine, one will enjoy happiness through children. Should the lord be in the 6th, 8th, or 12th, there will be no offspring, and if the 5th be with malefics, they will be weak, combust, or there will be issues obtained only by chance.

Should there be no children; even if they quit the world soon.

Notes: "Suta" in Sanskrit does not exclude a female issue for it means "son" exclusively in such occasions where the specific expression is needed interpreting according to circumstances.

The good conjunction of the 5th lord in the ascendant will ensure obtainment of children apart from happiness. If they join in an evil house, they will prove a defect in this respect.

If the 5th lord is in the 6th, the ascendant lord is conjunct. If the 5th lord is in the first, whereafter the native will lose his child. Mars, however, will not be fertile to yield an offspring.






Brihat Parosara Hora Sastra

5. Should the 5th lord be in fall in the 6th, or the 12th while Mercury and Ketu are in the 5th, the native's wife will give birth to one child only.

6. If the 5th lord is in fall and not in aspect to the 5th while Saturn and Mercury are in the 5th, the native's wife will give birth to one child only.

7. Should the 9th lord be in the ascendant while the 5th lord is in fall and Ketu is in the 5th along with Mercury, progeny will be obtained after a great deal of presence of ordalium.

Notes: The very presence of Mercury, Ketu, or Saturn in the 5th will join in a doubtful picture of progeny. If two of them are in the 5th, then there will be Kakavandhya Dosha (obtaining only a single issue) for the wife of the native, childlessness or even.

8. If the 5th lord is in the 6th, or the 12th or be in an inimical sign or in fall or in the 5th itself, the native will beget issues with difficulty.

9. Should the 5th house be owned by Saturn and be occupied or aspected by Saturn and Mandi, one will have adopted issues.

Notes: "Mandi," is the word used in the text which means Gulika. This identicality has been narrated in a previous chapter.

Should the native be brought up by 3 mothers or 2 fathers. The luminaries should be in the same Rasi and Navamsa. As a result of this yoga, the child will be brought up by 3 females equal to mother or women as father (i.e. paternal relatives soon after birth).

Adopted issue is indicated if the 5th is tenanted by the Moon and its lord is in the 12th, and while endowed with strength are many children. There is aspected by strong Mercury, Jupiter and Venus.




# Brinat Parasara

# Hora Sastra

If the 5th lord is with the Moon or be in her decanate, the native will beget daughters, so say astrologers.

Notes: The 5th lord's joining the Moon will confer more daughters than sons. The Moon is a planet of multiplicity and hence there will be a number of daughters. An alternative suggested by the sage is that the 5th lord should be in a decanate owned by the Moon. The Moon's decanates are: the first ten degrees of Cancer, the second ten degrees of Pisces, and the third ten degrees of Scorpio. If the 5th lord occupies a degree as above, then the native will obtain daughters.

# 14.

If the 5th lord is in a movable sign while Saturn is with the Moon, the child (so born) is in questionable birth.

Notes: There are 3 conditions denoted so that the owner of the horoscope is an illegal product. These are: (a) The 5th lord should be in a movable sign. (b) The 5th house should be occupied by Saturn, and (c) The Moon should be with Rahu. The combinations indicating illegal birth get nullified under certain conditions. For details see p. 55 of my English translation of Hora Sastra also.

# 15.

Undoubtedly the native is born of other's wombs if the Moon is in the 8th from the ascendant while Jupiter is from the Moon. Malefic's aspect/association in this Yoga is essential.





Chapter 16

16. If the 5th lord is exalted or be in the 2nd, 5th or 9th or be conjunct or aspected by Jupiter, obtainment of children will be there.

Notes: Anyone of the following 3 states of the 5th lord will ensure 5th lord in exaltation:

1. The 5th lord in the 2nd, 5th/9th house.
2. The 5th lord related to Jupiter by aspect.
3. Though Jupiter may be in conjunction with the 5th lord, it will ensure 6th or 8th obtainment of children.

17. One will obtain children that will indulge in mean deeds if the 5th is occupied by 3 or 4 malefics while the 5th lord is in fall. A benefic (including Mercury) in the 5th is excluded in the combination.

18. If the 5th is occupied by Jupiter while its lord is with Venus, one will obtain an offspring in the 32nd/33rd year.

19. Should the 5th lord be in an angle along with Jupiter, one will beget a child at the age of 30 or 36.

20. If Jupiter is in the 9th from the ascendant while Venus is in the 9th from Jupiter along with the ascendant lord, one will beget a child at the age of 40.







# Brihat Parasara

2t. The native will lose his child at the age of 32 if the lord is in the 5th, Rahu is in a malefic debilitation, and Jupiter is conjunct.

22. There will be loss of children at 33 and if a malefic is in the 5th from Jupiter while another is in the ascendant.

23. Should Mandi be in the ascendant while the lord is in fall, grief on account of loss of child will come to pass at the age of 56.

Notes: Mandi and Gulika are one and the same as described supra. The placement of Gulika in the ascendant while its lord is in debilitation will cause death of an offspring at the age of 56. Similarly, the debilitation of Gulika's dispositor will cause harm to the bhava concerned, i.e., the bhava occupied by Gulika.

Nine will be the number of sons that one will beget if Jupiter is in the 9th exaltation as it is with the lord and occupied by its own lord. There will be eight sons if Jupiter is in the 5th/9th while the 2nd lord is in the 10th. Saturn from the ascendant while is in the 9th give 7 sons out of which twins will be born twice. If the 5th lord in the 5th itself, will denote the birth of 7 sons out of which 3 will pass away. Only one son will be if Jupiter is in the 5th while Saturn has a malefic in it or if the native will beget offspring only through his 2nd wife. Should the 3rd be occupied by a malefic while the 5th has Saturn as lord with Mars, one will live long but lose his children one after the other as they are born.

# 17

# Chapter The Sixth Of House Effects

O Brahmin, listen attentively. The following are the effects produced by the 6th house relating to diseases, ulcers, etc.

1. Should the 6th lord be in the ascendant/8th, or in the 6th itself, there will be ulcers or bruises on the body. The sign becoming the 6th house will lead to the concerned limb.
2. ULCERS/BRUISES in the 6th/8th. The Karaka of a relative or the lord of such a house joining the 6th lord or being in the 6th/8th indicates ulcers/bruises. The Sun with such lordship to such a relative like father denotes affectation of head, and in such a house the Moon denotes nose, Venus denotes face, neck, navel, eyes, Saturn denotes feet and the abdomen.
3. In these three notes, we are instructed to know the possible afflictions to the native's relatives and to the native himself both from the horoscope of the native.






# Chapter 6

Firstly a certain significator or a certain lord should join the 6th lord or be in the 6th/8th house so that the relative signified by the said Karaka incurs ulcers, bruises etc. For the horoscope, the 6th lord is Venus. A Lagna in Sagittarius, the 6th is Taurus and the 8th is Cancer. Suppose Jupiter or the Matrukaraka Moon (signifying mother) joins the 8th house, though Venus is in Taurus. The Moon should not be deemed harmful in this regard. As a result, the mother will also incur bruises, ulcer, etc. by planets.

The relatives signified are denoted in ch, 32, infra. To know the possible affliction, the second clue is in the body. If the Sun is the lord of a particular area of the native, or is with the 6th lord or is in the 6th/8th, the native will be apt to incur affliction. As regards, Rahu and Ketu, their position in the 6th/8th house need only be considered in the context. Hence, normal disorders will cause stomachial afflictions.

# 6. FACIAL DISEASES

The lord of the ascendant should be in a sign of Mars or the face and be aspected by Mercury. Even if Mars, ruling the ascendant, is in Gemini or in Virgo and is aspected by Mercury, the native will suffer facial diseases. The placement of Mars in own sign can look different for Aries Lagna or for Scorpio Lagna. For Aries Lagna, Mars in Aries and aspected by Mercury will not produce the said adversity unless affiicted otherwise.

Man is seriously afflicted.






Brihat Parasara Hora Shastra

# 7-8. LEPROSY:

or Mercury having ownership of the ascending sign will cause leprosy. If the Moon is in the ascendant however Cancer and be with Rahu, there will occur leprosy. Saturn in place of Rahu will cause black leprosy. Mars similarly will afflict one with blood-leprosy.

# 9-12. DISEASES IN GENERAL:

If the ascendant occupied by the lords of the 6th and along with the sun, native will be afflicted by fever and tumours. Mars replacing sun will cause severing and hardening of the brood vessels and hits by weapons. Mercury so featuring will bring in bilious diseases while Jupiter in similar case will destroy disease. Similarly Venus will cause diseases through Saturn windy diseases, females, Rahu danger and Ketu navel through diseases. The Moon in such a conjunction will inflict dangers through water and phlegmatic disorders. Estimated similar be made from the respective significators for relatives like father.

# 23-25. UNFORTUNATE YEARS (continued)

The said 8th lord should simultaneously be in the 8th place from the Navamsa (i.e. 9th ascendant in the Navamsa chart). As a result, the native will incur blood vessel disorders in the 19th/22nd year of age.

Loss of wealth will come during the 31st year to pass if the 11th and 6th lords exchange their Rasis.

# Chapter 18

# Effects Of The Seventh House

O excellent Brahmins' listen to me detailing the effects of the 7th lord in his own sign or in exaltation, the wife (and his marriage), will obtain full happiness.

1. Should the 7th lord be in the 6th, 8th, or 12th, the wife will be sickly. This, however, applies as placement or exaltation to own house.

Notes: The placement of the 7th lord in the 6th/8th/12th house will cause a sickly wife. (Similarly Venus in an evil house or own sign, then this happens)




# Chapter

in Capricorn for a Saturn be feared. For example, need not an native for Aries in Pisces.

3. EXCESSIVE LIBIDINOUSNESS / DEATH OF WIFE:

If Venus is in the 7th, the native will cause loss of wife.

4-5. The 7th lord should be endowed by a benefic or be aspected and be conjunct with strength. Wealthy, honourable, happy and fortunate.

Co-occurrence, if the 7th lord is in fall or is combust or is in an inimical placement. There is plurality of wives and sickness to them will acquire one of wives.

Notes: Plurality of debilitated 7th lord's occupying its sign. There is a practical experience of disappointments and delays to the 7th lord will cause sickness to spouse. If the 7th lord is in an enemy sign, the native's wife will scarcely honour him.

6. PLURALITY OF WIVES: If the 7th lord is in a sign of Saturn or of Venus and be aspected particularly in exaltation, the same effects will come to pass.




Brihat Parasara Hora Shastra

# 7-gt. MISCELLANEOUS MATTERS

The native will befriend barren females (for sexual union) if the Sun is in the 7th. The Moon will cause association with such females as placed in the 7th. Mars (or girls with menses) will denote association with marriageable females. Mercury indicates mean females, harlots, and females belonging to traders' community. Wife of a Brahmin will be in the native's association if Jupiter is in the 7th. Base females are denoted by Saturn/Rahu/Ketu in the 7th (including the lord, vide ch. 24, 79) in the matter of sexual union.

Notes: Any sloka is normally indicative of absence of sterling character in the native. If the Sun is in the 7th in a horoscope promising, the native will seek pleasures from females who are barren. As regards the Moon, the sign becoming sexually corresponds to the 7th house. For example, when Virgo becomes the 7th house, Libra denotes prostitutes, Gemini a wife and so forth. Mars in the 7th denotes a female that is in her monthly course or one who has come of marriageable age or is devoid of conceiving ability. Similarly, Jupiter in the 7th is also no exception.

The results should be declared only after ensuring that the native is disposed to go out of the way for sexual union with the support of other horoscopic indications.

# 9-9t.

Mars denotes a female with attractive breasts. Saturn indicates a sick and weak spouse. Jupiter will bring a spouse with prominent breasts while Venus will bring one with excellent breasts.

these four ascendants, there must be severe affliction to the spouse character. The native will indulge in kissing the privities of the female if Venus is in a Rasi or Navamsa by or in conjunction with Mars, or is aspected with Mars. That is, he will have unusual habits in the matter of sexual gratification from the female.

If Venus is related to Saturn and his divisions instead of Mars and his divisions as stated in point 3 above, the native will have ugly relations with another male, for subduing his lust.

# 15. WORTEY SPOUSE..

The native will beget a spouse endowed with seven virtues who will expand his dynasty by sons and grandsons while the 7th lord is exalted and the 7th is occupied by a strong ascendant lord and a benefic.

Notes: The above verses hint at the possibility of the native obtaining children (and grandchildren) if the ascendant is in the 7th with a benefic as the 7th lord disposed in exaltation sign. The combination is meant for the native begetting a virtuous wife as well. The exaltation of the 7th lord is capable of bestowing a virtuous wife, if not.

# 16. EVILS TO SPOUSE...

If the 7th house or its lord is conjunct a malefic, the native's wife will incur evils, especially if the 7th house or its lord is bereft of strength.

# 17. LOSS OF SPOUSE..

If the 7th lord is devoid of strength and is relegated to the 6th, 8th or the 12th, or if the 7th...






Chapter 18

# 18. LACK OF CONJUGAL FELICITY

If the Moon is in the 7th as the 7th lord is in the 12th and the Karaka (indicator Venus) is bereft of strength, the native will not be endowed with marital happiness.

Notes: The Moon referred to here should obviously be decreasing. The Moon increasing, while the part of the planetary conditions as stated in the sloka is fulfilled, will improve the situation.

# 19-21. PLURALITY OF WIVES

One will have two wives if the 7th lord is in fall, or in a malefic sign while the 7th house, or the 7th Navamsa belongs to a malefic planet. If Mars and Venus are in the 7th or if Saturn is in the 7th while the lord of the ascendant is in the 8th, the native will have 3 wives. There will be many wives if Venus is in a dual sign while its lord is in exaltation as the 7th lord is endowed with strength.

Notes: For a dual marriage, the 7th from the natal ascendant or the 7th from Navamsa should be owned by a eunuch. So to say, Gemini, Virgo, Capricorn or Aquarius should be the 7th as above. While this is fulfilled, the 7th lord should be in his sign of debilitation or in a malefic's sign. The other two yogas are simple and need no elaboration.

# 35-39.

# TIMING OF WIFE'S DEATH

Loss of wife will occur in the year or 33rd year of age of the native if 7th lord is in fall while Venus is in the 8th. One will lose spouse in his 19th year if the lord is in the 7th while 12th lord is in the 7th. The native's wife will die within three days due to snake bite if the native has Rahu and Mars in the 7th. If Venus dispositor is in a sign of Saturn, death of wife will take place during the 11th or 21st year of age. Should the ascendant lord be in his sign of debilitation as the 2nd lord is in the 7th, loss of wife will occur in the 13th year of age.







# Chapter 19

# The Eighth House Effects

1. LONG LIFE: O excellent listen to the effects of the 8th house. If the 8th lord is in an angle, the native's life is indicated to be long.

2. SHORT LIFE: Should the 8th lord be in the ascendant or malefic, the native will live a short life.

# Chapter 19

# THREE MARRIAGES: Should the Moon from while Mercury be in the 7th Venus is in the 7th from the Moon and the 8th lord is in the 5th (from the ascendant), in the year 10th followed by another in the year 22nd and another in the 33rd year.

# DEATH OF WIFE: If the 6th, 7th and 8th are occupied by Mars, their order (long). Rahu and Saturn, the native's wife will not live.

# 3. SATURN

# TENTH AND LORD ABOUT LONGEVITY:

Similarly consider Saturn and 10th lord in the matter of longevity. To get the actual import of this verse, we should read it in the context of the previous verse. So life will pass to say, short if:

1. The 8th lord is in the 8th along with a malefic lord or along with the ascendant.
2. Saturn joins a malefic/ascendant lord in the 8th house.
3. The 10th lord is in the 8th along with a malefic planet/ascendant.

4-7. LONG LIFE: There will be long life if the 6th lord is in the 12th or if the 6th lord is in the 6th as the 12th lord is in the 6th or if the 12th lord is in the 6th and 12th lord are in the 8th. If the lords of the 5th, 6th, and 10th and of the ascendant, are in their own Rasis, enjoy navamsas, or in friendly signs, the native will have a long span of life. Should the lords of the 10th and Saturn are all disposed severally in an angle, trine or in the 11th, the subject will live long. Like these, there are many yogas dealing with the issue of longevity, strength and weakness of planets concerned be estimated in deciding longevity.

Notes: In sloka 4, we have three yogas for long life. These are:

1. The 6th lord in the 12th.

# The 6th and 12th Lords Simultaneously

The 6th lord in the ascendant while the 12th lord is in the 8th. The combinations in the two verses are quite clear.

# 8-13. LIFE.

One's span of life will be between 20 to 32 years if the ascendant lord is weak while the 8th lord falls in an angle. The native will be only short-lived if the 8th lord has a malefic in it and is in a position of strength. Death will be instant at birth if the 8th lord is conjunct with malefics.

The 8th and 12th lords are in angles/trines while the ascendant lord in the 6th. Malefic yoga has the 8th lord in it: this will cause immediate death if the 8th lord is in the 5th house, and all are malefics. Within a month of birth, death will befall if the 8th lord is in conjunction with malefics.

While the Moon itself is with beneficial aspect, the native will be bereft of life.

# Notes:

If the 8th lord is in an angle, the native will be long-lived, according to sloka of the chapter. The lord bereft of strength will reduce life span in a case.

# Long Life

One will be long-lived if the lord is in exaltation with respect to the ascendant. If the lord is exceedingly strong and supported by a benefic, the person concerned will be wealthy, virtuous, and long-lived.

Notes: Even if Jupiter is well-placed in the 9th house, it leads to a long span of life. If the Moon being in the ascendant exaltation, doubtlessly the life will be lengthy.

# Chapter 20

# Effects Of The Ninth House

O Brahmin, listen to effects of the 9th house. One will be fortunate (affluent) if Jupiter, the 9th lord, is in the 9th with strength. The 9th lord should be in the 9th house while the ascendant lord is endowed with strength; one will be fortunate.

Notes: "Bhagyasthana" is a given name to the 9th house. "Bhagya" denotes fortunes, affluence, etc. Hence, from the 9th house, one's capacity to retain the wealth earned should be studied.

# 3. FORTUNATE (AFFLUENT) FATHER

If the 9th lord is with strength as Venus is in the 9th while Jupiter is in an angle from the ascendant, the native's father is fortunate.

# 4. INDIGENT FATHER

If the 9th lord is debilitated while the 2nd or 4th from the 9th is occupied by Mars, the native's father is poor.

Notes: It is stated that Mars in the 10th or 12th from the ascendant (i.e. the 2nd or the 4th from the 9th)...





Brihat Parasara Hora Sastra

9th lord is in debilitation denotes poverty of wealth for the father. Even there be some the 10th/12th (not being in own house or in exaltation) make the native disinherit patrimony or enter into litigations. So to say, such patrimony will not come to the hands of the native, that too easily.

# 5. LONG LIVING FATHER.

Should the 9th lord be in exaltation while Venus is in angle from the ascendant and Jupiter in Navamsa from Ascendant, the native will enjoy a long-span life of the father.

# 6. ROYAL STATUS FOR FATHER.

If the 9th lord is in angle in aspect to Jupiter, the native's father will be endowed with conveyances or be equal to a king.

# 7. WEALTHY AND FAMOUS FATHER.

Should the lord of the 9th be in the 10th while the 10th lord being aspected by a benefic, the native's father will be very rich and famous.

# 8-9. VIRTUOUS AND DEVOTED TO FATHER.

Should Sun in deep exaltation be to the 9th lord in the 11th, the native will be virtuous, dear to the king and devoted to father. If the Sun is in a trine from the ascendant while the 9th lord is in conjunction with or in aspect to Jupiter, the native will be devoted to his father.

# 12. BEGGED

If the 10th lord and 3rd lord are both bereft of strength while the 9th lord is in fall or in combustion, the native will go begging for food.

Brihat Parasara Hora Sastra
COMBINATIONS FOR FATHER'S DEATH: The father of the native would have passed away prior to the birth if the Sun is in the 6th, 8th, or 12th in the 9th, the 12th lord is in the ascendant, and the 6th lord is in the 5th house. Should the Sun be in the 8th while the 8th lord is in the 9th, the native's father will pass away a year within birth. If the lord of the 12th is in the 9th while the 9th lord is in debilitation Navamsa, the native's father will face his end during the 3rd/16th year of the native. Death of father will occur in the 2nd or 12th year if the ascendant lord is in the 8th as the lord is with the Sun. Should Rahu be in the 8th from the 9th (i.e. 4th from the ascendant) as the Sun is in the 9th from the place, death of father will take place in the 16th/18th year of the native. If Saturn is in the 9th from the Sun as with Rahu, the native's father will die in the 7th or 19th year of the native. The native will lose his father in the 44th year if the 9th lord is in the 12th and the 12th lord is in the 9th. If the ascendant Moon is in the Sun's Navamsa, the native will lose his father in his 35th/41st year. One will lose his father in the 50th year if the lord of the 9th, Mars, is conjunct and Saturn. If the Sun is in the 7th from the 9th as Rahu is in the 7th from the 3rd (i.e. 9th from the ascendant).






# Chapter 20

If Saturn is in the 7th from the ascendant, the father will be fatal for the 6th or 25th year of the native. If the Sun is in the 2nd from Saturn (i.e. from the ascendant), the ages of 30, 21 or 26 will be fatal for the father. If the 9th lord is in debilitation while his dispositor is in the 9th, the native will lose his father at 26 or 30. Thus the astrologers may know the effects of the 9th house.

# 26. FORTUNES

One will enjoy abundant fortunes if Venus is in deep exaltation and be in the company of the 9th lord as Saturn is in the 3rd.

# 27-28. UNFORTUNATE PERIODS

Abundant fortunes will be acquired after the 20th year if the 9th lord is in an angle from the ascendant. Should Mercury be in his deep exaltation as the 9th lord is in the 9th itself, fortunes will be abundant earned after the 36th year.

# 29.

Should the ascendant lord be in the 9th as the 9th lord is in the ascendant, and Jupiter is in the 2nd, there will be gains of wealth and conveyances.

# 30. LACK OF FORTUNES

If Rahu is in the 9th from the ascendant, as his dispositor will be in the 8th from the ascendant and the 9th lord is in fall, the native will be devoid of fortunes.






# Brihat Parasara Hora Sastara

# 31. FOOD

By BEGGING; Should Saturn be in the 9th along with the Moon as the ascendant, the native will acquire food by begging.

# 32. Effects related to the 9th house

These are the effects explained briefly. I may further be estimated with the help of the state of the toros of the ascendant and 9th in other manners as well.

# 33. Effects of The Tenth House

I now explain the effects of the 10th house. Listen to these, O Maitreya, in the words of Brahma, Garga and others. Statements like "Brahma Gargadi Bhashitam," prove that sage Parasara had access to such expositions of Lord Brahma which would not be possible for mortals. The history of Parasara has been explained in the initial notes of ch. I supra and +t iof.

# 2. PATERNAL HAPPINESS

If the 10th lord is strong in exaltation or in own nusil*auamsa, the native will...





# Chapter 21

derive extreme paternal happiness, perform good deeds. will enjoy, fame and will

Notes: Though the word "Karma" means deed, it actually in the context of astrology denotes one's profession, job, livelihood etc. The 10th house rules one's paternal patrimony, happiness, last offices while the 9th house, as explained earlier, deals with one's father.

3. If the 10th lord is devoid of strength, the native will face obstructions in his work. If Rahu is in trine, he will perform religious sacrifices in an angle or in a trine, the native will perform this as Soma sacrifice deemed as a whole class of sacrificial ceremonies consisting of sixteen Vedic rites. The native will be extremely religious and meritorious.

4. If the 10th lord is with a benefic or be in an auspicious house, one will always gain through royal patronage in business. In a contrary situation, only opposite results come to pass.

Notes: Should the 10th lord be with a benefic or in a benefic's Rasi, the native will gain ever in his undertakings. The king (i.e. in his calling) means that if the 10th lord is with a malefic or in a malefic's Rasi, the native will be a loser in his calling and will not serve the king (i.e. person). The short and the long of the verse is to convey the idea that the 10th lord should be related to a benefic, happy, prosperous, and connections cause grief.




# Brihat Parasara Hora Sastra

5. Should the 10th and 11th be both occupied by malefics, the native will indulge only in bad deeds and will defile his own.

If the lord of the 10th is relegated to the 8th along with Rahu, the native will hate others, be a great fool and will do bad deeds.

Notes: The 8th house occupied by Rahu will spoil professional happiness of the native, as well as making him perform questionable deeds and incurring misconceptions with one and all.

6. If Mars is Saturn, and the 10th lord are in the 8th as the 7th lord with a malefic, the native will be fond of carnal pleasures and of filling his belly.

Notes: The effects for the combination described above are by the words "Parayana" (Sisnodara) as far as I understand, the meaning is as above.

7. Should the 10th lord be in exaltation and be in the company of Jupiter as the 9th lord is in the 10th, the native will be endowed with honour, wealth, and valour. One will lead a happy life if the 11th lord is in the 10th and the 10th lord is in the ascendant or if the lords of the 10th and 11th are conjunct.






# Cluptcr

in an angle. Should the 10th lord in strength be with Jupiter, native will doubtless obtain robes, and ornaments, happiness.

Should Rahu, Sun, Saturn and Mars be the native will incur cessation in the 11th, of his duties.

Notes: The 4 planets, viz, the Sun, Mars, Rahu and Saturn joining in the 11th house will ensure that the native not be successful in his performance. As a consequence, he will not have a happy calling or worth the name, and will gain nothing.

# 12.

One will be learned and wealthy if Jupiter is along with Venus while the ascendant lord is strong in Pisces and the Moon is in exaltation.

Notes: This means learning in the normal context. Apart, this denotes sacred knowledge derived from meditation, religion and philosophy which the seeker is taught how to understand his own nature and reunite with the Almighty avoiding reincarnation. This is (Gnana yogr). Jupiter and Venus joining in Pisces (the terminal house, denoting final emancipation) will endow the native with such supreme knowledge. The ascendant joining the exalted Moon renders the mind fertile enough to produce knowledge of one's own self.

For one cannot attain the Lord without first knowing what he is. Material wealth will also come to the native as a by-product of the planetary configuration in question. So one will be spiritually and materially wealthy.

# COMBINATIONS FOR FAME

One will be endowed with fame if the Moon is in the 10th while the 10th lord is strong and in relation to Jupiter. Fame will come to the native if the 10th lord is in the 9th and the ascendant lord is in the 10th and the 5th from the ascendant.

O excellent effects of the Brahmins, thus the effects of the 10th house have been told about in a brief manner. Other related effects can be guessed based on the relationship of the ascendant and of the lords of the 10th.

# Effects Of The Eleventh House

O excellent relating to the 11th house, I now explain the auspiciousness of which bhava make one happy at all times.

# Srlhat Parasora

# Eora Sastra

2. Should the 11th lord be in the 11th itself or be in an angle from the ascendant, there will be many gains. Similarly, if the 11th lord is exalted, though in combustion, the native will marry.

Notes: The second line of the above verse deserves proper approach. "Although in combustion having lost rays to the Sun". The word "gTfr", in this context means "although" otherwise possible as Navamsa interpretation "Sun's Rasi" which of course will be extreme rendering. To wit, the correct import is that even though the 11th lord is combust but be in exaltation the native will gain abundantly.

3. If the 11th lord is in the 2nd while the 2nd lord is in angle along with Jupiter, the gains will be great.

4. If the 11th lord is in the 3rd while the 11th is occupied by a benefic, the native will gain 2000 Nishkas.

Notes: "TTt" means the 11th bhava in the Bhava or house in question, i.e. the 2nd and not the 3rd. Since "Tri" already means "in house" will be redundant. (Nishka) though meaning a gold coin was generally taken to indicate Karsha or Suvarna also of 16 Mashas. This denotes certain weight of gold in the hoary days. The sage thus obviously hints at the opulence of the native quantifying in varied measures by the resultant Nishkas according to the merits of the planetary formations at birth.

# Chapter 23

# Effects Of The Twelfth House

O Brahmin, now I tell you about the effects of the 12th house. There will be good expenses on accounts if the lord is with a benefic, or be in own house or exalted. One will own beautiful houses endowed with superior scented articles and pleasures if the Moon happens to be exalted or be in own sign/Navamsa Rasi/Navamsa, or in the 11th/9th/5th. The said native will live with rich clothes, ornaments, learned and lordly.

And if the 12th lord is in the 6th/8th or be in enemy's debilitation Navamsa or in Navamsa, one will be devoid of happiness, will be troubled by expenses and deprived of general happiness. If he be in an angle/trine, the native will beget a spouse.






# Chapter 23

Just as these effects are derived from the ascendant regard in to the native, similar deductions can be made about co-born from the 3rd and other houses.

Notes: Hints given here are related to the native's horoscope effects to know from the native's example, brother's finances from the 4th (2nd house from the 3rd), marriage from the 9th (?th house from the 3rd), health from the 2nd (6th house from the 9th), mother's from the 9th from the 4th, wife's spending from the 6th house (i.e. 12th from the ?th) and so on so forth. Proceeding on these lines, we can see the possibility of predicting many important events for other relatives from the native's horoscope itself.

8. Planets placed in the visible half of the zodiac will give explicit results while the ones in the invisible half will yield potential results.

Notes: The visible half is the half of the zodiac of 180 degrees within a range from the ascendant's cusp seen backwards. The other half is invisible. A planet in the visible half of the zodiac will be more potent in effects while in the invisible half it is potential and less unmanifest.

9. If Rahu is in the 12th along with Mars, Saturn and Sun, the 12th native will go to hell. A similar effect will occur if the lord is with the Sun.

Notes: The 12th house relates to one's fate after death. Whether he will reincarnate, or attain the infernal region or the Feet of the Lord will have to be studied from the 12th house. In this connection, refer to ch.26 of Horasara also.

54. If the 5th lord is in the 6th, the native will obtain such loss to his enemies or will lose them, sons will be equal who purchased or will acquire an adopted son.

Parasara enunciates four different possibilities:

- 1. Obtaining enemies. The 5th lord indicates sons, the 9th lord signifies the class of enemy.
- 2. Loss of children from the 5th. Hence lose progeny as is the 2nd children it denotes.
- 3. Obtaining an adopted issue when one is unable to have living children. This is like adoption. Hence Point 2 above answers the circumstances.
- 4. Purchase of a child. The situation of the 5th lord in the 6th house is not very desirable, excepting Saturn for Virgo ascendant.

It is not advisable for a female to have her 9th lord in the 10th house from the point of view of filial happiness.

There will, however, be more daughters than sons, while the first child will be a male.

# Notes:

If the 6th lord is in the 2nd, the native will be adventurous, famous among his racemen, will live in foreign countries, be happy, be a skilful speaker and be interested in his own work. The native will further be skilful in dealing with hoary lore. His financial position will be somewhat shaky. He will enjoy good health.

# Notes:

If the 6th lord is in the 3rd, the native will be given anger, be bereft of courage, inimical to all of his co-born and will have disobedient servants. The 3rd house containing the 6th lord will not serve the native with intelligence at all times. To wit, he will be deprived of benefits due to his intelligence. He will also not be steady in disposition.

# Notes:

If the 6th lord is in the 4th, the native will be devoid of maternal happiness, be intelligent, be a talebearer, fickle-minded and very rich.





Brihat a Sastra
# Parasar llora

65. If the 6th lord is in the 5th, the native will have fluctuating finances. He will incur enmity with his sons and friends. He will be happy, selfish and kind.

# Notes:

His life span will also be considered from diseases. These are additional effects for the 6th lord in the 6th itself.

66. If the 6th lord is in the 6th, the native will have happiness but be mediocre in matters like wealth. The native will enjoy happiness.

# Notes:

His life span will also be considered from diseases. These are additional effects for the 6th lord in the 6th itself.

67. If the 6th lord is in the 7th, the native will be deprived of happiness through wedlock. He will be famous, wealthy, virtuous, adventurous, and honourable, but will be denying marital happiness.

# Notes:

The 7th house will dissatisfy the 6th lord's occupancy progeny. His own spouse will be his sworn enemy in the matter of happiness.

68. If the 6th lord is in the 8th, the native will be sickly, interested in others' wealth, and will desire purity of character. He will be inimical and impure (or degraded).

# Notes:

It is not good for the native to be ever occupied by the 6th lord. The 8th house will incur enmity on others' learning and wealth.






# Chapter 24

# 69.

If the 6th lord is in the 9th, the native will trade wood and stones (also means poison), and will have fluctuating professional fortunes.

Notes: The Maharshi seems to suggest that one in building construction will deal with the 6th lord in the 9th. It will further cause ups and downs in one's livelihood.

# 70.

If the 6th lord is in the 10th, the native will be known among his men, will not be respectfully disposed to his father and will be happy in foreign countries. He will be a gifted speaker.

Notes: One will be greatly valorous and learned in ancient lore. There will be litigations on account of ancestral properties. Dutifulness will also come to pass. These are in furtherance to the placement of the 6th lord in the 10th house.

# 71.

If the 6th lord is in the 11th, the native will gain wealth through his enemies, be virtuous, adventurous and somewhat bereft of progeny happiness.

Notes: One will, to some extent, be happy and yet be unhappy if the 6th lord occupies the 11th house. This is in regard to progeny. There is also a view that this can wholly deny acquisition of a child.

# 72.

If the 6th lord is in the 12th, the native will always spend on vices, be hostile to learned people and living beings. He will torture females as well.

Notes: The native will be of questionable morality and will ever be intent on deriving pleasure from females.





Hora Sastra
# 73. EFFECTS OF THE 7TH LORD IN VARIOUS HOUSES

If the lord is in the ascendant, the native will be afflicted by windy diseases, devoid of courage, and will go to others' wives. The native will not be firm in his actions. He will impart courage in words although he himself will be bereft of courage. So say learned astrologers occupied by the 7th lord.

# 74. If the 7th lord is in the 2nd

The native will gain wealth through his wife and many wives, which will further corrupt his character. This position will make one addicted to many women, leading to loss in marriage. His prosperity will ascend early.

# 75. If the 7th lord is in the 3rd

There will exist a great possibility of difficulty with the birth of children. Sometimes there is a possibility of a daughter being born. There is also a possibility of acquiring a son who will sustain (who will live long). Three salient features in regard to the placement of the 7th house are denoted by sage Parasara in general. Firstly, the possibility of having no children (rarely) and a daughter. Lastly, a happy child will live long while male children will pass away.






# Chapter 24

76. If the 7th lord is in the 4th, the wife will not be under his control. He will be fond of truth, intelligent and religious. He will suffer from dental diseases.

Notes: A disobedient wife follows the 7th lord. This is Mabarshi's instruction. However, Ramadayalu states in this context that the native's wife will brilliantly shine with devotion and chastity to husband. Lord Rama's sacred horoscope is a classic example having Cancer ascendant lord, in the 4th, of course with Saturn, the 7th even in exaltation. I do not possess the slightest competence to say that the Maharshi's view is untenable.

In this context, however, I quote a horoscope from "Saptarshi Nadi" (Volume Nadi was a product of intercourse between groups of four sages, each having seven great sages, in the presence of Parvati, a consort of Lord Siva. The benign ascendant on Taurus was also a participant. The horoscope (bearing No. 25 in the original volume) was analysed by Parasara himself as one of the seven Rishis in dialogue.

| Merc | Sun | Ven |

Brihat Hora Sastru

with the above horoscope, describes Parasara thus:

The native's spouse will be somewhat dark in complexion. She will be charming, intelligent, and modest. She will live free from any blemish (or Dosha). She will be fortunate, begetting fame from all the four directions. She will feed the needy. In beauty, she will be akin to Rathi, the spouse of Maha Vishnu.

She will possess many ornaments and will have a desire for other men. She will not question her spouse. This is how sage Parasara describes the native's wife in verses 27-29. Though the reason attributed for the chastity of the spouse cannot ignore the disposition of the 7th lord, the 7th lord is in the 4th.

The native giving a spouse who would be extremely devout is an asset proving the view of our sloka in regard to the present wife cannot be out of the control of the native. Thus, the edition states that the native's wife will not be chaste, and hence the version of our sloka is rightly interpreted.

Notes: I observed these are: (1) Delay in getting into married life proves seldom happy. The conjugal life will have disappointments or loss of children. (2) Severe affliction to the 5th house. The effects mentioned by the sage, viz. wealth, virtues, happiness, and honour will also come to pass. The progeny will visibly be absent.





Chapter 24

This great association will further rise to the native's people. He will be endowed with boosted spirits.

78. If the 7th lord is in the 6th, the native will beget a sickly wife, be inimical to her, given to anger and devoid of happiness.

Notes: The 7th lord in the 6th will reduce the general happiness of the native apart from severely inflicting poor health on his conjugal bliss. His wife will be weak in constitution. She will have adverse health conditions and will coalesce with harlots.

79. If the 7th lord is in the 7th, the native will be endowed with happiness through wife, only afflicted by windy diseases. The native will be courageous, skilful and intelligent.

Notes: By using the word "ii'qti" in the text meaning "only", the sage hints that the only defect in the 7th lord's placement will be troubles from windy diseases (like rheumatism, arthritis, etc.). One undesirable quality will, however, be found in the native, contrary to no adverse indication in the text, and that is his addiction to other females. This is an exception to Venus occupying the 7th house identically with Taurus or Libra.

80. If the 7th lord is in the 8th, the native will be deprived of marital happiness. His wife will be troubled by diseases, and will not obey the native.

Notes: As the 7th lord goes to the 8th house, the native will be liable to incur afflictions to her longevity. However, marriage may bring some pecuniary gains for the native.






Brihat Porssara Hora Sastra

81. If the 7th lord is in the 9th, the native will have many women, be well disposed to his own wife and will have many undertakings (or assignments).

82. If the 7th lord is in the 10th, the native will beget a wife, will be religious and endowed with wealth, disobedient tons etc.

83. If the 7th lord is in the 11th, the native will be endowed with less wealth and happiness from sons and will have daughters.

Notes: If the 7th lord is in the 11th house, there is a possibility of losing his children. He will obtain no happiness from his own sons. Living son also seems to be very remote. Probability.

84. If the 7th lord is in the 12th, the native will be a miser and will incur penury, his livelihood will be related to clothes.

85. EFFECTS OF THE 8TH LORD IN VARIOUS HOUSES (sloka 96): If the 8th lord is in the ascendant, the native will be devoid of physical felicity and will suffer from wounds. He will be hostile to gods and brahmins (or religious people).






# Chapter 24

If the 8th lord is in the 2nd, the native will be devoid of bodily vigour, and will not regain lost wealth.

If the 8th lord is in the 3rd, the native will be devoid of fraternal happiness, and devoid of servants and strength.

If the 8th lord is in the 4th, the child of its mother will be deprived of a house, lands and will doubtlessly betray happiness.

Maharshi Parasara uses the word "frR[" meaning that the native will lose his mother in the very childhood if the 8th lord is in the 4th house.

If the 8th lord is in the 5th, the native will be dull-witted, will have a limited number of children, be long-lived and wealthy.

Notes: One's financial acquisitions, though abundant, will not be steady and will be subjected to fluctuations. Though his actions and intentions will be bona fide, they will go unrecognized. He will not enjoy filial bliss.





Brihat Parasara
# 90.

If the 8th lord is in the 6th, the native will win over enemies, and during childhood will be afflicted by diseases and incur danger through snakes, water, and scorpions. The position of the 8th lord in the 6th house is a sureshot indication of success over enemies in litigations. However, this position is not very favourable for one's health. The native will be reduced to such calamities during childhood. Afterwards, he will be free from such dangers.

# 91.

If the 8th lord is in the 7th house, the native will have a malefic spouse. If the 8th lord is conjunct with the 7th lord, there will surely be difficulties in business and livelihood. The native will want for understanding between the spouse and will always be subjected to uncertainties. Outwardly, the native will be devoted to the Almighty. He will not be sincerely expert in stealing others' things.

# 92.

If the 8th lord is in the 8th, the native will be long-lived. If the said planet being weak in the 8th, the native will be blameworthy while the 8th lord should be strong in Shadbala. If he is bereft of strength, the native will not enjoy full span of life. The 8th house in occupation of its own lord will give a questionable spouse with character. However, she will be a source of financial help by her own earnings.





# Chapter 24

The native will inherit ancestral properties. The evil effects cited above will not come to pass for a native having Mercury in exaltation in Virgo. He should be within the first half of Virgo to stall the said evils. The later portion of Virgo his potence considerably decreases.

93. If the 8th lord is in the 9th, the native will betray his religion, be heterodox, will beget a wicked wife and will steal others' wealth. Notes: The native will suffer frequent misfortunes and downfalls. His prosperity will not be unobstructed and he will find it difficult to cope up with professional adversities. His father will suffer a cut in longevity. His understanding will be deficient. Progenic happiness will not come to him in full measure. His wife will be of "questionable birth". She will go to other men and progeny will be addicted to others' housewives. These are additional effects of a Gemini native, in a nativity. In case the 8th lord occupying the 9th house is Saturn, it will not produce these malefic effects. But his benefic tendencies will be quite meagre.

94. If the 8th lord is in the 10th, the native will be devoid of livelihood and be a tale-bearer. If there is an aspect from a benefic, then these evils will not mature. Notes: There is a school of thought to say that the 8th lord occupying the 9th house will cause the deaths of the native's parents. Apparently one right in parental placement of the 8th lord will produce all kinds of miseries in livelihood, fame, properties and like. According to Maharshi Parasara, if the 8th lord in the 10th is well related to a benefic, no evils will come to pass.



Brihat Parasara Hora Sasta

95. If the 8th lord along with a malefic is in the 11th, the native will be devoid of wealth and will be miserable but happy in boyhood later on. Should the 8th lord be in conjunction with a benefic and be in the 11th, the native will be long-lived.

Notes: The 8th lord in the 11th house, unless related particularly to a malefic, by conjunction, will not deprive the native of financial benefits. If he is alone in the 11th, he will not prove that bad in this respect. Moreover, for Taurus ascendant, Jupiter in the 11th house is not baneful. And for Scorpio ascendant, Mercury in the 11th will prove a highly favourable bargain in the matter of wealth, fame, knowledge, etc.

96. If the 8th lord is in the 12th, the native will spend on evil deeds and will incur a short life. More so, if there be a malefic in the said house.

97. EFFECTS OF THE 8TH LORD IN VARIOUS HOUSES (up to sloka this): If the 9th lord is in the ascendant, the native will be fortunate (or prosperous), will be honoured by the king, will be virtuous, dharmic, learned, honoured in public, and will hold a very high position which will bring him wealth and fame. He will be free from enemies. A female in a worthy position will prove a worthy housewife and be rid of afflictions from other sources. (These effects will not be enjoyed by a Scorpio native.)






# Chapter 24

98. If the 9th lord is in the 2nd, the native will be a scholar, dear to all, wealthy, sensuous and endowed with happiness from wife, sons etc.

99. If the 9th lord is in the 3rd, the native will be wealthy, virtuous and charming with fraternal allies.

100. If the 9th lord is in the 4th, the native will enjoy happiness, will have all kinds of wealth and be devoted to his mother.

101. If the 9th lord is in the 5th, the native will be endowed with prosperity, devoted to elders, bold, and learned.

102. If the 9th lord is in the 6th, the native will enjoy meagre prosperity, be devoid of happiness from material relatives and be always troubled by enemies.

103. If the 9th lord is in the 7th, the native will beget happiness after marriage, be virtuous, and famous. One will further be able to achieve success in all his undertakings. His prosperity will pick up after marriage. The native will be not well disposed to his father due to the additional effects of the 7th house placement of the 9th lord.







# Parasara Brihat Hora Sastra

If the lord is in 8th, the native will not be prosperous and will not enjoy happiness from his elder brother. Having the 9th lord relegated to the 8th house, he will be devoid of fortunes. He will face failures in all his undertakings. His father will primarily incur a cut in longevity. The native will be a source of miseries to his brothers/sisters. A blessing in disguise is probable with this position of patrimony by the native.

# Notes

If the 9th lord is in the 9th, the native will enjoy happiness and beauty with abundant virtues and fortunes from co-born. Should the 9th lord be in the 9th itself, the native will amass fraternal bliss. His co-born will own properties in large scale. He will achieve success in every undertaking. His father will play a significant role in his progress. The native's mother will be nurtured by his grand parents.

# 106.

If the 9th lord is in the 10th, the native will be a king or an army chief, equal to all. The sage suggests that the native will either be a minister or an army chief. Apparently, if the 9th lord is a prepotent one, one will enjoy royal status. The strength of the native will comparatively make lesser positions fall down.






# Chapter 24

107. If the 9th lord is in the 11th, the native will enjoy financial gains day by day, to be devoted to virtuous and meritorious acts. The native who has the 9th lord in the 11th house will see increasing fortunes. The 9th lord indicates one's prosperity and gains. Hence the said position is favourable for material upliftment. This will, however, not apply to Gemini ascendant having Saturn, the 9th lord, in the 11th house. On the contrary, it will prove highly detrimental for the native.

Additional effects due to the 9th lord's placement in the 11th house (excepting of course Gemini ascending), are spiritual high honours, success, metaphysical gains and achievements through father.

108. If the 9th lord is in the 12th, the native will incur loss and will always spend on auspicious acts and entertaining guests. The 9th lord in the 12th is said to cause loss on account of entertaining lavish parties. In the modern context, the native will land in financial difficulties on account of throwing parties and the position is not also auspicious for the happiness of elder brothers and sisters.

If the 12th lord is in the 12th, the native will have physical felicity, but will face heavy expenditure, and will be irritable and spiteful.

# MISCELLANEOUS

O Brahmin, those effects which are to be deduced considering the strengths and weaknesses of house lords are to be deducted based on their placements. In the case of a planet owning two bhavas, the results are to be deducted based on its two lordships. If contrary results thus indicated, will nullify, while results of varied nature will pass. The planet will yield effects according to its strength being full, medium, and negligible respectively. Thus I have told about the bhava effects due to lords in various bhavas.

Notes: We get important and key clues to analyze the effects of a lord placed in a certain bhava. Except the Sun and the Moon, the other planets own two bhavas each.






the case of the Sun the Moon, the results and cited will come pass. (Here also give due consideration to various other relative factors. Simply applying the checking pitfalls.)

When planet owns two signs, its placement in a certain bhava is affected by its two lordships. For example, take the case of Saturn in the 5th house for a Pisces native. His position as the 11th lord will give children and happiness through them. And as the 12th lord, he will deny progeny so that the native resorts to visiting shrines etc. in a bid to obtain progeny. In such a contrary situation the different results mentioned for Saturn's position in the 5th should not be declared straightaway but alternative sources (the significator of progeny) like Jupiter and the Moon should be looked upto.

Next we are clearly instructed in regard to results of different spheres. For example, again take the same case of Pisces ascendant having Saturn in the 5th house. Other results mentioned for the 11th lord being in the 5th house being: the native religious and happy. As the 12th lord in the 5th, the native will be devoid of education. After sorting out the controversy about it should be declared that Saturn in the 5th will deprive the native in Pisces ascendant of learning and make the native religious and happy (as due to 12th lordship).

# 68. ASPECTUAL EVALUATIONS

Deduct the longitude of the aspected planet (or house) from that of the aspecting planet. If the sum exceeds six signs (180 deg) deduct the sum again from 10 (or the latest signs 300 deg). Convert the sum into degrees and divide by two. The resultant product is Drishti and the resultant is Kona or aspectual angle. If the difference is in excess of 5 signs, ignore. Multiply the degrees value. If the difference is in excess of 4 signs deduct it from 5 signs (or 150 deg) and the resultant degree etc. become Drishti value. If the difference is in excess of 3 signs deduct it from 4 signs (or 120 degrees) halve the product to be increased by 30 to get Drishti value. If the difference is above 2 signs ignore and add 5 to the degrees etc. to get Drishti value. If it is in excess of one sign, ignore Rasis and divide etc. by 2 to get the degrees Drishti value.





Brihat parasara Hora Sastara

# 9.10. SPECIAL CONSIDERATION FOR SATURN'S ASPECTS

O Brahmin, if Saturn is the aspecting planet find the difference between him and the aspected planet; if the sum is above 1 sign, multiply the degrees (ignoring sign) by 2 to get Drishti value. If the sum is above nine signs, the degrees to elapse is doubled to get aspectual value. If this is above 2 signs, the degrees (in excess of 2 signs) be halved and deducted from 60. If the sum exceeds the degrees of signs, a figure of 30 to get Drishti value. In other cases, the sums processed be as explained earlier.

# 11. SPECIAL CONSIDERATION FOR MARS' ASPECTS

Deduct the longitude of Mars from that of the aspected planet. If the sum is 3 Rasis &#x26; c or 7 degrees (after ignoring Rasis) from 60. If it is above 2 Rasis, the degrees etc. be increased half of it (i.e. add 50% by signs, and superadd 15. If the sum is one Rupa is the value.

# 12. SPECIAL CONSIDERATION FOR JUPITER'S ASPECTS

Deduct the longitude of Jupiter from that of the aspected planet by him. If the resultant sum is 3 Rasis &#x26; c, halve the degrees (ignoring &#x26; c or Rasis) and increase it by 45. If the sum is 4 Rasis &#x26; c or Rasis, the degrees (ignoring &#x26; c, the Rasis) be subtracted from 60. This will be the aspectual value. The sum being in conformity with others than these be treated as stated earlier.

Notes: Throughout this chapter and others related to calculation of strengths of planets and houses, the term ..Virupa'





# Chapter 26

which 'Shashtiamsas' 'Kalas' has been used or 60 such units make Rupa. The planet that aspects is Drishti Graba. The planet that is aspected is known as Drisya Graha or the aspected. The longitude of 'the aspected' from that of the aspector is to be deducted. If the longitude of the aspected is lesser than that of the aspector, increase the longitude by 360 to facilitate deduction, which will yield aspectual Drishti or angle.

After finding out the 'Drishti' angles, the various quantities have been processed to be under the relevant principles:

1. When aspectual angle is between 30 and 60 degrees, reduce the resultant aspectual value by 30 to get aspectual angle and divide by 2.
2. If the aspectual angle is above 60 but below 90 degrees, reduce the aspectual value and add 15 to get aspectual value.
3. In case the aspectual angle is above 90 but less than 120 degrees, reduce the aspectual angle from 120, then increase by 30, to get aspectual value.
4. If the aspectual angle is between 120 and 150 degrees, reduce the angle of aspect from 150 to get aspectual value.
5. If the aspectual angle is between 150 and 180 degrees, reduce 150 from aspectual angle and double the resultant to get aspectual value.
6. When the aspectual angle is above 180 but below 300 degrees, deduct the aspectual angle from 300, halve the sum, to get aspectual value.

Needless to mention, there is no aspectual value if the angle is between 300 and 30 degrees.

For house in aspect, consider the cusp of the house akin to a planetary degree. In the case of aspects from Saturn, Mars and Jupiter, additions may be noted as a simple following formula.

A) Mars: When the aspect angle is 90-120 degrees, add 15 or 210-249 Virupas to the value obtained from the speculum.




# Grihat Parasara Eora Sastra

# B) Jupiter

When the aspect angle is 120-150 degrees or 240-270 degrees or increase

# C) Virupas

Saturn: When the aspect angle is 60-90 degrees or from 270-300 degrees or 45 Virupas to the value obtained without the speculum.

# Brihat parasara Hora Shastra

strength or Sthaanabah). Deduct from the longitude of the planet its (decp) debilitation point. If the sum is less than 6 signs, consider it as it is; if it exceeds 6 signs, deduct from 12 signs. The sum got to be converted into the same degrees and divided by 3 which is the planet's uchchabata etc.

Notes: These strengths are called Shadbala. These consist of the following:

1. Bala positional strength
2. Sthaana (or strength) Dig Bala directional strength
3. Kala Bala (Temporal strength) inclusive of Ayana Bala strength
4. Cheshta Bala (or motional strength)
5. Naisargika (or natural strength)
6. Drik Bala aspectual strength

These strengths are computed for the seven planets from the Sun to Saturn. The nodes are not considered. Firstly explained is sthaana Bara due to a planet's position. This comprises of the following considerations:

1. Uchcha (or Bala exaltation strength)
2. Sapta Rasi Bala strength accruing in Rasi, Hora, Dvadasamsa, Decanate, Saptamamsa, Navamsa, and Trimsamsa.
3. Ojhayugmarasiamsa (strength Bala acquired by placement in odd/even Rasi and in odd/even)
4. Kendradi Bala (due to placement in succedent or cadent house).
5. Drekkana Bala (due to placement in first, second, or third decanate of a sign).

In the present verses under comment, the sage explains the method to know the Uchchabala strength of a planet. To find out this, we need two things. Firstly the planet's longitude, secondly its debilitation point which is constant for all horoscopes. The deep debilitation points are noted on pp 38-39. For example, assume the Sun's placement in a given case is Pisces (or Libra 12° 15' 342° 15'). His deep debilitation point is 10° (or 190°). Hence:
