# 2-4. SAPTAVARGAJA BALA

If a planet is in its Moolatrikona Rasi, it gets 45 Virupas, in own Rasi 30 Virupas, friend's Rasi 20 Virupas, friend's Rasi 15 Virupas, neutral's Rasi 10 Virupas, enemy's Rasi 4 Virupas and in extreme Rasi for the enemy's 2 Virupas. Similarly those values occur in other 6 divisional occupations, Navamm, Hora, Decanate, Saptamamsa, Dvadasamsa and Trimsamsa. When all the Saptavargaja bala emerges.

Notes: Next step is to find out the Saptavargaja planet. The tables of various Vargas as well as of the planets, given the compound relationships are in the previous pages. The compound of two given planets, p. (including Hora lordship etc.) be seen in the vide i2 npra Rasi and not in the concerned divisional chart. Then chart only for each the strengths in Virupas of the Saptavargas which is then called saptavargaja bala of the planet.

# 4tr. OJHAYUGMARASIAMSA BALA

Each of Venus and the Moon in even Rasis and others in odd Rasis acquire quarter of Rupa (i.e. 15 Virupas). These are applicable to such Navamsas also.




# Brihat pdrasara Hom Sastra

Notes: Each of Jupiter, the Sun, Mars, Mercury and Saturn get 15 Virupas and the Moon get similar strength if they are placed in odd Rasis. Venus gets such strength in an even placement for in such odd or even Rasi/Navamsa.

The strengths acquired by Rasi positions and Navamsa be added together to know the Ojhayugmarasiamsa (Male planets get this strength in male Rasi/Navamsa. Female planets get such strength in female Rasi/Navamsa.)

5. KENDRADI BILA: A planet in an angle gets full strength while one in succedent gets half and the one in cadent gets a quarter (of Kendradi bala). Kendradi means angles etc. This denotes groups of four Rasis each. These are (i.e. angles, 1st, 4th, 7th and 10th) succedents, (i.e. 2nd, 5th, 8th and 11th) and (i.e. 3rd, 6th, 9th and 12th). The following are the Kendradi balas:

| (1) Planet in angle:     | 60 Virupas |
| ------------------------ | ---------- |
| (2) Planet in succedent: | 30 Virupas |
| (3) Planet in cadent:    | 15 Virupas |

6. DREKKANA BALA: Male, female and hermaphrodite planets get quarter strength respectively according to placements in the first, second and third decanates. This strength is acquired by a planet being in the 1st, 2nd or 3rd of a sign. Male planets are: the Sun, Jupiter, Venus and Mars, and female planets are the Moon and Mercury. Eunuch bodies are Drekkana. A bala of 15 Virupas will be acquired as under:

- Male planet in 1st Drekkana.
- Female planet in 2nd Drekkana.
- Eunuch planet in 3rd Drekkana.

For calculations of Drekkana, see Speculum supra. Needless to mention that if the Drekkana position is...





Chapter 27
other than what is required, then the strength on count This is strength also nil. This is called Linga (1) Bala. Balas acquired, viz. (2) Uchcha rgaja (3) Ojhayugmarasiamsa (4) bala, Saptava bala, Kendradi bala (5) Drekkana get and bala added together to all net Sthaana or positional strength. These are in Virupas and hence bc strength in Rupas.

# 7-71. DTGBALA OR DTRECTTONAL STRENGTH

(i.e. Deduct the 4th house Nadir) from the longitudes of Mars; the 7th house (i.e. descendant) and the Sun; (i.e. from that of Mercury; 10th house meridian) and Jupiter and Moon; and lastly from that of Venus the agcendant. If the sum is above 180 degrees deduct the sum either from 360. The sum so arrived in way be divided by 3 which will denote the Digbala of the planet.

As seen earlier, Jupiter and Mercury have this bala in the ascendant. Venus and the Moon have Digbata in the descendant 4th house. These strengths are full on the cusp of the respective house and nil on the cusp of the opposite planet. Hence note the degree on which it is bereft of directional strength. Deduct the cuspal strength from the former. If the product exceeds 180' deduct the same again from 360. The sum so arrived at be divided by 3, which will denote the Digbala of the planet in acquired Virupas. The powerful point is I Rupa when it is on its most, or 60 Virupas. For Saturn exactly on the 7th cusp gets I Rupa, examine degree gets zero Virupa and exactly on the ascending as directional strength.




# 8.9, KAALA BALA OR TEMPORAL STRENGTH

(upto sloka 17): Firstly NATHONNATHA BALA. Find out the difference between midnight and apparent birth time which is called Unnata. Deduct Unnata from 30 ghatis (rc). Double the Nata in ghatis which will indicate Natha bala identical for the Moon, Mars and Saturn. Deduct from 60 to know the Unnatha bala of the Sun, Venus, Mercury, irrespective of Jupiter and Nathonnatha (i.e. day and night, gets full Bala of I Rupa or 60 Virupas).

# Notes:

Kaala Bata (or temporal strength) comprises the following sub divisions:

1. Nathonnatha: (diurnal Bala and nocturnal strengths).
2. Paksha (Paksha: fortnight) Bala (strength).
3. Tribhaga Bala due to day/night being made in 3 parts.
4. Varsha-Masa-Dina-Hora Bala (Varsha: astrological year, Masa: month, Dina: week day and Hora: planetary hour).
5. Ayana (equinoctial Bala strength).
6. Yudhdha (strength due to partaking in planetary war).

Though Naisargika bala discussed in between this is an independent source of strength without reference to Kala bala. Firstly Nathonnatabala, Moon, Mars and Saturn get strength in the night. The Sun, Jupiter and Venus get strength in the daytime. The same Virupas of strength will be identically held by all the planets of each group. That the Sun's Nathonnata strength will be identically held by Jupiter and Venus. Similarly, in the other group.

# Formula:

Natha ghatis (apparent) x 2: Natha bala for Moon group. 50-Moon's Natha group gets Bala: Bala for Sun always 1 Rupa as Nathonnatha bala irrespective of birth being in day or night.

Another simple method is as follows:

Natha Bala: Birth time

Unnatha: 3 in degrees Minus 10 birth time in degrees.





Chapter 27
# Purpose

For this time at the rate of one degree per minute of time, or 15° per hour. This will convert the birth time into degrees.

# Paksha Bala

Deduct from the Moon's longitude that of the Sun. If the sum exceeds 6 signs, deduct the product so obtained into 12. The result will indicate the Paksha bala of benefic planets.

Paksha bala of each benefic should be deducted from 60 which will go to each malefic as follows:

| Notes:                  | Paksha                |
| ----------------------- | --------------------- |
| Pakshabala for benefic  | 60 minus Sun          |
| Paksha bala for malefic | benefic's Paksha bala |

Benefics form one group and each of them will get the figure of Paksha bala. (Mercury is to be treated as a malefic if he is conjunct a malefic. The Moon in dark half is a malefic if from 60 to 180, deduct if Moon-Sun is above or otherwise.)

# Tribhaaga Bala

One Rupa is obtained by one part of day time. Mercury (if birth is) in the first one third part of the day by Saturn in the second part of the day. Similarly, the Moon, and Mars get full strength in the last one third parts of the night. Jupiter gets this strength at all times.





Brihat Parasara Hora Sastra

Notes: This goes to one only, Jupiter, as I Rupa. However, the day duration or night duration of birth time must be divided by 3. With the table, Tribhaga bala can be known, according to the following:

| Being | 1st part of day   | 2nd part of day    | 3rd part of day   |
| ----- | ----------------- | ------------------ | ----------------- |
|       | 1 Rupa to Mercury | 1 Rupa to the Sun  |                   |
| In    | 1st part of night | 2nd part of night  | 3rd part of night |
|       | 1 Rupa to Saturn  | 1 Rupa to the Moon | 1 Rupa to Venus   |
|       | 1 Rupa to Mars    |                    |                   |

Thus, two planets will get I Rupa of Tribhaga bala. That is I Rupa to Jupiter and I Rupa to respective planets in other 5 whose birth occurs. The Tribhaga bala.

Notes: Under strengths, four different Virupas. These are:

| Order         | Lord | Virupas |
| ------------- | ---- | ------- |
| Varsha (year) | Lord | 15      |
| Masa (month)  | Lord | 30      |
| Dina (day)    | Lord | 45      |
| Hora (hour)   | Lord | 60      |

How to decide year is explained from Varsha lord: Astrological year is different from other measures. The day on which the astrological year begins can be found out from the Speculum abbreviated the p.272. To know the Varsha lord we should ascertain the number of days past from the beginning of Creation. This is a very tedious process hence we are concerned with the abbreviated Ahargana (or the number of days past from).





# Chapter 27

Creation). According to late Rev. Ebenezer Siddhanta Burgess, who translated Surya in English, as of January 1, 1960, the number of days from the beginning of Creation are 714,404,108.

To know the day on which the astrological birth took place, adopt the following formula. Divide the number of days from the day of Creation by 60. Reject remainder and multiply the post-multiplied product by 3. Increase by 1 and divide by 7. The remainder will indicate the week day on which the astrological year giving birth to the native opened. Sunday, indicates that birth took place on June 1, 1984.

Assume the number of Abbreviated Aharganas from the Speculum for January 0 as 65142. Add the number 1984, being the date of birth (inclusive of birth day) upto the date. Thus we get abbreviated days from creation to birth as 65295.

This product divided by 30 yields a quotient of 181. Remainder rejected. 181 multiplied by 3 gives 543. Increased by 1, this gives 544. When 544 is divided by 7, the remainder is 5. That is, the astrological year of birth for one born on June 1, 1984 began on a Thursday. Hence this strength goes to Jupiter, the ruler of Thursday.

Divide the same Ahargana by 30 and the quotient (devoid of remainder) passed to birth. The latest months from Creation completed be multiplied by 2 and increased by 1. The remainder indicates the month on which the birth month began. Continuing the same case, we divide 65295 by 30. The quotient is 2176. This sum multiplied by 2 increased by 1 denotes 4353. Dividing 4353 by 7, we get a remainder of 6 denoting the month of birth began on Friday. That is, Masa goes to Venus, the lord of Friday.

Though the week day of birth can be known from perpetual ephemeris or calendars, we better adopt the method which will confirm if the Ahargana is correct or is otherwise. The number of days followed as indicating Ahargana be divided by 7 and the remainder will indicate the week day of birth. In the example case 65295.



Brihat Parasara Hora Shastra

divided a remainder of 6. June 1, 1984

Friday. Hence the Ahargana followed by us is correct. While considering the birth should be treated from sunrise. Hence in this case, the Dina bala goes to Venus, ruler of the planetary hours. Each hour means parts divided into equal ghatikas. Horas from the Sun to Saturn. The first day is ruled by the lord of the 1st week day. The 2nd one is ruled by the lord of the 6th week day. The 3rd Hora is ruled from the first ruler. Similarly, it proceeds counted over the lord of that. Whichever planet rules the birth Hora gets the Hora himself. Horas are to be calculated for local mean time and not standard time of birth.

For reference, consult the Speculum of Horas infra. Vide

NAISARGIKA BALA:

14. (or and the resultant by 7 multiply Divide Rupa 60 Virupas) one will indicate the product which by I to 7 separately due to Saturn, Mars, Mercury, Jupiter, Venus, the Moon and the Sun, respectively.

| Rupas | Sun   | Moon  | Mars  | Mercury | Jupiter | Venus | Saturn |
| ----- | ----- | ----- | ----- | ------- | ------- | ----- | ------ |
|       | 0.857 | 0.286 | 0.429 | 0.571   | 0.714   | 0.143 |        |

This strength is acquired by a planet due to its luminosity. The brightest gets the highest Naisargika Bala while the least brightness is the darkest. The Sun is the brightest among the planets while Saturn is the darkest. This can be guessed from the above figures.

This is an independent strength for all nativities and for ever. Hence no individual has a significant use in Shadbala. If two planets are of equal Naisargika Bala, then the one with higher Shadbala prevails over the other.

# Brihat Parasara Hora Sastra

STRENGTH

# 18. MOTIONAL FOR SUN AND MOON:

The Cheshta (or motional strength) of the Sun's Ayana Bala will correspond to his Cheshta Bala. The Moon's Paksha Bala will itself be her Cheshta Bala.

Notes: For the Sun and Moon, there is no separate method of computation. The Sun's Ayana Bala (or motional strength) will be his Cheshta while the Moon's Bala is her Paksha.

For the other 5 planets, the method is described in slokas 24-25.

# 19. DRIG BALA (ASPECTUAL STRENGTH)

Drishti Pinda: Reduce the strength of a planet if a fourth malefic aspects one and add a fourth if it is aspected by a benefic. Super add the aspect of Mercury to the net strength of a planet.

Should there be a war between planets from Mars to Saturn, the victor's shadbala should be deducted and added to the Shadbala of the vanquished.

# 20. PLANETARY MOTIONS (MARS TO SATURN):

Eight kinds of motions are attributed to planets. These are Vakra.






# Chapter 27

Anuvakra (retrogression), (devoid of motion), Vikala (somewhat slower motion), Manda (slower than the previous motion), Sama (mentioned as faster than Manda), Chara (in motion against increasing motion). The sign in retrogression is due to such motions allotted strengths and 45, 30. 7.5, 30, 15' are: 60, 15, etc.

MOTIONAL STRENGTH FOR MARS ETC: Add together the mean and true longitudes of a planet and divide the sum from the Seeghrocha ori, by to,o. Reduces the product will indicate the resultant strength of the planet. The Rasi of the planet l2 signs from kendra.

Seeghra Kendra (or apogee) will denote the motional strength divided by 3 which will be converted into minutes and degrees. Thus there are six sources of strength: Drigbala, Cheshta, Kaalabala, nata OigUata, Bala.

Notes: Take the average between a planet's mean longitude and true longitude (i.e. Mars to Saturn). Deduct this from its cheshta Kendra. The product will be seeghrocha deduct again from 360 degrees. If tni exceeds 180 degrees, divide the Cheshta strength of the planet.







# Brihat Parqsara Hora Sastra

# 26-29

Thus I explained about the planetary strengths. Deduct the house from the bhava if the bhava happens to be in Gemini, Libra, Aquarius or the first half of Sagittarius. If Aries, Taurus, or first half Capricorn or the second half of Sagittarius happen to be the bhava, deduct 4th house from it. Should the Bhava be Cancer in Scorpio, deduct the ascendant from it and deduct the 10th house from the bhava happening to fall in Capricorn second half or Pisces.

Convert the product obtained into degrees etc. and divide by 3 to get the strength of the bhava. If the balance in the ascendant or descendant exceeds 6 signs, deduct it again before converting signs into degrees and dividing by 3. The division should be by a fourth if the bhava in question has a benefic on it. A malefic's aspect will entail one fourth reduction. If Jupiter or Mercury is a planet's aspect, add that strength aspected also. And the lord of that Bhava will be the net strength of that Bhava.

# SPECIAL RULES

# 30-31

The bhavas occupied by Jupiter and Mercury will each have an addition of 1 rupa while each of the Sun and Mars will suffer a reduction of 15 virupas to the bhavas. Birth happens to fall in Seershodaya if to be in day time, in dual (or common) Rasis if birth happens to be in twilight and falling in Prishtodaya Rasis if birth be in night.

If a planet has the required shadbala, it will favour the native by virtue of its strength. However, Saturn's extreme strength will prove long life as well as miseries.

# Notes

The minimum Shadbala requirements of the planets are under:

# 34-36.

Jupiter, Mercury and the Sun are strong if each of their Sthaana Bala, Digbala, Kaalabala, Cheshta Bala and Ayana Bala are respectively 165, 35, 50, 112 and 30 Virupas. The same required for the Moon and Venus are 133, 50, 30, 100 and 40. For Mars and Saturn these are 96, 30, 40, 67 and 20.

Even if the Shadbala is short of the sums stipulated in the previous two slokas, certain minimum strengths of the constituent will make the planet favourably purposeful, "ooiid.r- For this Jupiter, Mercury and the Sun.

39.40. ELIGIBILITY TO ISSUE FRUNFAL PREDICTIONS. O Maitreya, one who has achieved skill in industrious efforts in mathematics, grammar, justice, knowledge of geography, who is intelligent, has knowledge of space, one who has skilfully conquered time, one who is favourable to astrology, will doubtless be truthful.

# Balas And Kashta

Ishta

Now narrate the Dasa effects-good or bad-can be decided based on the planets.

1. EXALTATION RlyS: Deduct the planet's debilitation position from its actual position. If the sum exceeds 6 signs, the sum should then be increased from 12 signs. The degrees along with Rasis considered will indicate the Uchcha Rasmi of the planet.
2. CHESHTA RASMI: Cheshta Rasmi calculated from Cheshta Kendra similar to Uchcha computa- tions. The Cheshta Kendra for the Sun with Ayanamsa should be deducted from the Moon's Cheshta Kendra. If the Kendra is in excess of 6 signs; it is in Cheshta from 12 signs. Add 1 sign and multiply the degrees of the planet. This will indicate the Rasmi which Cheshta.





Brihat Parasora Hora Sastra

5. BENEFICIAL AND MALEFIC RAYS.. Add the Uchcha Rasmis and Cheshta Rasmis together and divide by two. The result will be auspicious (Subha Rasmis). Deduct to obtain inauspicious (or Asubha Rasmis).

6. ISHTA AND KASHTA (BENEFIC AND MALEFIC TENDENCIES) .. Reduce I from each of Cheshta Rasmi and Uchcha Rasmi. Then multiply the products by 10 and add together. Half of the sum will represent the Ishta phala (benefic tendency) of the planet. Reduce Ishta Phala from 60 to obtain the Kashta phala (malefic tendency).

7-9. ISHTA KASHTA SAPTAVARGAIA PHALA : 60, 22, 15, 1, 4, 2 and 30, 0, 45, are the Subhankas (or points) due to a planet's benefic placement in respect to exaltation, Moolatrikona, own sign, extreme friend's sign, equal's sign, enemy's sign, bitter enemy's sign, and debilitation sign. If Subhanka is deducted from Asubhanka (or Asubha Pankthi or points) 60, these inauspicious Vargas are halved.

10. A planet is considered auspicious in the first five places. In the sixth place it is equal, i.e. good. In other places, it is neither good nor bad. And in the three other places, it is inauspicious.

# II.I2. NATURE OF EFFECTS DAE TO DIGBALA

The directional strength of planet is itself representative of the effects due to the direction itself. Whatever is indicative of Digbala are the extent of auspicious effects obtained by a planet will be the strength. Deducting those figures on account of inauspiciousness is known. If the planet's strength is more in the case of Dasa and these will be auspicious. And are related to that Bhavas if converse inauspiciousness is predominant.

13.14. The various strengths (i.e. the other vargar multiplied by the planet's respective strength will indicate the auspiciousness or inauspicious aspect concerned. The Subha Pankthi will be known by multiplying the effects or inauspicious strength by the respective Pankthi.

# EFFECTS OF BHAYA

The strength of a Bhava and its lord have already been explained. The actual effects will be a combination of bhava strength and its lord's strength. If a benefic is in the bhava, there will be auspicious effects, and if a malefic is in the bhava, it will reverse the effects, i.e., add inauspicious effects. Similarly, if an auspicious planet is exalted or with such dignity, add auspicious effects. For debilitation, it is considered inauspicious and reduce auspicious effects. In AshtakaY4tg, add Bindus (points) and deduct inauspicious points. If a bhava extends to two Rasis, the rectification will be done per both the lords. In that case, whichever Rasi has more Bindus will yield more favourable results concerning that Bhava. If both the Rasis have more auspicious Bindus, take the average. Thus the auspicious and inauspicious effects of a bhava can be understood.

# Chapter 29

# 3. METHOD OF PADA CALCULATIONS

Brahmin, I shall now tell you about the Padas (or Arudhas) for the planets and bhavas as laid down by the earlier sages. The word "Pada" exclusively denotes the ascendant (or Lagna Pada). Jaimini (author of Poon'a Mimamsa) has dealt extensively with this system of astrology.

To work out the nativitiy as indicated below calling it the standard nativity, we shall consider:

# Chapter 29

In calculating the Arudhas for the various houses, we have to proceed as under. First of all we understand thus: the 12 Arudhas

| 1.  | l-a.gna (or Pada simply)  | Arudha of 1st house.  |
| --- | ------------------------- | --------------------- |
| 2.  | Dhana Pada                | Arudha of 2nd house.  |
| 3.  | (Bhratru) Vikrama Pada    | of 3rd house.         |
| 4.  | Matru (Sukha) Mantra Pada | Arudha of 4th house.  |
| 5.  | (or Putra) Roga Pada      | Arudha of 5th house.  |
| 6.  | (or Satru) Pada           | Arudha of 6th house.  |
| 7.  | Dara (Kalatra) Pada       | Arudha of 7th house.  |
| 8.  | Marana Pada               | Arudha of 8th house.  |
| 9.  | Pitru Pada                | of 8th house.         |
| 10. | Karma Pada                | Arudha of 9th house.  |
| 11. | Labha Pada                | Arudha of 10th house. |
| 12. | Vyaya Pada                | of 12th house.        |

In calculating the Arudha pada for a house; note the number of signs its lord moved away from that sign. Count so many signs from the lord in question. The sign arrived will be the Arudha for the sign under consideration.

In the standard nativity, Scorpio is the ascendant and its lord Mars is 9 signs away from the ascendant and its arrival is in Cancer.

# 5. SPECIAL EXCEPTIONS

The same house or the 7th from it does not become pada. The same house, the 10th its when the fails in pada. Similarly when the zth trecomes the of a house, from the originar house question ,a" an be treated paia.-ir as its ruler of a bhava be in the 4th from the bhava, th.o ;i"-;;; house occupied bc noted as.

Notes: In these two slokas, exceptions in calculating Arudhas are outlined. These are:

1. If the lord of a house Pada is in that very house, then the farts in that house is per thc exccption, itserf. l"',i"i- *r1, we have to count ten srgns get P-ada, For examplc, Sagittarius is certain Bhava ni"i"g lrpir* therein, with the pade having .fallen, in Sagittariri lili: Instead of trcating sagittarius as from sagittarius the Arudha, we count l0 signs and reach Jupiter having virgo. Thus virgo is the paaaili.
2. If the lord of b_hava is in its opposite house, then for the zth itserf becomes thEt pada Arubha. Instead ,rr"ri"g the 7th house ag Arudha, we have the said to count l0 signs from the zth house which wiil indicate Bhavainquestion as Arudha. For example, Aquarius ascendant having saturn in the 7th in Leo. countioj-io'it*; from Leo, we reach Taurus. Hence Taurus is tne iruOna ?oi Aquarius ascendant having Saturn in Leo.





# Chapter 29

3. If the lord of a bhava is in the 4th from the bhava, no counting is required. The house occupied by the lord (i.e, 4th from the bhava) itself is the Arudha. For example, Leo ascendant having the Sun is the 4th sign in Scorpio gets Scorpio as itself Arudha Lagna.

6-7. PADAS FOR PLANETS: Note the position of a planet and see how many signs away its position is its own sign with reference to count many sign and the resultant sign so sign from the said own planets. If a planet owns two Rasis or if a Rasi is owned by two planets, consider the stronger and declare effects accordingly.

Mtes: Here we are taught of what can be called as Graharudha or Arudha. From a perusal of the above verses, we can take it to mean that there are 9 planetary Arudhas. Since the sage uses owned planets obviously hints at co-rulership of Rahu and Ketu. Rahu is a co-ruler of Aquarius while Ketu shares ownership of Scorpio (Vide sloka 157, ch. 46 infra).

Assume that the Sun is in Capricorn. Counting from Leo we get 8 signs. Again from Leo we reach Pisces and count 8 signs for which is the Arudha for the Sun. The exceptions stated do not apply to Graharudhas.

In case of other planets (Mars to Saturn) then the counting planet's each owns two signs. Arudha in such a case is with reference to the stronger of the two signs. For deciding judgement one has to use his wise apart consulting hints in ch. 46. However, we do not have authentic information available as to how to use Graharudhas. Either we have to work on experience or keep silent on this issue. The literature available on Jaimini system is limited nothing more can be said about this.

# FORMATION OF ARGALA.

Maitreya, I explain to know definite effects of houses and planets.

Argala below (from or a planet) planets 4th, 2nd and the 11th a house iithe






# Erihat Parasara

# Eora Sastrd

Argala while obstructors of the Argala will be those in the 10th, 12th and 3rd. If the Argala planet causing is stronger than the obstructing one, the former will prevail. If the number of Argalas are more than the obstructing planets, then also the Argala will prevail. If there are 3 or more malefics in the 3rd, they will cause vipareeta (more effective intervention) which will also be harmless and be very favourable.

The 5th is an Argala place where the planet in the 9th will counteract Argala. As the nodes have retrograde motions, the Argalas and obstructions should be counted accordingly in a manner. Sages say that the Argala caused by one planet will yield limited effects, by two medium and more than two excellent effects. Argalas should be counted from a sign or a planet as the case may be. The Argala unobstructed will be fruitful while the duly obstructed will go astray. The Argala effects derived will be in the periods of the planet concerned.

Notes: 'Argala' in Sanskrit is figuratively used to denote impediment or obstruction. Argala is calculated from a house or from a planet. The 4th, 2nd and 11th house cause Argala (from for a bhava or a planet). A planet in the 10th (where the Argala is calculated) coming from the 4th will obstruct the Argala. Similarly, a planet in the 12th will counteract Argala emanating from the 2nd while the one in the 3rd will impede Argala from the 3rd. Some suggest that the Argala places are countable from the Argala places in the original place of the planet. This is not logical firm our findings.

Just as we mark the Gochara phases, let us have the Argala and their obstructions as under:

Now see a hypothetical geniture given on the next page for an easy grasp of the Argala scheme. The ascendant in the hypothetical chart is Aries. Mars in the 4th, Sun and Mercury in the 2nd, and Jupiter in the 11th cause Argala for the ascendant. (An Argala by benefic under 'subhargala' goes by the name and is deemed favourable. We will confine ourselves to the extent of Argala in simple terms.

# Chapter 32

# Planetary Karakatwas (Indications)

I now detail below the planets obtainable from the Sun to Saturn. Some say that Rahu will become a Karka when there is a state of similarity between (two) planets. Yet some say that the 8 planets including Rahu will have to be considered irrespective of such a state.




# Chapter 3

# 3-8. ATMA KARAKA DEFINED

Among the maximum number of degrees traversed, whichever has the sign called 'Atmakarka' If the degrees in a particular sign are identical, then the one with more minutes and if the arc is identical, then the one with higher seconds will have to be considered. In that case, three are called Madhyakarka, Anthyakaraka, and Upakheta.

Rahu, to be decided as above and as per further rules below. Out of these Karakas, Atmakaraka is the prime on the native just as the king is the head of all affairs.

# 12. IMPORTANCE OF ATMAKARAKA

Just as the minister cannot go against the king, the other Karakas such as Putrakaraka, Amalyakarka, etc., cannot predominate.






# Brihat Parasara llora Sastra

Atmakaraka in the affairs of the native. If the other karakas give adverse effects, Atmakaraka cannot be beneficial. Similarly, if other karakas are favourable, Atmakaraka cannot be malefic with their influences.

# KARAKAS

planet next to Atmakaraka. The term is called Amatyakaraka. Similarly, in terms of longitude, Bhratru karaka, Matru karaka, Putrakaraka, Streekaraka, and Gnati are inconstant significators. These chara karakas are considered identical. If Matrukaraka and Putrakaraka have the same longitude, both become a deficit of one karaka. In that case, the significator will be relative for the concerned influence of benefic/malefic karakas.

# Notes

A total of eight Chara significators are suggested as variable (highest longitude devoid of Rasis):

| 1. | Atma Karaka (next in longitude)                    |
| -- | -------------------------------------------------- |
| 2. | Amatya Karaka (next to Amatya in longitude)        |
| 3. | Bhratru Karaka (next in longitude)                 |
| 4. | Matru Karaka (next to Bhratru Karaka in longitude) |
| 5. | Pitru Karaka (next to Matru Karaka in longitude)   |
| 6. | Putra Karaka (next to Pitru Karaka in longitude)   |
| 7. | Gnati Karaka (next to Pitru Karaka in longitude)   |
| 8. | Stree Karaka (next to Gnati Karaka in longitude)   |





# Chapter 32

The sage also suggests a school of thought which only considers seven significators, treating Matru Karaka and Putra Karaka as identical. This section thus counts only seven Karakas. Since some advocate the use of added karakas, Rahu is also included in the planets traversed from Sun to Saturn. The degrees by Rahu should be counted from the end of the Rasi he is in. In the standard nativity (ch. 29) we take the following karaka planets into consideration.

| Karaka         | Planet   | Longitude |
| -------------- | -------- | --------- |
| Atmakaraka     | The Moon | 27°35'46" |
| Amatyakaraka   | Venus    | 27°17'50" |
| Bhratru Karaka | Jupiter  | 26°07'13" |
| Matru Karaka   | Rahu     | 22°22'54" |
| Pitru Karaka   | Mercury  | 14°54'13" |
| Putra Karaka   | The Sun  | 7°12'18"  |
| Gnati Karaka   | Mars     | 6°00'46"  |
| Dara Karaka    | Saturn   | 3°00'18"  |

If two planets have the same longitude identical to the second of arc, both of them will be qualified for that particular karakatwa or significatorship. In that case, there will be a shortage of planet for Dara Karakatwa. The constant indicator Venus should then be considered in the matter of marriage etc. under Dara Karaka.

# HOUSE SIGNIFICANCE:

I now narrate the significance of the houses. The first house denotes the soul.






# Chapter 25

self), the 2nd house wife, the 11th preborn, the 3rd younger brothers/sisters, the 5th progeny also and the 7th house said planet that a in the 5th becomes "ii": a karaka significators of the house in order are: the Sun, Jupiter, the Moon, Jupiter, Mars, Venus, Saturn, Jupiter. Jupiter and Saturn.

Notes: The karakatwas of each house are better signified in ch. II supra. The reader may consult the said chapter. Certain indications are additional in the present case. The significator of each bhava is enunciated above. For an easy grasp, these are:

1. The Sun 1st house (self, soul, constitution etc.)
2. Jupiter 2nd house (family, finance, wife etc.)
3. Mars 3rd house (courage, later-born etc.)
4. The Moon 4th (mother)
5. Jupiter 5th house (progeny)
6. Mars 6th house (enemies)
7. Venus 7th house (wife, conjugal bliss etc.)
8. Saturn 8th (longevity)
9. Jupiter 9th house (fortunes, religion etc.)
10. Mercury 10th (honour)
11. Jupiter 11th house (pre-born)
12. Saturn 12th house (expenditure)

Although we have stated the significators of the bhavas to be planets, certain bhava signifies more than what is stated above. In that case, the significator can also be different. For example, Jupiter is karaka for the 9th house which means fortunes. When the question of father arises from the 9th house, the significator is the Sun. Or take the case of the 12th house. The 12th house indicates final emancipation as well which for Saturn approach is not the indicator but Ketu. Thus a detailed significance through bhavas is required.

Effects of Karakamsa

O Brahmin, I now tell you about the effects of Karakamsa with Aries etc. identical occupied by the Atma is the Navamsa. The Atmakaraka is the one who traversed the 8 planets, from Sun to Rahu. These have been explained in the previous chapters.






# Chapter 33

Atmakaraka will be a nuisance from rats and cats. Should he be in Taurus Navamsa, further increase at all times. Should he be afflicted by itch etc. If in Gemini Navamsa, he will be in Cancer. If he be there, he will be from fear of water etc. If he be in Leo Navamsa, he will be from fear of fire etc. will cause itch, corpulence, will make trouble while in Libra Navamsa.

Atmakaraka will be one a trader and skilful in making robes. Scorpio Navamsa said will bring troubles from snakes etc. and also from affliction to mother's breasts. There is that by Atmakaraka. Navamsa occupied by Capricorn gains from water-dwelling beings, pearl, coral etc. If it is Aquarius Navamsa, the native will construct tanks etc. And in Pisces Navamsa, the Atmakaraka will grant final emancipation. A benefic's aspect will remove evils while that of a malefic will cause no good.





Brihat Parasara Hora Sastra

O Brahmin, if there be only benefics in the Karakamsa and the Navamsa of Lagna and be aspected by benefics, the native will undoubtedly become a king. Should the Karakamsa be occupied by malefics devoid of association, the native will be endowed with wealth and learning. The combination of benefic and malefic will yield mixed results. If the Upakheta (or upagraha, sloka 5 32) is in its exaltation sign, or own/friendly sign, and is devoid of malefic aspect, the native will go to heavens after death.

If the Atmakaraka is in the divisions of Venus, the native will go to others' wives. Otherwise, the contrary will prevail.





# Chapter 3t

# 13-18.

Brahmin, EFFECTS OF PLANETS IN KARAKAMSA:

If the Sun is in the Karakamsa, the native will be engaged in royal assignments. If the Moon Full is there, he will enjoy pleasures and be a scholar; more so if Venus is in Karakamsa. If Mars is in Karakamsa, he will use the weapon through fire and be an alchemist. Should Mercury be strong in Karakamsa, he will be skilful in arts and trading, and be intelligent and educated. Jupiter in Karakamsa denotes good acts, endowed with spiritualism and Vedic learning. One will be endowed with a longevity of 100 years, and will look after state affairs if Venus is in Karakamsa. Saturn in Karakamsa will give such livelihood as due to the native's family. Rahu in Karakamsa denotes a thief, a bowman, a machinery maker, and a doctor treating afflictions. If Ketu be in Karakamsa, one will deal with elephants and be a thief.

# RAHU-SUN IN KARAKAMSA:

Should Rahu and the Sun be in Karakamsa, there will be fear from snakes; if a benefic aspects the said combination, there will be no fear but a malefic aspects will bring death (through serpents). If Rahu occupy benefic Shadvargas, one being in Karakamsa, will be a doctor treating poisonous afflictions while the aspect from Mars on the said combination denotes that the native will burn either his own house or that of others. Instead of that of Mars, Mercury's aspect will not cause the said effects. If Rahu and the Sun be in Karakamsa and be in a malefic's sign aspect to Jupiter, one will burn neighbouring house while the aspect of Venus will not cause such an event.




# Brilat Parasara

# Sasna Hora

GALIKA IN KARAKAMSA

23-24. he Karakamsa-placed: Should the Full Moon aspect Gulika, the native will lose his wealth to thieves but is unaspected by others, one will administer poison or will himself die of poisoning. If Gulika is in Karakamsa in aspect to a malefic, one will suffer from diseases of ears. Ketu is in Karakamsa denotes one initiated into religions order. One will be severed ears.

25.29. EFFECTS OF ASPECTS ON KETU

Venus will be devoid of strength if Mercury and Saturn aspect. If Mercury and Venus aspect, with Saturn's aspect, he will be the son of a female slave or will perform penance or be a pseudo-ascetic. Venus aspecting the Sun together will make one serve the king. Thus, the effects are told briefly of Karakamsa.

O Brahmin,




# Chapter

# 30.3 EFFECTS OF THE 2ND FROM KARAKAMSA:

If the 2nd from Karakamsa falls in the divisions of Venus/Mars, wives will be addicted to others. If Venus or Mars is said 2nd, the tendency will prevail while an evil aspect of Venus/Mars will destroy wealth. If Ketu is in the said position, it will cause last death.

# 32. EFFECTS OF THE 3RD FROM KARAKAMSA:

A malefic in the 3rd from Karakamsa will make one timid, while a benefic will make one valorous.

# 33-35. EFFECTS OF THE 4TH FROM KARAKAMSA:

If the 4th from Karakamsa is occupied by Venus (or a large planet), the effect will be palatial buildings. One will own a house made of stones if the exalted planet in the 4th is Saturn. Mars and Ketu denote a house made of bricks, while Jupiter indicates a house made of grass. If the Sun and Moon be in the 4th from Karakamsa, one will have union with his wife in an uncomounded house.





Srihat Parasara Hora Sastra

If Rahu and Mars are in the 5th from Karakamsa, one will suffer from a pulmonary consumption, more so if the Moon aspects them. The aspect of Mars on the said house will bring boils or ulcers. Ketu's aspect on the said house will cause dysentery and said-diseases caused (impure) by water. If Rahu and Gurika be in the house there will be fear from mean people and poison. Should Mercury be in the said house, the native will be of the highest an-ascetic order or one hoarding the said staff. The sun and Mars in the house respectively denote one using a knife and Saturn denotes a bowman in this context. Rahu and Ketu in the said house respectively denote a machinist and a watch maker. Venus in the said house will make one eloquent, a poet and an speaker.

36.40. EFFECTS OF THE 5TH FROM KARAKAMSA:

41.45. EFFECTS OF KARAKAMSA AND THE 5TH THEREFROM: If Jupiter and the Moon are in Karakamsa or the 5th thereof, the native will be an author. Venus in the said house...






# Chapter 33

place will make one an ordinary writer while lesser Mercury will give effects still in this respect. Should Jupiter be alone in the house, one said will be a knower of everything, be versed in philosophy, a writer, and a grammarian. and Vedanta but not an oratorian or a logician, (follower of Mimamsa one of Hindu philosophy), of the six chief systems Sun Saturn one dull-witted in assembly, the a musician, (of sage Kapila enumerating 25 true principles on final bliss), with emphasis and versed in rhetorics singing, and Ketu or positions to the said will effectively pass. Some say that the Karakamsa will similarly be considered.

# 46. EFFECTS OF THE 6TH FROM KARAKAMSA:

If the 6th from Karakamsa is occupied by a malefic, the native will be indolent if benefic is there. The 3rd from Karakamsa.

# 47.48. EFFECTS OF THE 7TH FROM KARAKAMSA:

If the Moon and Jupiter are in the 7th from Karakamsa, the wife will be beautiful. Venus indicates a wife versed in arts. The Sun denotes a wife related to a higher age bracket, or a core while Saturn in this context will bring a pious/sick wife. Rahu denotes a widow in marriage.






# 49. EFFECTS OF THE 8TH FROM KARAKAMSA

A benefic planet owning Karakamsa will be long-lived while a malefic will reduce the life span. Aspect/conjunction of both benefics and malefics yield a medium span of life.

# 50.56. EFFECTS OF THE 9TH FROM KARAKAMSA

If 9th from Karakamsa is occupied by a benefic, the native is truthful, devoted to elders and attached to his own religion. If a malefic is so related, one will be attached to falsehood in boyhood.

If Saturn and Rahu are so related, one will be averse to learning. If Jupiter and the Sun are so related, one will betray his elders. Should Mars and Venus be joining six identical vargas, a female will die. Mercury related to the native will cause imprisonment due to association.

If Jupiter alone is related with a female by aspect or by conjunction, the native will be devoted to sensual enjoyments.






# Chapter 33

EFFECTS OF THE IOTH FROM KARAKAMSA :

If the 10th from Karakamsa is aspected or conjoined by a benefic, the native will have firm riches, be sagacious, intelligent. A malefic will cause harm and deprive him of bliss. Venus related to his profession will confer many gains in business and make him do many great deeds. The luminaries related to the 10th from Karakamsa if in aspect or conjunction with Jupiter will acquire a kingdom.

EFFECTS OF THE ILTH FROM KARAKAMSA :

If the 11th from Karakamsa is aspected by or conjunct a benefic, the native will enjoy happiness from coborn gaining apart from every malefic. If a malefic is in the said undertaking, the native will gain by questionable means, and be famous and valorous.






# Brihat Parasara Hora Sastra

# 336

If the 12th from Karakamsa has a benefic, the expenses on good account will be while a malefic will cause bad expenses. If the 12th be vacant then also good effects will follow. If there be a benefic planet in exaltation in the 12th from Karakamsa aspected or if Ketu is so placed and aspected by or conjunct a benefic one will attain heavens after final emancipation (from Karakamsa) if Ketu is in the 12th identical with Aries/Sagittarius aspected and is by a benefic.

If Ketu in the 12th from Karakamsa with aspect/conjunction of a malefic one will not attain final emancipation. If the Sun and Ketu are in the said 12th the native will worship Lord Siva. # Brihut Parasara

# Hora Sastra

If the Moon is in the Karakamsa in aspect to Venus, the native will be an alchemist and if in aspect to Mercury he will be a doctor capable of curing all diseases. If the Moon is in the 4th from Karakamsa and be in aspect afflicted to Venus, the native will be afflicted by white leprosy; if in aspect to Mars blood and bilious disorders, and if to Ketu black leprosy. Should Rahu and Mars be in the 4th or 5th from Karakamsa the native will suffer from pulmonary consumption and if there be Moon's aspect this affliction will be certain. Mars alone in the 4th/5th from Karakamsa will cause ulcers.

If Ketu be in the 4th or 5th from Karakamsa one will suffer from dysentery due to (impure) water. Rahu and Gulika in the 4th/5th from Karakamsa will make one a doctor curing poisonous afflictions or will cause troubles through poison. Should Saturn be alone in the 4th or 5th from Karakamsa, the native will be skilled in archery. Ketu lonely placed in the 4th/5th from Karakamsa will make one a maker of watches etc. Mercury so placed will make one an ascetic of the highest order holding staff. Rahu, Sun and Mars respectively denote a machinist, a knife user and spear/arrow user.

# 85-86.

The Moon and Jupiter in the Karakamsa or the 5th denotes a writer well-versed in all branches of learning. The grade of writership will comparatively descend in the case of Venus and further in the case of Mercury if so placed as above.





Chapter 33
PLANETS IN 5TH FROM KARAKAMSA: Should Venus in the 5th from Karakamsa, be eloquent poet. The native will be a poet, and be a Jupiter replacing denotes will be an exponent and be all-knowing but that he will be unable to speak in assembly. He will be a grammarian, a scholar further in Vedas and Upanishads. Saturn in this context will make one ineffective in an assembly, while Mercury will make one skilful in Meemamsa of the six chief Darsanas. Mars in Karakamsa or the 5th therefrom will make one Justice while Moon denotes a Sankhya Yogi, a rhetor or a singer. The Sun in the said 5th will make learned in music. Ketu in the said 5th will make one a mathematician skilled in astrology. Should Jupiter be related to the said Ketu, these learnings will be by inheritance. All these as well apply to the 2nd/3rd from Karakamsa and to the Karakamsa from applying to the 5th from Karakamsa itself.

Should Ketu be in the 2nd/3rd from Karakamsa, the native will be defective in speech, more so if a malefic Ketu above.

8. The summary of points 6 and 7 is: the 10th and 9th planets are benefic lords the highest while thus, the 11th and 8th lords are the most adverse. brihat Parasara Hora Sosta

NATURAL BENEFICS AND MALEFICS.. Jupiter and Venus are benefics while the Moon is mediocre. Mercury is neutral (i.e. a benefic when associated with a benefic and a malefic when related to a malefic). Malefics are the Sun, Saturn, and Mars. Full Moon, Mercury, Jupiter, and Venus are stronger in the ascending order. Weak Moon, the Sun, Saturn, and Mars are stronger in malefic disposition in the ascending order.

In revealing maleficence due to angular rulership, Moon, Mercury, Jupiter, and Venus are significant in the ascending order.

Notes: Jupiter and Venus are first rate benefics. The Moon is next to them. The Moon's variable dispositions have been given in the earlier pages. Mercury is neutral, i.e. in relation to a benefic and is a malefic in relation to a malefic. He has no disposition of his own. If he is alone, he will be favourable.

Considering the four planets in benefic classes, viz. Moon, Mercury, Jupiter, and Venus are superior in the ascending order. That is, Mercury is more beneficial than the Moon, Jupiter is more beneficial than Mercury, and Venus is the highest benefic. However, some exponents hold the view that Jupiter is the highest benefic.

As regards malefics, the Sun, Saturn, and Mars come under this class when the nodes are excluded for they do not have their own disposition. Here again, the Sun is the least malefic, Saturn is more malefic than the Sun, and Mars is the highest malefic against the Sun and Saturn.

# ANGULAR AND TRINAL LORDSHIPS:

If there be an exchange between an angular lord and a trinal lord, or if these...






# Chapter Two

Join lords in an angle or in a trine, or if a trinal lord is in angle or vice versa, or if there be full aspect between such them, they cause yoga.

One born in a voea will become a king and famous.

# Notes:

The permutations following will emerge from these two verses which will make the native famous giving status. These are:

1. Exchange between an angular lord and trinal lord. For example, ascendant having Mercury in Aquarius and Saturn in Virgo.
2. Angular lord and trinal lord in a trine, whether they own or not.
3. Angular lord and trinal lord in an angle, whether they own or not.
4. Trinal lord in an angle, whether he owns or not.
5. Angular lord in a trine, whether he owns or not.
6. Angular and trinal lord in mutual opposition (as is particularly good in bhavas).

If the planet and same gets an angle, the lordships of a trine will prove a yogakaraka. Specially.

# 19-22. &#x26; ARIES ASCENDANT

listen to these with examples. Even though Mars is the lord of the 8th, he will be helpful (other) to auspicious planets. Saturn, Mercury and Venus are malefics. Auspicious are Jupiter and the Sun. The mere conjunction of Saturn and Jupiter will not produce auspicious effects (although they own a trine angle). If Jupiter is at the disposal of a malefic, he will surely give inauspicious results. Venus is a direct (or independent) killer. Saturn etc. will also inflict death if associated with an adverse planet (i.e. Venus). That is how the effects will be derived by an Aries native.

# Notes

For Aries ascendant Mars is the ruler of the 8th. The ascendant is his Mooratrikona sign while the secondary sign. He will hence predominantly be favourable. He cannot be independently auspicious but can help another planet favourable like the Sun or Jupiter or even the Moon through good qualities. It is also not illogical to conclude that if Mars is well related to Jupiter or the Sun and is in good bhavas, favourable effects will come through him.




# Brihat Parasara Hora Sastra

The Moon's role is not discussed by the sage. The Moon will give mixed results according to association, angular etc. as she is an ruler.

# 3.6. NAMES OF NABHIASA YOGAS

Rajju, Musala and Nala yogas. The Dala yogas are Maala and Sarpa. The twenty Akriti yogas are: Geda, Sakata, Sringataka, Yupa, Vihanga, Hala, Vajra, Yava, Kamala, Sara, Sakthi, Danda, Nauka, Koota, Chatra, Vaapi, Chapa, Dhanushi (or Ardhachandra), Chakra and Samudra. The seven Sankhya yogas are Vallaki, Daama, Paasa, Kedara, Sooia, Yuga and Gola yogas. Thus these are 32 in total.

# 7. RAJJU, MaSALA AND NALA YOGAS

All the planets in movable signs cause Rajju yoga. All the planets in fixed signs cause Musala yoga. All the planets in dual signs cause Nala yoga.






# Chapter 35

If 3 angles are produced so yoga while malefics are placed by benefics Maala yogas will cause results.

11. GADA, SAKATA, YIHAGA, ANDYAVA YOGAS. If all the planets occupy angles, Sakata yoga occurs in the ascendant when all the planets are disposed to the 4th and the 10th house. If all planets confine in the 2nd, 6th and 11th or in the 4th, 8th and 12th, then Vihaga yoga occurs. All planets in the 3rd, 7th and 10th or all malefics in the ascendant cause Halayoga. Vajra yoga is caused by benefics in the 4th and 10th. In a contrary situation, all malefics in the 7th, 4th and the 10th generate yoga.

KAMALA AND VAPI YOGAS

12. Kamala yoga is produced. If all of them be in all the 4 angles, vapi yoga occurs in all the cadent houses or in all the succedent houses.

SAKTI AND DANDA YOGAS: If all the 7 planets are in the 4 houses commencing from the ascendant, they cause Yupa yoga. If a similar occupation commences.

from the 4th house yoga, and from the 5th house Sara from the 2nd house Sakthi yoga Danda are formed.

# 14. NAUKA, KOOTA, CHATRA AND CHA?A YOGAS:

The planets occupy the seven houses from the ascendant, Nauka yoga occurs. Koota yoga occurs when commencing houses the 4th, 5th and 10th. Here again the planets should occupy seven continuous houses.

# 15. CHAKRA AND SAMUDRA YOGAS:

If all the planets occupy six alternative signs commencing from the ascendant, Chakra yoga is formed. Samudra yoga is produced if they occupy similarly six alternative signs commencing from the 2nd from the ascendant.

# 16-17. SANKHYA YOGAS:

If all planets are in one sign, Gola yoga is formed. Similarly, if all are in 2 signs, yoga, 3 signs, Soola yoga, 6 signs, Kedara yoga, and 7 signs, Veena yoga is produced. None of these seven yogas will be operable if another yoga explained earlier is derivable.

# 18. EFFECTS OF NABHASA YOGAS (upto stoka 50)

RA.IIU YOGA.. One born in Rajiu yoga will be fond of wandering, charming, mischievous, and be cruel and will earn in foreign countries.






# Chapter 35

D. MASALA YOGA .

One born in Musala will be endowed with wealth etc., be dear to king, with honour, wisdom, be firm in disposition. He will have many famous sons.

20. NALA YOGA .

One born in Nala yoga will have uneven physique, be interested in accumulating money, very skilful, helpful to relatives, and charming.

21. MAALA YOGA .

One born in Maala will be happy, endowed with robes, conveyances, food and pleasures, with many females.

22. SARPA YOGA .

One born in Sarpa will be poor, cruel, miserable, will be crooked, and will depend on others for food and drinks.

23. GADA YOGA .

One born in Gada yoga will always make efforts to earn wealth, will perform sacrificial rites, be skilful in Sastras, and endowed with precious stones and gold.

24. SAKATA YOGA .

One born in Sakata will be foolish, ugly or afflicted by diseased nails.





Brihat Parasara Hora Sastra

will live pulling by carts, be poor and devoid of friends and relatives.

# 25. VIHAGA YOGA

One born in V haga will be a messenger, will live by sexual dealings, be shameless and interested in quarrels.

# 26. SRINGATAKA YOGA

One born in Sringaraka will be fond of quarrels and battles, be happy, dear to king, endowed with an auspicious wife, rich and will hate women.

# 27. HALA YOGA

One born in Hala yoga will be poor, miserable, given up by friends and relatives, be a farmer, be agitated, and be a servant.

# 28. VAJRA YOGA

One born in Vajra yoga will be happy in the beginning and at the end of life, be valorous, devoid of desires and fortunes, and be charming, inimical.

# 29. YAVA YOGA

One born in Yava yoga will observe fasts and other religious rules, will do auspicious acts, be charitable, obtain happiness, wealth and firm sons in his mid-life.






# Chapter 35

# 30. KAMALA YOGA

One born in Kamala yoga will be rich, virtuous, long-lived, very pure, famous, will perform hundreds of auspicious acts and be a king.

# 31. VAPI YOGA

One born in Vapi yoga will be capable of accumulating wealth, be endowed with lasting happiness, will have sons, and be free from eye afflictions and be a king.

# 32. YUPA YOGA

One born in Yupa yoga will be strong, interested in sacrificial rites, endowed with a wife, and be interested in fasts and other religious observations, and distinguished.

# 33. SARA YOGA

One born in Sata yoga will make a living through animals, will earn through arrows, will be mean, indulge in torture, and eat meat.

# 34. SAKTHI YOGA

One born in Sakthi yoga will be miserable, unsuccessful, mean, lazy, long-lived, and skilful in war, bereft of wealth, and auspicious.

# 35. DANDA YOGA

One born in Danda yoga will lose his wife, be indigent, unkind, serve away from his men, and be miserable.






# 364

# Brihat Parasara

# Hora Sastia

# 36. NAAKA YOGA

One born in Nauka yoga will derive his livelihood through water, be wealthy, famous, dirty and miserly, wicked, wretched.

# 37. KOOTA YOGA

One born in Koota yoga will be a head jail liar, will be poor, crafty, cruel and will live in hills and fortresses.

# 38. CHATRA YOGA

One born in Chatra yoga will help his own men, be kind, dear to kings, very intelligent, and be long-lived at the beginning and end of his happy life.

# 39. CHAPA YOGA

One born in Chapa yoga will be a liar, will protect secrets, be a thief, be fond of wandering in forests, and be devoid of luck and happy in the middle of his life.

# 40. ARDHA CHANDRA YOGA

One born in Ardha Chandra Yoga will lead a king, possess an army, will have a splendorous body, be dear to and endowed with gems, gold and ornaments.

# 41. CHAKRA YOGA

One born in Chakra yoga will be an emperor prostrating at the feet of the gem-studded diadems whose kings' heads will be adoring.






# Chapter 31

42. SAMUDRA YOGA .. One born in Samudra yoga will have many precious stones and abundant wealth, be well-disposed to people, and will have firm wealth and be endowed with pleasures.

43. VEENA YOGA .. One born in Veena yoga will be fond of songs, dance and musical instruments, wealthy and be a leader of men, be skilful, happy.

44. DAAMINI YOGA .. One born in Daamini yoga will be helpful to others, will have righteously earned wealth, be very famous, will have many sons and gems, be courageous and red-lettered.

45. PASA YOGA .. One born in pasa yoga will be liable to be imprisoned, be skilful in work, will talk much, be bereft of good qualities and will have many servants.

46. KEDARA YOGA .. One born in Kedara yoga will be useful to many, be an agriculturist, be truthful, happy, fickle-minded and wealthy.







# Brihat Parasara Eora Sastra

# 47. SOOLA YOGA

One born in Soola yoga will be sharp, indolent, prohibited, bereft of wealth, and famous be torturous, valiant, through war.

# 48. YUGA YOGA

One born in Yuga yoga will be heretic, devoid of wealth, be discarded by others, be devoid of mother virtues, and be devoid of sons.

# 49. GOLA YOGA

One born in Gola yoga will be strong, intelligent, wealthy, learning, and be devoid of dirty, sorrowful, and miserable results.

# Many Other Yogas

If there be a benefic yoga produced in the ascendant, while a malefic is therein.

# 1. BENEFIC &#x26; MALEFIC YOGAS





# Chapter 36

eruses yoga. Asubha similarly benefics in both the 2nd cause yoga. Subha Marefics also cause Asubha yoga. One eloquent, charming and virtuous while his counterpart will do sinful acts and will enjoy (or swallow) wealth.

Notes: Subha yoga is of two kinds. It can be a single benefic in the ascendant. It can also be formed by a benefic in the 2nd and by another simultaneously. Obviously, the latter subha is still superior. (Needless to mention that if the ascendant, 2nd and 12th, simultaneously occupied are by 3 benefics, then Subha yoga of extraordinary grandeur is established.) This gives physical beauty, virtues, excellent disposition. Though the text does mention additional effects: a happy life, health, wealth, longevity, fame, etc. These additional effects will not accrue by a single ordinary benefic in the ascendant. A malefic or malefics in these places will produce Asubha yoga or inauspicious yoga. As a result, each is inauspicious. The subject will be impudent, unethical and will indulge in sinful deeds and be capable of bracketting others' possessions. While a single malefic may not give bad results, two or three positions in such will produce most unfavorable results, apart from affecting health, longevity adversely.

Needless to mention that in analyzing the results due to good or bad combinations, one should take planet's strength, relations with other planets, the dignity, and many other factors into consideration. A yoga productive of expected good results can be nullified by other compensating malefic factors while a good yoga may not be effective when involved in adverse circumstances. For example, assume Mercury is in the 2nd house while Jupiter is in the 12th house. It will be detrimental to rush to the conclusion that the ascendant is surrounded by two benefics, and that subha yoga results will improve the native. Conversely, this is worse than Asubha yoga. Again take Asubha. Assume Virgo rises while Saturn is in exaltation in the 2nd and the Sun is in Leo in the...

# GAJAKESARI YOGA

Should Jupiter be in an angle from the ascendant or from the Moon, and conjunct (another) benefic, avoiding the inimical sign, Gajakesari yoga will be splendorous, born in Gaja Kesari yoga with many laudable virtues. The Parasari type of Gaja Kesari Yoga is constructed on a different footing. That Jupiter-Moon should be in mutual angles is normally accepted under this name.

In my opinion this kind of angularity cannot yield supreme effects. The case of Maha Purusha Yoga can better be known as Paricha Yoga. In other cases, specifically the name Kesari. In point of fact, the two need mutual angular placement called as the Moon-Jupiter angle.

Deepika, Ch' 6, sloka 14, vide Phala Yoga, Kesari simply states: "The native will destroy the band of hi-9 and will be a lofty speaker in an assembly. He will be lived and famous. He will serve a king. He will be intelligent."

There are two kinds of Gaja Kesari yogas mentioned therein. The first kind is formed by an angle from the Moon. This is the common type of yoga. The second type of yoga is: The Moon should be aspected by Mercury or Venus while the aspecting planet is free from debilitation and combustion.






# Chapter 36

# Kumara Swameeyin

stating that the Moon should be in Taurus, Pisces, Aquarius or Sagittarius. To wit, Gaja yoga is applicable only for four placements. That is, Jupiter should be in the 4th or in the 10th from the said Moon. This comes to pass when a constituent is in Taurus, Pisces, Aquarius or Sagittarius. While the Moon is in Taurus, Jupiter should be in Aquarius or vice versa. Alternatively, the Moon should be in Sagittarius while Jupiter is in Pisces, or vice versa. Please note that even the exaltation sign for Jupiter in Cancer is omitted which is making such a specific statement, the author of Kumara Swameeyin must obviously have possessed an unparalleled authority.

Then we come by C.G. Rajan to the Tamil translation of Parasara Hora. His version states that the Moon and Jupiter should be in mutual angles, but that the Moon should not be in the 5th from her, nor should she be in aspect to Mercury so that the Yoga obtained is not simultaneously annulled. Further, the Moon should be free from combustion and debilitation.

The Sanskrit edition of Parasara Hora of Sri Venkateswara Press, Bombay, has it in such a manner that Vaidyanatha of Jataka Parijata did take these verses from Parasara. (In fact, many of the Raja yogas given in our current chapter have been used by other works like Phala Deepika, Kumara Swameeyam, Parijata, Sata Manjari, Jataka etc.).

Coming back to Gaja yoga Kesari given by the Bombay series, we find that the Jupiter-Moon mutual angularity finds the first kind of yoga given in the version by Vaidyanatha while the second occurs in the Bombay series guise. It is stated there that Mercury aspecting the Moon, not placed in debilitation nor being combust causes yoga. In the second yoga, Venus and Jupiter are not given any yogas.

However, the two yogas given by Vaidyanatha and Parasara are exactly identical with the ones given in Prasad Pustaka Hora of Thakur Bhandar. The edition from Varanasi, Chaukambha edition does not differ from our version.





Brhat Parasara Sastra
# Hora

Thus; I have placed all the different versions of Gaja Kesari Yoga before the reader. Though the name does not deserve any special consideration as for yoga, I would give less importance to the mere angular positions of formations, other than Jupiter-Moon. We may understand that Raja Yoga will result in the following conditions in a given order.

1. As given in Kumarr Swameeyam.
2. As given in Chaukambha yoga edition and our edition.
3. The second kind of yoga given by Jataka Parijata.
4. The second kind of yoga given by Bombay edition of Parasara.

But, why should Mercury not aspect the Moon or be in the 5th from her? Contrarily, when Mercury and the Moon are in mutual angles, Mercury in the 5th from the Moon will be an impetus to rather than becoming an impediment.

Gaja Kesari yoga formed in any of the four manners will give wealth, fame, etc. in the Dasa related to them. There is also a thought that one born in Kesari yoga will be rich in the dasa of Venus.

AMALA YOGA: If there be exclusively a benefic in the 10th from the ascendant or the Moon, Amala yoga will exist. Amala yoga will confer lasting fame till the moon and stars exist and will make the native honoured by the king, enjoy pleasures, be charitable; fond of relatives, helpful to others, and virtuous.

Notes: The 10th house from the Moon or from the ascendant should contain a benefic and be without a malefic occupation. If a malefic joins in the 10th simultaneously, the efficacy of the yoga will be void. Amala Yoga gives name and fame and lasting for decades. Wealth is not.

# 7-8. PARVATA YOGA

Benefics or will Parvatha yoga, as the 7th and 8th are vacant, are occupied by only benefics. One born in Parvatha yoga will be wealthy, famous, charitable, learned, eloquent, and be the leader of a city.

Notes: This is formed in accord; according to different classical authors.

1. According to our version, there need be benefics in angles alone while the 7th and 8th are unoccupied. Then the yoga formed is known as Parvatha yoga.
2. The Tamil edition of Parasara (translated by C.G. Rajan) has this yoga in two manners: That is, benefics should be in angles and 6th and 8th. Alternatively, they should be in 9th angles.
3. The Sanskrit yoga is thus (1) As per our version. (2) The yoga in two forms again; in mutual angles and of the 12th and of the ascendant lords are exactly followed by friendly aspected planets.
4. Sata Yoga Manjari (English translation by Prof. B. S' Rao) puts it thus: The lord of ascendant should be in his own sign or in dispositor with an angle or a trine sign that is identical from the ascendant.
5. Coming thus: If the ascendant, planets in the 8th and 12th are unoccupied, while malefics remain occupied. There is no mention of benefics occurring.
6. This yoga has an identical version given by C.G. Rajan's edition.
7. The edition of Thakur Prasad describes this yoga per our version.

(p. 233)

# Jataka Fari$ts

It has two versions of this Yoga. The first one is formed in a manner identical with the Tamil Parasara Hora. The second is formed per the second series of Parasara Hora.

(1926 edition by Sastra Press) It has it as Yavanas by benefics. So: The ascendant, 7th and 10th angles are occupied by the 4th lord. Note that there are no pre-requisites. More varieties of Parvata Yoga are given by Yavanas.

Thus, when we consider the version in our text, the maturity of this yoga will be during the Dasa periods of the benefics in the angles.

9-10. KAHALA YOGA should occur in mutual angles while the 4th lord and Jupiter lord is strong, the 4th lord being in Kahala sign should be conjunct the 10th lord. In effect, the native will be energetic, adventurous, endowed with a complete army consisting of chariots, elephants, horses, infantry and will lord over a few villages.

Notes: This yoga is identically defined in the other three versions of Parasara Hora, viz. Venkateswara, Chaukamba and Thakur Prasad. The first type of Kahala yoga is formed when the angles of the ninth and fourth are in mutual strength. The second type of yoga mentioned by him is formed if the 4th lord is in his own sign or in exaltation or in conjunction with the 10th lord. The aspect of the 10th lord is an addition in the Tamil version whereas the conjunction is noted in our version. The native being foolish is noted.

The effects attributed by Mantreswara are: long life, prospering Moon, fame, and virtue like increasing leadership. These are comparable to what is generally stated for Chamara Yoga.

# MATSYA YOGA

Benefics in the 9th and mixed planets in the 5th and ascendant, malefics array of planets in the 4th and 8th - this at birth will produce yoga. In effect, the native will be an astrologer, Matsya be synonym of kindness, strong, beautiful, famous, learned, pious.

Note: While our version and that of Chaukambha mention that the ascendant and the 9th be occupied by benefic planets, the versions of Sri Venkateswara Press, Bhandar and Thakur Prasad Pustaka C. G. Rajan stipulate that malefics should not be in the ascendant and benefics should be in the ascendant and the 9th. Jitatr has the same view as by the latter group requiring that it is benefics that should be in the ascendant and the 9th is obviously correct as three groups are selected for this yoga, thus: Benefics in the first group, in the second group (i.e. malefics) and both mixed in the 3rd group.

# 31-32. KALANIDHI YOGA

Should Jupiter be in the 2nd or the 5th and be aspected by Mercury and Venus, Kalanidhi yoga is caused. In effect, the native will be virtuous, honoured by kings, bereft of diseases, happy, wealthy and learned.

# 33-34. KALPADRUMA YOGA

Note the following four planets: (a) the ascendant lord, (b) the dispositor of the ascendant lord, (c) the dispositor of the Navamsa planet at the ascendant, (d) the dispositor of the planet at "c". If all these are disposed in angles and trines from the ascendant, Kalpa Druma yoga exists. Ong with this yoga will be endowed with all kinds of wealth, be a king, pious, strong, fond of war and merciful.

Notes: Kalpa Druma yoga is also known as Parijata Yoga. Kalpa Druma denotes the Celestial Tree while Parijata denotes the Celestial Flower. Both of these are known to grant any boon to the possessor who is said to be Devendra, the god of gods. In the obtainment of yoga, there are four participants. # Kalpa Druma Yoga

The Now see how Kalpa Druma yoga is formed in the chart.

# Constituents of the Yoga

1. The ascendant lord
2. The Moon.
3. Jupiter is in own sign Sagittarius and hence
4. Jupiter's Navamsa dispositor is in Sagittarius no dispositor.

All the above are in a trine from the natal ascendant who clearly form Karpa'druma yoga. The effects were obtained by the sage Tilak, including fondness for foreign rule.

# Trimurthi Yogas

Counted from the 2nd lord if benefics occupy the 2nd, 12th and 8th, Hari yoga is obtainable. If the 4th, 9th and 8th with reference to the 7th lord are occupied by benefics, Hara yoga is generated.

One born in anyone of the said yogas will be learned and endowed with wealth and sons.

# Notes

There are actually three yogas given in different verses. These are Hari Yoga, Hara Yoga, and Brahma Yoga. This represents the trinity of Hindu Gods jointly, hence is known as Trimurthi yogas.

Some interpret this as one yoga knowing it as 'Hariharabrahma yoga' however this is incorrect. For formation of Hari Yoga the 2nd lord's position is to be noted firstly. From the said position of the 2nd lord, each of the 2nd, 12th and 8th be occupied by benefics.

See the chart on the next page.

35-36.




# Chapter 36

In the above case, 2nd lord is Saturn. Note from Saturn, 2nd is occupied by Venus, 12th by Mercury and the 8th by Jupiter.

The second yoga is Hara Yoga (Hara denotes lord Sive.) See the chart for an easy fulfilling the conditions laid down by Parasara.




# Brihai parasara Hora Sastra

In the above case, Saturn rules the 7th house placed in Pisces. From him the 4th, 9th and 10th are respectively occupied by Jupiter, Venus and Mercury. Thus lastly Brahma yoga. This is formed if the 4th, 10th and 11th from the sign occupied by the ascendant tenant are benefics.

Note this yoga from the following:

# Chapter 36

# LAGNADHI YOGA

Should benefics be counted in the 8th from the ascendant conjunction/aspect and be devoid of malefics, Lagnadhi yoga is produced making one a great learned person, happy.

Notes: Sage Parasara does not include the 6th house for Lagnadhi yoga. Only two houses are suggested, viz. the 7th and 8th from the ascendant. This is so given in the versions of Chaukamba, Sri Venkateswara Press, Thakur Prasad Bhandara and C G. Rajan as well. The last three versions have an additional condition that the 4th house from the ascendant should at the same time be vacant. In Chandradhi yoga, the sage has included the 6th house, see infra, after a study of the various texts, we can conclude to the following effect: The 6th, 7th and 8th houses be occupied by benefics in any manner, i.e. the three benefics, Mercury and Venus may be disposed in one, viz, Jupiter, in 6th, 7th and 8th. No other malefic should be in these houses nor aspect the occupants. The 4th from the ascendant or from the Moon, as the case may be, should remain unoccupied. Then Adhi yoga is obtained. The benefics mentioned should also be free from combustion and debilitation. If the yoga is formed in the above conditions, the native will be highly wealthy and be among the most supreme men on the earth. The best Adhi yoga is, however, with Mercury in the 6th, Jupiter in the 7th and Venus in the 8th house.

ADHI YOGA FROM THE MOON: If benefics occupy the 8th, 6th and 2nd counted from the Moon, Adhi yoga obtains. According to the strength of the participating planets, the native concerned will be either a king or a minister or an army chief.

DHANA YOGA: Should all benefics be in Upachaya (i.e. counted from the 3rd, 6th, 10th), two benefics from the Moon, one will be very affluent; with regard to wealth. If a single benefic is there, the wealth will be medium to negligible.

# 7.10, SUNAPHA, ANAPHA AND DURADHARA:

If the planet, Sun, is the 2nd from the Moon, there is a yoga with other planets in both the 12th and 2nd places. Sunapha yoga and Anapha yoga are caused. One born with Sunapha yoga will be endowed with intelligence, a king or equal to a king. One born in Anapha yoga will enjoy wealth, fame, self-earned wealth, and will be famous, charming, virtuous, free from diseases, and happy. One born in Duradhara yoga will enjoy pleasures, and will be charitable and endowed with excellent conveyances and force.

Excluding the Sun, there should be no planet with the Moon or in an angle from the Moon or in the 2nd/12th from the ascendant, Kemadruma yoga is formed. One born in Kemadruma yoga will be much reproached, be bereft of intelligence and learning and reduced to penury and perils.

Chapter 39

Next take the natal ascendant lord and the 5th lord from the natal ascendant. In assessing the strength to the natal ascendant, the strength and relationship between these two lords should be correctly understood. Their Vimsopaka strengths are respectively 16.45 and 16.60 making them extremely well disposed to cause yoga in the horoscope. Hence it is apparent that the sage correlates Putra Karaka with the Karakamsa (or the Chara Atmakaraka) and the 5th lord from natal ascendant with the natal ascendant itself.

# 6-7 MAHA RAJA YOGA

Notes: An exchange between the 5th lord and the ascendant lord will bestow a supreme Raja yoga on the native. For example, in the case of a Pisces-born, and the Moon in the ascendant, Jupiter in the 5th (Chara).

In the second stage, the Atma Karaka and Putra Karaka are brought in the picture. They can jointly be in the 5th in the ascendant (or in Karakamsa Lagna and the 5th from there) or separately both of them should be in their respective exaltation signs, or in own signs, or in own Navamsas and related to a benefic. # Chapter 39

Again, I now tell you of the Raja yogas based on the planets and conjunctions with different dignities and aspects of the planets.

The 9th lord is akin to a minister, and more if two planets aspect, especially the 5th lord. Even if these two are conjunct in any house, the native will obtain a kingdom. If the 10th lord is in aspect to the 4th and the 10th and the 5th and 9th lords.

If lords join the one of the 5th, 10th, 4th and the ascendant in the 9th, the native will become a ruler with fame spreading over the four directions.

Should the lord of the 4th or of the 10th join either the 5th lord or the 9th lord, the native will obtain a kingdom.





Brihat parasara Hora Sastra
Notes: There are four yogas mentioned in the above verse which can be understood as under:

1. 4th lord joining the 5th lord.
2. 4th lord joining the 9th lord.
3. 10th lord joining the 9th lord.
4. 10th lord joining the 5th lord.

It will be still superior if the 4th lord joins both the 5th and the 9th lord, or if the 10th lord joins the 5th and the 9th lord. It may be noted that this is a yoga caused by an angular lord.

If the 5th lord is in the ascendant, the native will become king in the company of the 9th lord or of the 10th lord.

Should Jupiter be in his sign identical with the 9th house and be in the company of either Venus or of the 5th lord, the native will obtain kingship.

Two and half ghatis (i.e. 60 minutes of time) from mid-day or from mid-night is auspicious time. A birth during an auspicious time will cause one to be a king or equal to him.

Notes: Though mid-day and mid-night are denoted in translation for Dinardha and Nisardha, a clarification is essential in regard to the implications of these. Mid-day simply denotes 12 Noon while mid-night denotes zero hour as per common use. But what the sage implies is somewhat different. Dinardha means half of the day while Nisardha means half of the night, keeping the Sun in mind and Sun's place. The verse has a yoga to indicate that if there is a birth at a given time when the Sun has set.





Chapter 39

within an hour of the said Dinardha or Nisardha, will be the native a king. I shall illustrate this with a practical case. Take for instance a birth on 15th February 1947 at E 2 and 26 N 19. The local sun rise is at 0639 and sun set at 1749 hrs. Hence for this latitude the day duration is 11h 11m and night duration 12h 49m, Divide the day duration by two to get Dinardha which is 5h 35m. Similarly dividing night duration by 2 get as 6h 24m. Add 5h 35m to sun rise which will give half the day duration. Thus by adding 5h 35m to 12h 13m, we get 13h 19m, we get of night, the night duration halved and the figure arrived at is to be added to sun set. Thus we get 0h 13m (i.e. 13m later than the usual mid-night).

From the above we may understand that by simply taking 12 noon as mid-day and hour 0 as mid-night it will serve no purpose in the context of the yoga suggested by the sage. Need to mention that LMT is to be used for these calculations. Uttara Kslanrita has two yogas in this respect, viz. Koteeswara and Lakshadhikari yoga (vide crr 4, sroka 30;).

According to its author if there be a birth within 2 (i.e. 4E minutes as against parasara's mention of 60 minutes) Dinardha and Nisardha, a king is born who will conquer his enemies and observe religious rules of conduct and be further learned. He adds that if in the said case an exalted planet is in the 2nd house, in aspect to another exalted planet, a Koteeswara is born. If the planet aspecting is in its own house (instead of being in exaltation) the native will then be only a Lakshadhikari. Suffice it to say that there will be relatively less riches in the second case.

Should the Moon and Venus be mutually in the 3rd and 11th and be in aspects, a Raja yoga is obtained. Notes: As the sloka question, we find two conditions under which the Moon and Venus form two Raja yogas. In the first instance they should be in mutually 3 and 11.





Brihat Parasara Hora Sastra

In the second instance, Moon and Venus can be mutually aspect where many standard texts. This type of yoga is found in Vargothamsa.
