While the four angular lords are treated in one and the same breath, the sage gives special importance to the 9th lords individually. The effects may suitably be based on the given explanations for angular lords above.

# EFFECTS OF 9th LORD's DIVINATIONAL DIGNITIES

If parijatamsa, the 9th lord is in the native places, will visit holy if in Uttamamsa well, if in Gopuramsa he had done so in the past births as he will perform sacrificial rites, he will be in simhasanamsa mighty, truthful, be a conquerer and will concentrate only on the Supreme giving up all religions, if in Paaravatamsa he will be the greatest of ascetics, if in Devalokamsa he will be an ascetic or a religious holding a "udgei (qTS) mendicant that has renounced attachments all mundane and carrying three long staves tied together right hand (filEfq) if in Brahmalokamsa he will perform yaga (Horse Aswamedha sacrifice,) and will attain the state of Lord Indra (god of gods). If the 9th lord is in lravatamsa of person born will be Sri Rama a synonym of Dharma or virtues just as Yudhishtira (the eldest of pandavas).





# Chapter 4l

Notes: The 5th lord has been in spiritual and material planes as well. Whereas the 9th lord is solely related to one's spiritual achievements as could be seen by Maharshi Parasara by the treatment given in the above 5 slokas.

The word Tridandi has been translated as above in the context of relating the native to a Sansyasi as these slokas concentrate on the spiritual achievements of the native. 'Tridandi' also means one who obtained command over speech, mind, and deed. Without these three things, it will not be possible for one to achieve bliss. One who had good in his mind though in the other two spheres, viz. speech and actions cannot be called one of good character. One who thinks and speaks similarly but acts in a contrary manner cannot be a successful spiritualist.

Lastly, one who speaks undesirable words though good in thinking cannot also reach self-realisation. Hence it is evident that one should be a 'Tridandi' or endowed with Trikarana Suddhi, that he locates the Almighty at every point of space and time.

We have so far seen that 5th and 9th lords primarily are wealth givers. The sage also denotes the 5th and 9th lords as lords of 'Lakshmi' though normally means splendour. It relates to divine splendour acquired by a person through his merits. If a person is splendorous, we see in him what is called Brahma Varchas or the splendour of God, free from any material attachment. One cannot but recall great personages in this context like Hamsa, Maharshi Rama Krishna, Ramana, Sankaracharyas of various periods, Sivananda and so on. In all cases, the 5th and 9th lords enabled them to earn that splendour. The wealth they earned is such that it cannot be exhausted even after many centuries, i.e. divine status.

# 28. ANGULAR AND TRINAL LORDS RELATED:

The known angles are called Vishnusthaana (i.e. houses of Lord Vishnu) while the trines are called Lakshmi sthaanas.



Brihat Porasara Hora Shastra
If the lord of an angle establishes relationship with a trinal lord, Rajayoga will obtain.

# Notes

The 4 houses, viz. known as the 1st, 4th, 7th and 10th are Vishnusthaanas while the 5th and 9th are Lakshmisthaanas.

In Hindu mythology, Lakshmi is a consort of Lord Vishnu, thus having a relationship between an angular supreme lord and a trinal lord of causing Rajayoga, is capable of bestowing the blessings of Sri Vishnu and His consort Lakshmi with permanent wellbeing.

# The kinds of relationship that will be favourable are:

1. An exchange between these two lords.
2.
Mutual placement existing between these two.
3. Mutual trinal placement between these two.
4.

The first three kinds of relationships are powerful while the last two cannot be equally powerful but in a lesser degree.

A sixth kind of relationship can also be extended to Navamsa positions in this context though I have no specific classic sanction for this.

For example, in a Capricornian's case, Mars of Venus in the Navamsa and Venus in that of Mars will confer a superior Raja yoga. This form of relationship will be equally powerful like the 3 relationships mentioned earlier by me in the following paragraph.

After seeing such a relationship between an angular lord, their dignities and a trinal lord like Parijata etc. will have to be decided as could be seen in the six verses.

Notes: The two planets, viz. an angular lord and a trinal lord with such a relationship, should be simultaneously in Parijatamsa and the other in a still higher Amsa. The reader can intelligently manipulate these Am'sas according to such slokas, studying the effects.

When we reach the period of Parasara, there are baseless arguments that the author of Brihrit Parasara, Parasara, could not have lived thousands of years ago; but a very recent author that lived after Varaha Mihira, should be on and so forth. This misconception does not hold.






# Brihat Parasara Hora Sastra

deserve an answer at all and is worth being brushed aside as idle gossip. The holders of such opinion may advance million arguments in their own favour. That conveys that Parasara was a predecessor of Salivahana and not Bhattotpala, Maharshi etc. Jaimini, author of Poorva Mimamsa and propagator of Astrology was a disciple of Parasara.

If Parasara lived in the 17th century, what about Jaimini? This is an ample proof that our sage was parent in Maha Bharata time and was the illustrious Vyasa.

# Chapter 42

# For Periury Combinations

1. O Lord, you have stated such yogas to acquire wealth. Please tell me about such yogas causing utter poverty.

2. The native will be penniless if the ascendant lord is in the 12th while the 12th lord is in the ascendant along with a Maraka planet inflicting death or be in aspect to such a planet.

3. The native will be penniless if the ascendant lord is in the 6th while the 6th lord is in the ascendant with conjunction or aspect of a Maraka lord.

4. Should the ascendant or the Moon be in the 8th, the person with Ketu concerned will be penniless.

5. If the ascendant lord along with a malefic is in the 8th or 12th while the 2nd lord is in an enemy's sign or in debilitation, even a native of royal scion will become penniless.





Brihat Parasara Ilora Sastra

6. If the ascendant lord is conjunct the 6th, 8th and 12th lords or Saturn he will be penniless.

7. Should the 5th and 9th lords be respectively found in the 6th and 12th houses and be aspected by malefics, the native will be penniless.

8. If the lords of the 10th and 9th, excepting the malefics, be in association with or aspect one of the Maraka planets, the native will become penniless.

9. Note that the planets ruling the signs occupied by the lords of the 6th, 8th and 12th, if said dispositors are in such evil houses and be associated or aspected by malefics, the native will be miserable and indigent.

10. The lord of the Navamsa occupied by the Moon joining a Maraka planet or occupying a Maraka house will make one penniless.

11. Should the lord of natal ascendant and that of Navamsa ascendant be conjunct or be aspected by Maraka planets, one will be penniless.






# Chapter 42

If malefics are occupied by benefics inauspicious houses, the native will be distressed while even auspicious houses will be occupied by the matter of food.

12. If malefics are associated with one of the lords of the 6th, 8th and 12th, being bereft of a trinal lord's aspect, will cause harm to the native's financial periods.

13. A planet with one of the lords of the 6th, 8th and 12th, being bereft of a trinal lord's aspect, will cause harm to the native's financial periods.

14. If the 8th/12th from Atmakaraka lord and the ascendant be aspected by Atmakaraka Navamsa, the native will be bereft of wealth.

15. The native will be a spendthrift if the 12th from Atmakaraka is aspected by the dispositor of Atmakaraka or if the 12th from the ascendant is aspected by the natal lord.

16-18. Should Mars and Saturn be together in the 2nd house, the native's wealth will be destroyed.

Itell you some yogas for poverty along with their nullifications.





Brihat Parasara Hora

# Chapter 43

# Longevity

Should planets aspect the Sun in the 2nd, there will be great wealth. There is no doubt in it. The aspect of Saturn will cause penury while the Sun aspected by Saturn will give riches (i.e. poverty) and fame. The same effects will be declared if Saturn is in the 2nd in aspect to the Sun.

O Sage, you have dealt with combinations for wealth and poverty. Kindly detail the methods of ascertaining the life span of human beings.

Following the Pindayu system of longevity, slokas dealing with these calculations is fully explained with the entire system being practical so that the reader follows the calculations involved thoroughly.

# IO-II. DEDUCTIONS FOR PLANETS IN VISIBLE HALF

Full, half, one third, one fourth, one fifth and one sixth are the deductions of contributions made by malefics in the visible half of the zodiac. Benefics in such cases only lose half of what malefics lose. Should there be more than one planet in a house, the deduction due to the strongest planet will only prevail and not due to other planets in that house.

Waning Moon is a benefic for this purpose.

# 12-13. MALEFICS IN ASCENDANT

In case the ascendant is occupied by malefics, adopt the following procedure: Convert the years etc. into minutes of arc and multiply by the contribution made by the occupant. The years so arrived will be deducted from the respective net contribution aspect donated by the planet.

If there is malefics containing the ascendant, then the loss will only be half through these calculations.

# l+15. ASCENDANT'S CONTRIBUTION

The number of years contributed by the ascendant will correspond to the number of signs it gained (from Aries) while the degrees in the particular sign will also correspondingly donate (i.e. 30 degrees: 1 year). If the Navamsa lord is stronger than the ascendant lord, then the contribution will be computed only based on the Navamsas gained.

O Brahmin, now I tell you about Nisargayu. The allotted years are 16-17, 18, 20 and 50 for the Moon, Mars, Venus, Mercury, Jupiter, the Sun and Saturn from the period of birth.

This conveys to us that the years are dedicated for the planets when they are in deep exaltation. These are halved at deep debilitation. Then the rectifications are the same as to Pindayu. The method of its contribution is also the same as seen in Pindayu scheme.

Now about Amsayu contributions by the ascendant planets. The years correspond to the number of Navamsas counted from Aries. Multiply the longitude in question by 108. If the product exceeds 12, expunge multiples of 12 and consider the final product in Rasi, degrees etc.

# 23. LONGEVITY FOR OTHER LIVING BEINGS

For living beings as such computations be made. The said figure be multiplied by the figure corresponding to its full span of life and divided by the figure corresponding to full span of human beings.

# 24.29. FULL LIFE SPAN OF VARIOUS LIVING BEINGS

I now tell you the full life span figures for various living beings. Gods and sages enjoy endless life proportions as against ordinary mortals. The full life span of eagles, owls, parrots, crows and snakes is one thousand years. Falcon, rook, bear, and frog life in these cases is 300 years. Dromoo, lifespan is 150 years while it is 120 years for human beings.






# Chapter 43

OTIIER CLUES TO LONGEVITY

# 33-40.

you give details in the methods of the Brahmins, as on the positions of other lords, under this matter of longevity. This is based on the 8th lord, Saturn, the Moon, natal lord, ascendant (Hora Lagna). These are grouped into six thus: the lords of the ascendant and the 8th hand, Saturn and Moon on the one hand, and the other on yet the other hand, the natal ascendant and Hora ascendant long life group, movable if the two are in sign/signs denoted. One in fixed sign and the other in a long sign will bestow life. One in movable sign will also give medium life. If both are in fixed sign then life is denoted. Short life is obtained if one is in a common sign or if both are in fixed signs. The type of life denoted is again determined by three or two signs.





# Chapter 43

groups be only considered. If the three groups denote scales, then the one indicated by the pair of natal and Hora ascendant will only be considered. In case of three indications if the Moon is in the ascendant then the one indicated by Saturn-Moon pair will only come to pass.

Notes: Three groups are considered for longevity calculations. Following are the groups, consisting of three each:

| Group     | Constituents                                             |
| --------- | -------------------------------------------------------- |
| 1st group | natal ascendant, lord and 8th lord from the group-Saturn |
| 2nd group | natal and the Moon.                                      |
| 3rd group | Hora ascendant Langa. (For see 63).                      |

Thus two planets in one group, two planets in another group and two ascendants in yet another group are selected. Now their positions will denote the basic position of each group thus:

1. Long life: If both the constituents pass (jointly or separately), to another long life will come in a dual sign and in a fixed sign will also give the same scale of longevity.
2. Medium life: One in movable sign and another sign will give medium life. Both in dual signs will also give the same effects.
3. Short life: One in movable sign and another sign will indicate short life. Both of them in dual signs produce again short life.

Thus, all the six possible positions of a pair group are covered. Which is to be considered for arriving at life span circumstances and in what scale (viz. medium and short) indicated by two or three groups, suppose two groups indicate medium life while another short take medium span as the basic if three indicate identical scales, one. Alternatively that is possible to consider as the case may be. It is also that one group denotes long life, another medium life and yet another short that case point follow given below.

# 6.

If she is in the natal given pair of Hora-natal ascendants, then the indication by the Moon or in the 7th, will be ignored if the indication of Saturn-Moon be alone considered. Moon is neither in the ascendant nor the 7th, then follow the indication of Hora-natal given as in rule 2 above.

# FURTHER CLARIFICATIONS.

If long life is denoted by all the said three groups, the span is 120 years, if by two groups it is 108 years and if only by one group it is 96 years.

If medium life is arrived at by three groups, it is 80 years, by two groups 72 years and by one group 64 years. If short life is denoted by the said three groups, it is only 32 years, if by two groups 36 years and by one group 40 years. These are rectified as follows:

# Chapter 44

# Maraka (Killer) Planets

O sage, you have mentioned a lot about longevity. Be kind enough to throw light on Marakas or killers.

O Brahmin, the 3rd and 8th houses are the two houses related to death. The 2nd house is also a house of longevity. The 8th from the 8th is the 12th house from the 3rd, and the 7th house is the 12th from the 8th - are two principal Maraka houses. The lords of these houses will also acquire such qualities giving life or taking away life.

Out of the two powerful Maraka houses, the lords of the 2nd and the 7th are known as Marakas. The major periods of these planets will bring death depending on whether he has long life, medium life or short life.





# Chapter 44

Notes: The 2nd and 7th are denoted as Maraka houses. The 2nd is a more important house to kill than the 7th. Thus, the 2nd is 12th from the 3rd, and from the 7th from the 8th.

If there is a malefic in the 2nd or in the 7th, he will be a prime killer while a benefic planet will not be so. The Dasa of such will inflict death.

Notes: The 12th house is also a terminal house of death, for it is related to malefics connected to the 2nd, 3rd, and 8th. The Dasa of a malefic, whether or not he is a lord of one of these houses, will also prove harmful for span of life. However, a different approach is recommended.

The rules given are just general hints to decide death. The life span should be ascertained through Ayurdaya calculations, and the exact periods of other dasa be decided later on. Simply saying that the 2nd lord's dasa will bring death and so on will suggest forth will be a misnomer.

The sage suggests that the occupants of the 3rd, 8th, and the 3rd, though known as houses of longevity, are simultaneously capable of causing death. For the information of the reader, the Maraka planets in the ascending points of lords of 12th, 3rd, 8th, 7th, and 2nd are: occupants of 6th and 11th are grade second killers. The last group consists of occupants/lords of 5th, 9th, 10th, 4th, and 1st. They are the least Marakas. However, these Marakas can also become depending on the given clues in slokas infra.



Brthd Parasara Hora Sastra

A difficult subject may take guidelines to be fully explained like longevity cannot in a chapter like this. The reader should form a basic opinion before present works on longevity.

8. The dasa (sub period) of a benefic planet, although related to the latter, is not related to a malefic planet. The former is ill-disposed to a maraka.

9. Should preference be given to kill in a malefic planet, he will be the first to die.

10-14. O Brahmin, I tell you further about Marakas' medium life spans, viz. short, medium, and long. Short life is before 31 years, medium life is from 31 to 64 years, and long life is beyond 64 years. It is narrated that the longevity of Brahmins is called supreme. O excellent native, longevity is 20 years old till the year 100. Such should be protected by sacred recitations, offerings of ghee, etc.

RAHU AND KETU AS MARAKAS: If Rahu or Ketu be in the ascendant, or be in the 7th from a Malaka lord or be in the 6th, 8th or 12th thereof, or be with such a planet, they acquire powers of killing in their major periods or sub periods. For one born in Capricorn or in Scorpio, Rahu will be a Maraka. Should Rahu be in the 6th, 8th or 12th, he will give difficulties in his dasa periods. He will not, however, do so if aspected by or conjunct with a benefic.

They will not be Marakas if they are in 3rd, 9th, 5th and 11th houses. If a node joins a Maraka planet, it will act as a Maraka. Rahu is termed as a primary maraka for Capricorn and Scorpio ascendants. If he is in one of the adverse houses for these ascendants, his dasa will bring death or intolerable difficulties.

# Avasthas Of Planets

O sage, you have earlier stated (states) that the Avasthas of planets be considered in the context of planetary effects. Bc





Chapter 45
# 1. O excellent Avasthas of Brahmins, various kinds of planetary states have been expounded.

Out of these, I tell you the summary of infant and other states (in the first instance).

# 2. INFANT STATE ETC

Infant, youthful, adolescent, old and dead are the states of planets placed in the ascending order at the rate of six degrees in odd signs. This arrangement is reversed in the case of even signs.

# Notes:

These 5 Avasthas are known as Baatadi Avasthas. For odd signs, the placement concerned will denote as under Avastha:

| Infant (Baalavastha)            | 0 to 6°   |
| ------------------------------- | --------- |
| Youthful (Kumaravastha)         | 6 to 12°  |
| Adolescent (Yuvavastha)         | 12 to 18° |
| Advanced state (Vridhdhavastha) | 18 to 24° |
| Dead (Mritavastha)              | 24 to 30° |

The above order is to be reversed for placement in an even sign.

# 3. RESULTS

One fourth, half, full, negligible and are the grades of results due to a planet in youthful, adolescent, infant, old and dead states.

# 4. AWAKENING, DREAMING AND SLEEPING STATES

If a planet is in its own sign or in exaltation it is said to be in a state of awakening (or alertness). In the sign of a friend or of a neutral it is in dreaming state while in enemy's sign or in debilitation it is in a state of sleeping.





Hora Sastra
450 Brihat Parasara

Dreaming.

According to a planet in Awakening, to a full, medium being due to it will be results or nil.

There are nine kinds OF STATES

# 7. OTHER KINDS

Deena, Santa, Pramudita, Swastha, viz. Deepta, KoPa, Khala, Vikala.

If a sign is in its exaltation in Deepta, a friend's sign is in thick Pramudita, in own sign Swastha, in neutral's sign Santa, in friendly sign Khala, and being in an enemy's sign Vikata, in a malefic's state by the Sun-Kopa.

Depending on such a state of the eclipsed planet, the house occupied will obtain corresponding effect.




# Chapter 45

YET OTHER AVASTHAS .. . Lajjita, Garvita, Kshudita, Trushita, Mudita and Kshobhitare the other kinds (six) states of planets. Due to the planet is associated with a node or with the Sun, Saturn or Mars, it is in Lajjitavastba. If a planet is in exaltation Moolatrikona, it is Garvitavastha. The avastha if the planet is in an enemy's sign, or conjunct or aspected by an enemy or even be in conjunction with Saturn. If a planet is in a watery sign and be in aspect to a malefic but not a benefic, the avastha is called Kshudita. If a planet is in a friendly sign, or conjunct by a benefic or is conjunct Jupiter, it is said to be in Trushita. If a planet is conjunct the Sun and is aspected by a malefic or is aspected by an enemy, it is said to be in Kshobhitavhshta. The houses occupied by a planet in kshuditavastha are destroyed.






452                              Brihot Parasara Hora Sastra

19.23 The learned should estimate the effects due to a house in the manner cited above (i.e. with the help of avasthas), after ascertaining the strength and weakness of the various planets. Weak planets cause reduction in effects while stronger ones give greater pointed effects.

If a planet in the 10th house is in Lajjitavastha, Kshudhitavastha or Kshobhitavastha, the person will always be subjected to miseries. If a planet in the 5th house is in Lajjitarasrha, there will be destruction of progeny, or there will be only one surviving child.

The wife of the native will die if there is a planet in Kshg6ti0avastha or in Trushitavastha.

# Chapter 45

# EFFECTS in Garvitavastha OF 1A.RVITAVASTHA ETC.

A planet will cause happiness through regalhood, skill in arts, financial gains at all times, improvement in business. A planet in Muditavastna will give happiness from gardens, clothes, ornaments, happiness from relatives, living in royal palaces, destruction of enemies and acquisition of wisdom and learning.

A planet will give aversion to God, loss of intelligence, loss of child, interest in evil speeches and things. A planet in Kshobhitavastha will give acute evil disposition, miseries, financial debacles, distress to meet obstruction to income due to royal wrath.

A planet in Trushitavastha will cause downfall due to grief and passion, account of relatives, physical decline, troubles, financial distress, loss of physical strength and miseries.

A planet associated with females will lead to loss of wealth due to one's own wicked deeds, physical miseries caused by evil people and decline of honour.






# Hora

# Brihat Parasar-a Sastta

30.37. CALCULATION OF SAYANA AND OTHER AVASTHAS

Now I tell you of the avasthas viz' Sayana, Sabha, Aagamana, Gamana, Prakasana, Netrapani, Upavesana, Nrityalipsa, Kautuka and Nidra, and the Aiama, Bhojane, the number of such chesthas occupied by the planet for which Avastha is to be calculated.

Note the number denoted by the planet (Sun 1, Moon 2 etc.). Multiply that by the number of ghatis of birth and the number gained from the ascendant of Aries. This figure will be divided by 12 and the remainder thus obtained will indicate the corresponding Avastha.

The sub state in the said Avastha can be found out by the Avastha concerned. Multiply the figure denoted by the same and increase it by the constant of 12. The remainder thus: Sun 5, Moon 2, Mars 2, Rahu 4, Ketu 3, Saturn 5, Jupiter 3, Venus 4, Mercury 3.

For whom the planet is being known, the product obtained at be divided by 3. In this process, if the remainder is 1, it is Drishti, and if 2, it is Vicheshta.

So far narrated are three different groups of Avasthas. The present Avasthas are called Sayanadi Avasthas. These may be adopted to know the importance of supreme Avasthas.

The following formula (Sayanadi) is used to calculate the planet's Avastha at birth:

(s * p) / Avastha

Where 's' denotes the serial number of the star from Aswini at birth; 'p' denotes the planet.





Chapter 45
status ptanet (i.e. of the counted from the Sun Sun Mercury 4 etc; 'n' denotes position (i.e. 'a' the Navamsa I to 9 Navamsas); denotes Janma (or Nakshatra ruling star, i.e. the one occupied by the Moon); 'g' denotes took place (i.e. 20gh 2 vigh is 2lgh) and denotes the ascendant's order counted from Aries (i.e. Cancer Leo 5, so on forth).

In place of some translators given above, interpret the word 'Amsa' as degree occupied by the planet which is not correct. [n this connection, the reader's attention is drawn to Balabhadra's Hora Ratna, ch 3 wherein the author gives himself an example for the Sun being 7th Navamsa in the of Leo and thus he considered only 7 as multiplier. He has not taken into account the Sun's degree. He quotes Adhbbuta Segara as for calculation of Sayanadi Avasthas. It will thus be clear that 'Amsa' is not degree in this context.

Also please note that (the Aagamanavastha 6th one) is known by some exponents as Gamanechchavastha.

Take now as an example with the following data. The Sun in Krittika 3rd Navamsa (i.e 12'Taurus), birth star Krittika, of Taurus in Scorpio. With these we produce following keeping forrmula information, S:3 L : 3 P:l g 3t Hence n:3 r: 8.

to find the Avastha, (3xlx3)*(3*31*8) -12 remainder. With the help of remainder 3, we count three from Sayana. This indicates Avastnas Netrapani Avastha for the Sun. Similarly for 9 planets, such Avasthas will be found out. In a given horoscope, the factors for all the 9 planets while factors .s', .p' and .n, will be identical variable.

After knowing the Avasthas of various planets, we have to find out the sub state of each Avastha. The formula for knowing sub-state is made in two stages, as under.





Brihat Parasara Hora Sashtra

Stage 1, Stage 2: (R*pa) + 3: substate

Where 'A' is Avastha, is first syllable's value reference with to the narrative's personal name, R is remainder stage in l, and 'pa' is planetary additament denoted in the slokas, above such as Sun 5, Venus 3 etc. The remainder at stage will denote sub state such as I is Drishti, 2 cheshta 2 O vicheshta.

We need information about Anka value or value syllable for first of the person. These are:

38-39. EFFECTS OF CHESHTA ETC. Tri, is Drishti in an Avastha: If the sub state the results being stated will be for the Avastha medium, full in cheshta and negligible. The good and bad effects of planets will be deciphered based on the.






# Chapter 45

and planets. In exaltation, the strength and weakness of planets reveal pronounced effects due to Avasthas.

If a planet is in good Avastha (sub state), the effects will be full. If the sub state is Vicheshta, the good effects are neutralised. If the sub state is Drishti, good effects will be feebly felt.

A planet in exaltation will give a particular effect due to a fuller measure. If a planet is in bad Avastha as sub state, the evil effects will be less. With Drishti, evil effects will be felt. If Vicheshta is bad, the effects are neutralized.

In debilitation, the evil effects of a planet will be pronounced. Each Avastha gives different effects—good or bad—according to the Avastha. No constant evaluation is made with the name of an Avastha. This is what is conveyed in the following slokas.

40-51. EFFECTS OF THE SUN'S BIRTH.

If the Sun is in Sayenavastha, the native will incur digestive deficiency, many diseases, stoutness, ulcer of legs, bilious vitiation, and heart strokes. If the Sun is in Upavesanavastha, the native will suffer poverty, will indulge in litigations, will be hard-hearted, wicked, and in his undertakings. If the Sun is in Netrapani avastha, the native will always be happy, wise, helpful to others, endowed with prowess and wealth, very happy, and will gain royal favours. If the Sun is in Prakasanavastha, the native will have a liberal disposition, plenty of wealth, will be a speaker in the assembly, will perform many meritorious acts, be strong and be endowed with charming beauty. If the Sun is in Gamanavastha, the native will be disposed to live in foreign places, be miserable, indolent, bereft of intelligence and wealth, and be distressed due to fear and be short-tempered. If the Sun is in Agamanavastha, the native will be interested in others' wives, devoid of his own men, be interested in doing evil deeds, be dirty, ill disposed and be a bearer. If the Sun is in Sebhavastba, the native will be disposed to help others, always endowed with wealth, gems, lands, new houses and robes, and be very virtuous.

In Aagamavastha, will lose money on account of others' females, will have strength, will be untruthful, will incur headaches. If the sun is in J..fining off and will take bad food and eat remnants by the learned, the native will be honoured.

Nrityalipsavastha, will have knowledge of poetry and etc., will be a scholar, trimsetra is in Kautukavastha. If the Sun is adored by kings on the earth, the native will always be happy, endowed with spiritual knowledge, will perform sacrificial rites, will move amidst kings.

52.63. EFFECTS OF THE MOON'S AVASTHAS AT BIRTTI.

If the Moon is in Sayanavastha, the native will be honourable, sluggish, given to sexual lust, and will face destruction. If the Moon is in Upavesanlvastha, the native will be troubled by diseases, be dull-witted, not endowed with mentionable wealth (i.e. will have only negligible wealth), hard-hearted, will do unworthy acts and will steal wealth from others. If the Moon is in Netrepani avastha, the native will be troubled by great diseases (long lasting in nature), garrulous, wicked and will indulge in bad deeds.

Should the Moon be in Prakasavastha, the native will be famous in the world, will have his virtues exposed through patronage, be surrounded by horses, elephants, females and ornaments. If the Moon is in Gamanavastha, the native will be sinful, cruel and always troubled by afflictions; if with increasing rays, the native will be distressed to fear. If the Moon is in Agamanavastha, the native will be honourable, will suffer diseases of feet, will secretly indulge in sinful acts, be poor and devoid of intelligence.

If the Moon is in sabhavastha, the native will be eminent among men, honoured by kings, and kings of kings, be very beautiful, will subdue the passion of women, be skilful in sexual acts and be virtuous. If the Moon is in Agamavastha, the native will be garrulous, virtuous and if the said Moon is of dark fortnight, the native will have two wives, be violent. If the Moon is in Bbojanavastha, the native will be endowed with honour, conveyances, attendants, social status.

However, the position of Mars in the 2nd house or the 5th house in Netrapani Avastha will cause fear from lions and from giving the native's earnings lands. Further, the wife will predecease him. Should Mars be in Gamanavastha, the native will incur diseases of the joints, pains in the dental area, and will have afflictions like burning eyes, fear from dogs, and adore the guise of a female. These are the effects of Mars in the ascendant.

In other houses, Mars in Gamanavastha will bring luxuries of royal life. Shifting over to sloka 69 of our text, in the context being the sage uses the meaning of Mars in Agamanavastha, as 'elephant killer' by some commentators. It is actually interpreted that the native will walk with the majestic gait of an elephant, imparting surprise to onlookers. Mars will cause diseases of rectum. In Agamanavastha or in Sayanavastha in the 5th house, if Mars be in Bhojanavastha, there will be untimely death for the native. In other houses, Mars will confer wealth. # EFFECTS OF MERCURY

BIRTH: Should Mercury in sryanavastha be in the ascendant, the native will be lame and will have reddish eyes (like black bee); if Mercury be in the said Avastha in other houses, the native will be addicted to licentious pleasures and be wicked.

If Mercury be in uplvesanavrstba in the ascendant, (the native will possess seven virtues; if aspected by or conjoined with malefics, penury will result and if by benefics happiness will follow.) If Mercury be in Netrrprni Avrstba, the native will be devoid of learning, wisdom, well-wishers and satisfaction but be honourable; if Mercury be in the 5th house Avastha, the subject will be bereft of happiness and be endowed (more) with female children and gain finance abundant through royal patronage.

If Mercury be in Prakasavastha, the native will be notorious, will cross the boundaries of ocean in respect of many branches of learning, be endowed with great faculty of discrimination and will destroy evil people. If Mercury be in Gamanavastha, the native will visit the court of kings on many occasions and Goddess Lakshmi (wealth) will dwell in his abode.

If Mercury be in Agrmmavasthl, the same effects due to his being in Gamanavestha will fructify. If Mercury be in sabhavastha and be in exaltation, the native will be affluent at all times, be equal to (the king in Hindu mythology) Kubera, lord of wealth or a minister, be devoted to Lord Vishnu and Lord Shiva, be virtuous and will attain emancipation.

Should Mercury be in Agamavasthr, the native will serve base men and gain wealth thereby and will have sons and one fame-bringing daughter. If Mercury be in Bhojanavastha, the native will face financial losses, litigations, physically will lose on account of fear from kingly.





Hora Sastra

and will be become thin due to royal wrath, fickle-minded will be in physical and conjugal felicity. If Mercury bereft with honour, will endow the native with prowess (i.e. gems, sons, friends, conveyance, corals etc.), if with the said due recognition in assembly.

The native will be addicted to pleasures. If Mercury be in a malefic's sign, the native will long for licentious prostitut$ and will be in Krututrvlstbr, and be in the ascendant, one in the 7th/8th with the said Avastha.

# 87. EFFECTS OF JUPITER'S AT/ASTHAS AT BIRTH

If Jupiter is in Seyanavastha, the native will be very tawny in complexion, will have prominent cheeks, and will have fear from enemies. If Jupiter is in Upavesanavastha, the native will be garrulous, troubled by king and enemies, and will have ulcers on face and hands.

If Jupiter be in Netrapani avastha, the native will be afflicted by diseases, devoid of music and dances, tawny in complexion, and attached to other castes. If Jupiter be in prakusevatn, the native will enjoy virtues, be happy, splendorous, and will be holy to Lord Krishna.

If Jupiter is in the exalted state, the native will attain greatness among Kubera—the lord of wealth. If Jupiter is in Grmanavastha, the native will be adventurous, scholarly, and happy on account of friends, endowed with various kinds of wealth and Vedic learning.

If Jupiter be in Agamanavastha, excellent women and the goddess of wealth will never leave the native's abode. If Jupiter be in Sabhavestha, the native will attain comparability with Jupiter (the God of speech) and be endowed with superior wealth, rich with elephants, horses, and chariots, and will be learned.

If Jupiter be in Agamavastha, the native will be endowed with various conveyances, honours, children, wife, friends, and learning, noble, fond of literature, and will be equal to a king, easily taking the virtuous path.

If Jupiter be in Bhogavastha, the native will always receive food, excellent horses, elephants, and chariots of Lucre, while the goddess will never leave his house. If Jupiter be in Nrisalipsavastha, the native will receive royal honours, be wealthy, endowed with knowledge of moral learning (a branch of learning dealing with magical or mystical formularies), and be supreme among the learned and a great grammarian.

# 99.IIO. EFFECTS OF AVASTHAS OF VENUS AT BIRTH

If Venus be in Sayanavastha, the native will incur dental diseases, be short-tempered, will be bereft of wealth, will seek union with courtezans and be licentious. If Venus be in Upavesanavastha, the native will be endowed with a multitude of nine gems (affi1w) and golden ornaments, be happy, will destroy enemies, be honoured by the king and will have highly increased honours. If Venus be in Nedpnt





# Chapter 45

Avastha the ascendant, 10th, the 7th or there will be loss of wealth on account of expenses due to severe sight afflictions (i.e. heavy medical diseases) and if the said Avastha occurs when Venus is in other houses, there will be large houses owned by the native. Should Venus be in exaltation sign, friendly sign, the native will sport like a lofty elephant, be equal to a king and be skilful in poetry and music.

If Venus be in Gamanavaitba, the native will not have a long living mother, will lament over separation from his own people and will have fear from enemies. If Venus be in Agamanavastlra, the native will command abundant wealth, be ever enthusiastic to visit superior shrines, will contract diseases of the hand and foot.

If Venus and be in Sabhovastha the native will earn eminence in the king's court, be very virtuous, destroy enemies, and will be equal to Kubera in wealth, charitable, among men. If Venus is in Agamavastha, there will be no advent of wealth but troubles from enemies, separation from pleasures and lack of children and diseases from the wife.

Should Venus be in Bhojanavastha, the native will be distressed due to hunger, and will have many kinds of fear from enemies. If the said planet is in Virgo, the native will be rich and honoured by scholars. If Venus be in Nrilyalipsavastha, the native will be very intelligent, skilful in literature, will play musical instruments like lute, and be affluent.

If Venus be in 'utukavasthr, the native will attain greatness equal to Lord Indra, will have Lakshmi in his abode. If Venus is in Nidravastha, the native will be learned and will blame others, be garrulous and interested in serving others, wandering over the earth.

In Sayana Avastha, if Venus is in the 7th or in the 11th houses, the native will be endowed with all kinds of happiness, will face riches; and will have 5 daughters. In short, Venus in the 7th will destroy the progeny of the native. If Venus is in Upavesanavastba, the native will have a defect or injury on the right side of the body. He will suffer from pains of joints.




# Brihat Parasara Hora Sastra

Should upavesanavastha occur to Venus or in own sign, the native will be endowed in exaltation with all kinds of happiness. There will be sure loss of eyesight if Venus is in Netrapani Avastha. The 10th house placement of Venus in Netrapani Avastha is not praiseworthy for riches while houses other than the ascendant, 2nd and 10th will bring wealth apart from giving two wives.

Prakasana Avastha: Venus placed in the 2nd, 4th, 9th or the ascendant will give wealth and disposition. And if he be in the 10th exaltation or in friendly sign, the native will occupy a high position with the king. In other houses, Prakasa Avastha of Venus will give many diseases and miseries. If Venus is in Sabhavastlrithe, the native will receive royal favours akin to Kubera in wealth. Should Venus be in Sabhavastba an enemy's sign or in aspect to an enemy, it will destroy everything.

The degree of learning will confer a high degree while Nidravastha will cause litigations, poverty, diseases, disputes. Kautukavastha of Venus will give abundant wife and numerous children.

# Chapter 475

# III.I22. EFFECTS OF SATURN'S AVASTHAS AT BIRTH.

If Saturn is in Sayanavastha, the native will be troubled by thirst, and will incur hunger diseases in boyhood and later become wealthy. If Saturn be in Upavesanavastha, the native will be troubled greatly by enemies, will contract ulcers all over the body, be punished by the king, and will be self-respected.

If Saturn be in Netrapani Avastha, the native will be endowed with charming female wealth, will have royal favour and friends, will have knowledge of many arts and be eloquent, a speaker.

If Saturn be in Prakasavastha, the native will be very virtuous, very wealthy, intelligent, sportive, splendorous, merciful and devoted to Lord Siva.

If Saturn be in Gamanavastha, the native will be very rich, endowed with sons; will grab the enemy's lands and be a scholar at royal court.

If Saturn be in Agdmrnavastha, the native will be akin to a donkey (i.e. foolish), bereft of happiness, will always pitiably roam without patronage from wife and children.

If Saturn be in Sabhavrstha, the native will have surprising possessions of abundant precious gold, stones with great judicial (or political) knowledge and be brilliant.

If Saturn be in Agomavastha, the native will incur diseases, and will not be skilful in earning royal patronage.

If Saturn be in Bhojanavastha, the native will be weak-sighted, will enjoy tastes of food, and be fickle-minded due to delusion.

If Saturn be in Nrityalipavastha, the native will...






# Brihat Parasara Hora Sostra

If Saturn be in Kautohavastha and be righteous, honoured by the king, will be extremely opulent, heroic in warfield. The native will be endowed with lands and wealth, and be happy, with pleasures through charming females and learned poetry. If Saturn be in Nidravastha, the native will be endowed with charming virtues, valorous, and will destroy rich pleasures and be skilful in seeking enemies even harlots.

If Saturn in Sayanavastha is in the 5th or 8th, the native will be endowed with progeny and happy in all manners; in the ascendant, if poor and peaceless. This Avastha places, very alien will also cause diseases irrespective of the planet's placement. Saturn in Upavesanavastha or in the ascendant in the 10th will cause destruction of wealth. Saturn placed in the 5th/7th will cause unchecked difficulties of wealth, and will be destruction there.

When this Avastha occurs to Saturn, his entire race will be "destroyed". Should an aspect occur to Saturn from an enemy's sign, there will be absolute possession, and the native's digestive defects will cause difficulties. If Saturn is in exaltation in his own sign, the native will enjoy all kinds of happiness and will be ever devoid of diseases. Saturn in the 5th/7th/9th will destroy this Avastha to the native alone.

Should Saturn occur in another house than the 5th/7th/9th, the native will be meritorious, rich, skilful, favoured by the king, and very learned. If Saturn is in Nidravastha, the native will have two wives and many issues. In the 10th house, there will be places and obstruction living in alien diseases in angle to undertakings at every step. If he is in an evil or in a trine, these effects will not come to pass.






# Chapter

# RAHU'S AVASTHAS OF EFFECTS

If Rahu be in sayansvastha, the miseries will experience.





Brihat pardsara Horo Sasta

but if Rahu in the srid Avastha be in Taurus, Virgo or Aries the native will be endowed with earth grains. If Rahu be in upavesanavastha and distressed the native will be due to ulcers, be endowed with royal association, honourable, highly and ever devoid of financial happiness.

If Rahu be in Netrapani Avastha, the native will be troubled by diseases, will have fear from wicked people, snakes and thieves and will incur financial decline. If Rahu be in prakasavastha, the native will acquire a high position, will perform auspicious acts, will obtain elevation of financial state, be highly virtuous.

be a chief in the king's court, be charming like frcsitry clouds (that will cause soon rain) and be very prosperous in foreign places. If Rahu is in Gamanavlstha the native will be endowed with numerous children, be scholarly, wealthy, and honoured by the king.

If Rahu is in ignr;;a"th", the native will be very irritable, bereft of intelligence and crooked, wealth, misery and ribidinous. If Rahu is in sabbavasthr the native will be scholarly, miserly, and endowed with wealth and happiness.

If Rahu be in gamavastha, the native will be always mentally distressed, will have fear and litigations from enemies, be bereft of his own men, will face financial destruction, and be crafty and emaciated.

If Rahu is in BhoJanrvostha, the native will be distressed without food, dull-witted, not bold in his acts and be bereft of progenic happiness. If Rahu be in Nrityalipsavastha, will contract great and unsubduing disease, will have eyes and fear from enemies and will decline righteously.

If Rahu be in Kautukavastha, the native will be devoid of a position (or a place), be interested in others' wealth. If Rahu be in Nidravastha, he will be a repository of virtues, be endowed with children, proud, bold, and very affluent.

Notes: If Rahu in Sayaoavastha is in Taurus, Leo, Virgo or there will be all round happiness whereas he is adverse with this Avastha. Rahu's upavesanavurttu will destroy one's wealth and will cause difficulties. His Netrapani Avastha in the ascendant or in the 7th will bring many evils and miseries while in other houses it will bring danger from animals. Rahu prakasanavastha in Leo.

# A Glimpse - Verma

# KERALA ASTROLOGY

The present work A Glimpse of Kerala Astrology is a condensation of three recognized Kerala classics: Kerala Jyo,tisna, Kerala Sutra, and Gopata Ratnakara, which are unique in their own way and speak by these enlightened readers - our astrology. We suppose illuminating parts of...
